
Chapter - 1
oṃ .. 
namaḥ sakalakalyāṇadāyine cakrapāṇaye .
viṣayārṇavamagnānāṃ samuddharaṇahetave .. 1 ..
 
totādriśikharakṣetre devagandharvasevite .
puṇyatīrthasamāyukte sarvartukusumānvite .. 2 ..
 
praśastāśramasaṃyukte puṇyakṣetropaśobhite .
vedavedāntaniṣṭhaistu taponiṣṭhairmaharṣibhiḥ .. 3 ..
 
sāṃkhyasiddhāntasaṃyuktaiḥ yogasiddhāntavedibhiḥ .
itihāsapurāṇajñairdharmaśāstrārthakovidaiḥ .. 4 ..
 
vedāṅgajñānakuśalairyukte devarṣibhistathā .
rājarṣibhiḥ samāyukte mantrasiddhairmahātmabhiḥ .. 5 ..
 
sanako nāma yogarṣirbrahmaputro mahātapāḥ .
bhagavajjñānasiddhyarthaṃ tapastepe suduścaram .. 6 ..
 
śatavarṣaṃ dhyāyamāne paramātmānamātmani .
na lebhe'bhi mataṃ so'pi taptvā ghorataraṃ tapaḥ .. 7 ..
 
śokena mahatā'viṣṭo babhūva sa munistadā ..
tataḥ śokārṇave magnaṃ jitakrodhaṃ jitendriyam .. 8 ..
 
dāntaṃ yogāṅganirataṃ taṃ bhaktaṃ bhaktavatsalaḥ .
vākyametajjagaddhātā jagāda jagato hitam .. 9 ..
 
vāsudevaḥ paraṃjyotiradṛśyaḥ puruṣottamaḥ .
śrībhagavānuvāca .
tvayā yogīśvareṇeha sutaptaṃ tapa uttamam .. 10 ..
 
prāpsyase na cirādbrahman mahatastapasaḥ phalam .
samāśvasihi bhadraṃ te mā viṣīda mahāmate .. 11 ..
 
kṛtakṛtyo jagatyasmin śāṇḍilyaḥ śrūyate mahān .
tamāśrayasva bhadraṃ te bhagavaddharmasiddhaye .. 12 ..
 
etasmin parvataśreṣṭhe purā'nena mahātmanā .
sākṣādbhagavato vyaktādacyutādacyutābhidhāt .. 13 ..
 
adhītāstrisuparṇādyāḥ sākṣātsadbrahmavācakāḥ .
śākhāśca niṣadaḥ sarvāḥ saṃhitā brāhmaṇābhidhāḥ .. 14 ..
 
niruktāni tato jñātāḥ padārthāḥ sapta ca kramāt .
jñānaṃ ca dvividhaṃ jñātaṃ śāstrāṇi vividhāni ca .. 15 ..
 
trayodaśavidhaṃ karma dvādaśādyātmasaṃyutam .
śrutvaivaṃ prathamaṃ śāstraṃ rahasyāmnāyasaṃjñitam .. 16 ..
 
divyamantrakramopetaṃ mokṣaikaphalalakṣaṇam .
bhūyaḥ saṃcoditāttasmāttena lokahitaiṣiṇā .. 17 ..
 
śrutaṃ vistarataḥ śāstraṃ bhogamokṣapradaṃ hi yat .
anuṣṭupchandoba ddhena proktaṃ bhagavatā svayam .. 18 ..
 
sātvataṃ pauṣkaraṃ caiva jayākhyetyevamādikam .
tatsarvaṃ viditaṃ samyak śāṇḍilyasya mahātmanaḥ .. 19 ..
 
evaṃ sakalaśāstrajñaḥ śāṇḍilyaḥ paramo guruḥ .
āste śiṣyaiḥ parivṛtaḥ svāśrame śramanāśane .. 20 ..
 
pāñcakālyaṃ paraṃ yajñaṃ kurvāṇaḥ sarvadā vaśī .
sa te vakṣyati dharmajño dharmaṃ bhāgavataṃ mune .. 21 ..
 
tamāśrayasva bhadraṃ te bhagavajjñānasiddhaye .
ityuktvā'stamitā vāṇī vāsudevasamīritā .. 22 ..
 
ityadbhutatamaṃ vākyaṃ śrutvā hṛṣṭatanūruhaḥ .
tadā kṛtārthamātmānaṃ manyamāno mahāmuniḥ .. 23 ..
 
śāṇḍilyadarśanākāṅkṣī saṃcacārācalādhipam .
apaśyadāśramaśreṣṭhaṃ śāṇḍilyasya mahātmanaḥ .. 24 ..
 
nānāpuṣpasamākīrṇaṃ nānāphalasamanvitam .
nānāpakṣigaṇairjuṣṭaṃ nānāmṛganiṣevitam .. 25 ..
 
kamalotpalasaṃkī rṇaiḥ śobhitaṃ kamalākaraiḥ .
bhagavaddharmajijñāsāparaiḥ śāntairamatsaraiḥ .. 26 ..
 
munimukhyaiḥ samākīrṇaṃ sarvatra ca mumukṣubhiḥ .
sapraviśya tamadrākṣīnmunimukhyairupāsitam .. 27 ..
 
śiṣyaiḥ parivṛtaṃ śāntairātmaniṣṭhaṃ dayāparam .
divyajñānopapannaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā divyakriyāparam .. 28 ..
 
udvahantaṃ parāṃ bhaktiṃ vāsudeve parātpare .
abhyavandiṣṭa sanako vinayāttasya pādayoḥ .. 29 ..
 
tiṣṭhantaṃ bhagavaddharme dṛṣṭvā divyena cakṣuṣā .
śāṇḍilyo muniśārdūlaḥ sanakaṃ brahmasaṃbhavam .. 30 ..
 
abravīnmadhuraṃ vākyaṃ kṛtārtho'si mahāmune .
bhagavān suprasannaste sutaptaṃ tapa uttamam .. 31 ..
 
ādiṣṭo'haṃ bhagavatā bhavadarthe taponidhe .
ityuktvā'dhyāpayāmāsa vedamekāyanābhidham .. 32 ..
 
mūlabhūtastu mahato vedavṛkṣasya yo mahān .
sadbrahmavāsudevākhya paratatvaikasaṃśrayam .. 33 ..
 
divyairbalādikairmantraiḥ sākṣāttatpratipādakaiḥ .
alaṅkṛtamasandigdhamavidyātimirāpaham .. 34 ..
 
adhyāpya saṃjagādāsya svarūpaṃ ca samāgati m .
śāṇḍilyaḥ .
eṣa kārtayugo dharmo nirāśīḥkarmasaṃjñitaḥ .. 35 ..
 
yogākhyo yogadharmākhyaḥ śāstrākhyaśca samāgamaḥ .
pravartyate bhagavatā prathame prathame yuge .. 36 ..
 
yugeṣu mandasañcāra itareṣvitareṣvapi .
anantaceṣṭādadhyakṣādaniruddhāt sanātanāt .. 37 ..
 
brahmaṇo mānasaṃ janma prathamaṃ cākṣuṣaṃ smṛtam .
dvitīyaṃ vācikaṃ cānyaccaturthaṃ śrotrasaṃbhavam .. 38 ..
 
nāsikyamaparaṃ cānyadaṇḍajaṃ padmajaṃ tathā .
eteṣvapi ca sarveṣu sākṣādbhagavato vibhoḥ .. 39 ..
 
brahmaṇā munimukhyaiśca suparṇādyairmaharṣibhiḥ .
vālakhilyamukhaiścānyaiḥ kramādrājarṣibhistathā .. 40 ..
 
eṣa prakṛtidharmākhyaḥ prādhītaḥ prathamo dvija .
saptame padmaje sarge prāpto bhagavatastathā .. 41 ..
 
vivasvatā tataḥ prāpto manunekṣvākuṇā tataḥ .
ikṣvākuṇā ca kathito vyāpya lokānavasthitaḥ .. 42 ..
 
eṣa eva mahān dharma ādyo vipra sanātanaḥ ..
durvijñeyo duṣkaraśca sātvatairdhāryate sadā .. 43 ..
 
cāturātmyaparairnityaṃ pañcakālaparāyaṇaiḥ .
balādimantraniratairdevatāntaravarjitaiḥ .. 44 ..
 
eṣa dharmo yathā prāpto mayā tadga dataḥ śrṛṇu .
sāṅgopaniṣadā vedāḥ samadhītā mayā purā .. 45 ..
 
ṛgyajussāmasaṃjñāstu saṃkīrṇā devatāntaraiḥ .
vyāmiśrayāgasaṃyuktāḥ pravṛttiphaladāyinaḥ .. 46 ..
 
tadarthāśca parijñātā yathānyāyaṃ yathāvidhi .
kvacit kvacit pradeśeṣu bhagavantaṃ jagatpatim .. 47 ..
 
tadīyaṃ karma ca jñānamapraṇāḍyā vadanti hi .
tathā tadatisaṃkṣiptamanabhivyaktalakṣaṇam .. 48 ..
 
agnīndrādipraṇāḍyaiva pradeśeṣu bahuṣvapi .
pravadanti jagannāthaṃ tathā ca sakalāḥ kriyāḥ .. 49 ..
 
nityādikā muniśreṣṭha pravṛttiphalasaṃyutāḥ .
devatāntaranāḍyaiva prabruvanti suvistarāt .. 50 ..
 
tathā kvacit kvacidvipra pravadanti ca kevalam .
indrādidevatāvarjaṃ tatkarmā'pi suvistaram .. 51 ..
 
mantrāḥ prācuryatastatra phalasaṅgasamanvitāḥ .
evaṃ vyāmiśrarūpatvātteṣu niṣṭhāṃ na labdhavān .. 52 ..
 
yastu sarvaparo dharmo yasmānnāsti mahattaraḥ .
vāsudevaikaniṣṭhastu devatāntaravarjitaḥ .. 53 ..
 
tajjijñāsā balavatī tadā tvāvirabhūnmama .
tato'tra parvataśreṣṭhe tapastaptaṃ mayottamam .. 54 ..
 
anekāni sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ tapaso'ntataḥ ..
dvāparasya yugasyānte ādau kaliyugasya ca .. 55 ..
 
sākṣātsaṅkarṣaṇādvyaktāt prāpta eva mahattaraḥ .
eṣa ekāyano vedaḥ prakhyātaḥ sātvato vidhiḥ .. 56 ..
 
durvijñeyo duṣkaraśca pratibuddhairniṣevyate .
mokṣāyanāya vaipanthā etadanyo na vidyate .. 57 ..
 
tasmādekāyanaṃ nāma pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ .
śvetadvīpe purā'dhīto nāradena surarṣiṇā .. 58 ..
 
sanaḥ sanatsujātaśca bhavānapi sananda naḥ .
sanatkumāraḥ kapilaḥ saptamaśca sanātanaḥ .. 59 ..
 
ete ekāntidharmasya ācāryāśca pravartakāḥ .
marīciratryaṅgirasau pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ .. 60 ..
 
vasiṣṭhaśca mahātejā ete citraśikhaṇḍinaḥ .
manuḥ svāyabhbhuvaścāpi samārādhya jagatpatim .. 61 ..
 
mahatā tapasā caiva devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum .
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu tadante samadhītya ca .. 62 ..
 
mūlaśrutiṃ yathāvaccā ṛṣayo'dhyāpitāstu taiḥ .
tataste ṛṣayastvaṣṭau lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā .. 63 ..
 
ślokānāṃ śatasāhasrairmūlavedaṃ nirīkṣya ca .
tathā divyāni tantrāṇi sātvatādīni cakrire .. 64 ..
 
anyacchāstraṃ tu tantrākhyamasmānmanvādayo'pi ca .
dharmaśāstrāṇyanekāni kariṣyanti yathātatham .. 65 ..
 
anyeṣāmapi śāstrāṇāṃ yoniretadbhaviṣyati .
asmin dharmaśca arthaścoktaḥ suvistaram .. 66 ..
 
mokṣaśca sūcitaḥ paścādatroktaśca yathātatham ..
aśvamedhādayo yajñā adhikṛtyācyutaṃ harim .. 67 ..
 
yathā kriyante ca tathā dviṣaṭkārṇapurassaraiḥ .
nivṛttiphaladairmantraistasyāsādhāraṇairhareḥ .. 68 ..
 
pūjitā viniyujyante tasmiṃstasmiṃśca karmaṇi .
ṛgādimantrāḥ sarve'pi tathā cāsmin prakīrtitāḥ .. 69 ..
 
vasūrājoparicaro mūlavedena saṃskṛtaḥ .
svargalokādhikārārthametaduktaprakārataḥ .. 70 ..
 
aśvamedhādikān yajñānanvaśiṣṭadyathāvidhi .
anyāṃśca bhagavadyāgān khinnavṛttyadhikārataḥ .. 71 ..
 
iti śruta mayā pūrvaṃ sa cārthaḥ pratibhāti me .
sumanturjaiminirbrahman bhṛguścaivaupagāyanaḥ .. 72 ..
 
mauñjyāyanaśca tatsarvaṃ samyagadhyāpitā mayā .
naranārāyaṇābhyāṃ tu jagato hitakāmyayā .. 73 ..
 
tathā'nuṣṭhīyate mūladharmo badarikāśrame .
eṣa prakṛtidharmākhyo vāsudevaikagocaraḥ .. 74 ..
 
pravartate kṛtayuge tatastretāyugādiṣu .
vikāravedāḥ sarvatra devatāntaragocarāḥ .. 75 ..
 
mahato vedavṛkṣasya mūlabhūto mahānayam .
skandhabhūtā ṛgādyāste śākhābhūtāstathā mune .. 76 ..
 
jaganmūlasya devasya vāsudevasya mukhyataḥ .
pratipādakatāsiddhā mūlavedākhyatā dvija .. 77 ..
 
ādyaṃ bhāgavataṃ dharmamādibhūte kṛte yuge .
mānavā yogyabhūtāstu anutiṣṭhanti nityaśaḥ .. 78 ..
 
tatastretāyuge sarve nānākāmasamanvitāḥ ..
vyāmiśrayājino bhūtvā tyajantyādyaṃ sanātanam .. 79 ..
 
antardadhāti sarvo'yaṃ vāsudevasamāhṛtaḥ .
tato yogyāya bhagavān prādurbhāvayati svayam .. 80 ..
 
yathā purā mayā prāpto devād jñānabalātmanaḥ .
tathā prakāśito vedaḥ sarahasyo mahāmune .. 81 ..
 
evaṃ nigadite samyak śāṇḍilyena mahātmanā .
tataḥ kṛtārthamātmānaṃ manyamānaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ .. 82 ..
 
sanakaḥ praśritaṃ vākyaṃ śāṇḍilyaṃ munimabravīt .
sanakaḥ .
bhagavan sarvadharmajña sarvaśāstrārthapāraga .. 83 ..
 
tvatprasādena saṃprāpto mayā dharmavaro mahān .
nivṛttilakṣaṇākhyo'yaṃ pratibuddhairniṣevitaḥ .. 84 ..
 
kathamapratibuddhaistairmagnairbhavamahāmbudhau .
prāpyate bhagavaddharma ekāntibhiranuṣṭhitaḥ .. 85 ..
 
śāṇḍilyaḥ .
śrūyatāmabhidhāsyāmi yadahaṃ coditastvayā .
etadarthaṃ mayā pṛṣṭaḥ purā saṅkarṣaṇaḥ prabhuḥ .. 86 ..
 
parityajya paraṃ dharmaṃ miśradharmamupeyuṣām .
bhūyastatpadakāṅkṣāṇāṃ śraddhābhaktī upeyuṣām .. 87 ..
 
anugrahārthaṃ varṇāṇāṃ yogyatāpāda nāya ca .
tathā janānāṃ sarveṣāmabhīṣṭaphalasiddhaye .. 88 ..
 
sātvatādīni śāstrāṇi bhogamokṣapradāni ca .
upadiśya tu divyāni śāstrāṇi tadanantaram .. 89 ..
 
pārameśvaraśāstrāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ munipuṅgava ..
sārabhūtaṃ viśeṣeṇa pauṣkarārthopapādakam .. 90 ..
 
mūlavedānusāreṇa chandasā'nuṣṭubhena ca .
lakṣagranthena sarvārthakriyājñānopalabdhaye .. 91 ..
 
sa me'bravīnma hāśāstraṃ pārameśvarasaṃjñayā .
tasmāttu sāramuddhṛtya sarvaśāstropayoginam .. 92 ..
 
ślokaiḥ ṣoḍaśasāhasraiḥ pārameśvarasaṃjñayā .
saṃpravakṣyāmi te śāstramidānīmavadhāraya .. 93 ..
 
nārado'pi purā caitadapi saṃkṣepato vibhoḥ .
kṣīrodaśāyino devāt sākṣāt saṃśrutavān dvija .. 94 ..
 
jñānakāṇḍakriyākāṇḍabhedenai va dvidhākṛtam .
yatra saṃkīrtyate samyagvāsudevasya vai vibhoḥ .. 95 ..
 
divyamātmasvarūpaṃ ca nityā jñānādayo guṇāḥ .
pradhānā ṣaṭ samastāśca vyastā yugmatrayeṇa hi .. 96 ..
 
kīrtyādayo guṇāścānye ākṛtiśca parātparā .
nityaikā vāsudevākhyā tataḥ sṛṣṭyādihetunā .. 97 ..
 
saṅkakarṣaṇādivyūhaśca jagajjanmādayo'pi ca .
upāsanārthaṃ bhaktānāmāstikānāṃ mahātmanām .. 98 ..
 
jagatāmupakārārthaṃ vāsudevasya vai vibhoḥ .
parātparasvarūpasya caturvyūhasturīyakaḥ .. 99 ..
 
vyūhaḥ suṣuptisaṃjñaśca svapnavyūhastathaiva ca .
jāgradvyūhastathā'nye ca vyūhā mūrtyantarā api .. 100 ..
 
mūrtayo vibhavākhyāśca prādurbhāvāntarāṇyapi .
lakṣmīpuṣṭyoḥ svarūpe ca nitye bhagavatā saha .. 101 ..
 
kāntyādayo'vatārāśca bhūṣaṇānāṃ tu vigrahāḥ .
nityāḥ kirīṭapūrvāṇāmanityāśca pṛthagvidhāḥ .. 102 ..
 
cakrādīnāṃ svarūpaṃ ca nityānityobhayātmakam .
garuḍapramukhānāṃ tu anyeṣāmātmanāmapi .. 103 ..
 
vibhoḥ sādhanabhūtānāṃ svaṃ svaṃ nityaṃ svarūpiṇām .
eteṣāṃ mūrtayo nityā anityāśca pṛthagvidhāḥ .. 104 ..
 
vibhorvai vāsudevasya sthānaṃ nityaṃ parātparam .
anyeṣāṃ vyūharūpāṇāṃ vibhavānāṃ tathaiva ca .. 105 ..
 
nānāvidhāni sthānāni virajāṃsi bahūni ca .
teṣāṃ vistāramānaṃ ca tathā svaṃ svaṃ vyavasthitam .. 106 ..
 
tatsālānāṃ pratolīnāṃ saṃkhyāmānaṃ ca lakṣaṇam .
jīvātmanāṃ svarūpa ca muktāmuktobhayātmakam .. 107 ..
 
teṣāṃ gativiśeṣāśca procyante yatra vistarāt .
bhagavanmantramūrtīnāṃ tathā'nyeṣāṃ krameṇa tu .. 108 ..
 
ma ntradhyānaṃ tathā mudrā yogarūpaṃ ca kīrtitam .
jñānakāṇḍābhidhānena tadetat parikīrtitam .. 109 ..
 
yatra nityāni karmāṇi snānādīnyakhilāni ca .
naimittikāni kāmyāni prāyaścittāni vistarāt .. 110 ..
 
tulābhārādikādīni karmāṇi vividhānyapi .
tathā ca karṣaṇādīni sthāpanāntānyaśeṣataḥ .. 111 ..
 
prāsādapratimābhadrapīṭhādīnāṃ ca lakṣaṇam .
evamādīni cānyāni deveśayajanārthataḥ .. 112 ..
 
kīrtyante vistarādyatra kriyākāṇḍaṃ tu viddhi tat .
evaṃ dvividharūpaṃ tu śāstraṃ vakṣye'vadhāraya .. 113 ..
 
Chapter - 2
śrīḥ .
kriyākāṇḍe dvitīyo'dhyāyaḥ .
śāṇḍilyaḥ .
athādhikārasiddhyarthaṃ snānaṃ vakṣyāmi pūrvataḥ .
yena bhakto'bhiṣiktastu syādarho yāgahomayoḥ .. 1 ..
 
snānaṃ tu dvividhaṃ kuryānmalasaṃkaraśuddhaye .
sāmānyavidhinā snātvā viśeṣavidhinā tataḥ .. 2 ..
 
sāmānyaṃ laukikaṃ snānaṃ viśiṣṭaṃ mantrasaṃskṛtam .
taccāpi śaucapūrvaṃ syāttadādau kathayāmi te .. 3 ..
 
brāhmaṃ muhūrtamāsādya udayātpūrvameva ca .
mantrajñaḥ prayataḥ kuryādvidhidṛṣṭena karmaṇā .. 4 ..
 
saṃprabuddhaḥ prabhāte tu utthāya śayane sthitaḥ .
nāmnāṃ saṃkīrtanaṃ kuryāt ṣoḍaśānāṃ prayatnataḥ .. 5 ..
 
oṃ namo vāsudevāya namaḥ saṃkarṣaṇāya te .
pradyumnāya namaste'stu aniruddhāya te namaḥ .. 6 ..
 
kramaśaḥ keśavādīnāṃ yāvaddāmodaraṃ dvija .
namo namaḥ keśavāya namo nārāyaṇāya ca .. 7 ..
 
mādhavāya namaścaiva govindāya namastataḥ .
viṣṇave'tha namaskuryānnamaste madhusūdana .. 8 ..
 
namastrivikramāyātha vāmanāya namastataḥ .
śrīdharāya namaścātha hṛṣīkeśāya oṃ namaḥ .. 9 ..
 
namaste padmanābhāya namo dāmodarāya ca .
divyānāmavatārāṇāṃ daśānāmatha kīrtanam .. 10 ..
 
ekaśrṛṅgādikānāṃ tu vihitaṃ kramaśaḥ prabhoḥ .
namaste mīnarūpāya kamaṭhāya namo namaḥ .. 11 ..
 
namo'stvādivarāhāya nārasiṃhāya te namaḥ .
namo vāmanarūpāya namo rāmatrayāya ca .. 12 ..
 
kuṭhārajyāhalāstrāya namaḥ kṛṣṇāya vedhase .
kalki viṣṇo namaste'stu pūrvaṃ sapraṇavaṃ dvija .. 13 ..
 
yathāsthitakrameṇaiva bhedāṃstvetān harervibhoḥ .
namaskuryāt prabhāte tu yāgānte tu dinakṣaye .. 14 ..
 
śabdenoccatareṇaiva saṃhṛ ṣṭijananena tu .
stotrāṇi cātha mantrāṇi udīryānyāni vai tataḥ .. 15 ..
 
ityevamādibhiḥ stotrairabhiṣṭūya śriyaḥ patim .
idaṃ vijñāpayāmāsa haraye varadāyine .. 16 ..
 
harirharirbruvaṃstalpādutthāya bhuvi vinyaset .
namaḥ kṣitidharāyoktvā vāmapādaṃ mahāmate .. 17 ..
 
bahirnirgamanārthaṃ tu sañcālyādau tameva hi .
jalasaṃpūrṇapātraṃ ca astramantroddhṛtaṃ mune .. 18 ..
 
devāgnigirigoṣṭheṣu nadyāṃ vā na śmaśānake .
valmīke mūṣikāsthāne vṛkṣamūle surālaye .. 19 ..
 
jalāntare ca mārge ca na gṛhṇīyāt kadācana .
deśe manorame grāhyā vihāya caturaṅgulam .. 20 ..
 
prāṇyaṅgatuṣabhasmāsthikāṣṭhaloṣṭavivarjitam .
paraśaucāvaśiṣṭaṃ yacchreyaḥkāmaiḥ sadā naraiḥ .. 21 ..
 
anaṅgārāmanūṣārāṃ tathā kṛṣṇāmavālukām .
śastrādinā'strajaptena nikhanecchubhadeśagām .. 22 ..
 
mṛdaṃ doṣavinirmuktāṃ tatastenaiva cāharet .
snānopakaraṇaṃ cānyacchamīśākhāḥ sapallavāḥ .. 23 ..
 
arkanyagrodhakhadirakarañjakakubhādikam .
śarajodumbarāśvatthaplakṣadarbhāṃśca vaiṇavān .. 24 ..
 
āmrāṅkuramapāmārgamarjunaṃ dhātakīṃ śamīm .
anyāni ca pavitrāṇi teṣu saṃpannamāharet .. 25 ..
 
yathāvasarametadvai nṛpavat saṃprayojya ca .
kūpasnānaṃ na kurvīta taṭākādiṣu satsu ca .. 26 ..
 
teṣu nālpodake snāyāttīrtheṣu bahuvāriṣu .
eteṣvapi tu na snāyāt satyāṃ sariti sādhakaḥ .. 27 ..
 
saritsvapi ca sarvāsu viśiṣṭāḥ syuḥ samudragāḥ .
tāsāmapi viśiṣṭāḥ syuḥ sarvāḥ prāksrotasaḥ sadā .. 28 ..
 
nadīnāmapi sarvāsāṃ dakṣiṇaṃ tīramuttamam .
prāksrotasaḥ sravantyastu yatra codaṅmukhasthitāḥ .. 29 ..
 
prāktīraṃ tatra tīrthaṃ syāt sarvapāpapraṇāśanam .
kūpāddaśaguṇā vāpī vāpyā daśaguṇā nadī .. 30 ..
 
nadyāṃ snānaphalaṃ snātustathā tasyāḥ samudragāḥ .
tathā daśaguṇaṃ tasyāḥ prāksrotāḥ kurute phalam .. 31 ..
 
prāksrotasodaṅmukhāyāḥ prāktīre'nantakaṃ phalam .
pūrvaṃ tu kṣālite tīre saṃprokṣya sthāpayet pṛthak .. 32 ..
 
jalasaṃpūrṇapātraṃ ca astramantroddhṛtaṃ mune .
śaucārthaṃ mṛdamāhṛtya jalakūle nidhāya vai .. 33 ..
 
manorame śucau deśe tṛṇānnikṣipya bhūtale .
divāsandhyāsu karṇasthabrahmasūtra udaṅmukhaḥ .. 34 ..
 
kuryānmūtrapurīṣe tu rātrau ceddakṣiṇāmukhaḥ .
na kuryādbhuvi viṇmūtre saṃbhavaddīrghajantuṣu .. 35 ..
 
na cāpsu na girau cāpi catvareṣu catuṣpathe .
na rājamārge no vīthyāṃ na devāyatane kvacit .. 36 ..
 
na śmaśāne na caitye ca na bhasmani na govraje .
na grāmamadhye viprendra kurvītāpyanyathāvidhi .. 37 ..
 
ātmacchāyāṃ tarucchāyāṃ na meheta kadācana .
avakuṇṭhyottamāṅgaṃ tu na paśyeddiggaṇaṃ malam .. 38 ..
 
tathā jyotīṃṣyapaśyaṃśca devatāyatanāni ca .
purīṣaṃ gudasaṃyuktaṃ kāṣṭhaparṇatṛṇādibhiḥ .. 39 ..
 
vāmahastena sammārjya tena hastatalena tu .
gṛhītaśiśnaścotthāya jalakūlaṃ samāśrayet .. 40 ..
 
ūrudvayāntarasthena gudaṃ mṛddāyinā'pi ca .
dākṣiṇyajānorbāhyaṃ ca dīyamānajalena ca .. 41 ..
 
vāmena dakṣiṇenaiva pāṇinā kukkuṭāsanī .
aspṛṣṭatīrthaḥ śaucārthaṃ mṛdbhirabhyuddhṛtairjalaiḥ .. 42 ..
 
gandhalepakṣayakaraṃ śaucaṃ kuryādatandritaḥ .
tisro liṅge mṛdo deyā ekaikāntaramṛttikāḥ .. 43 ..
 
pañca vāmakare deyāstisraḥ pāṇyorviśuddhaye .
mūtrotsarge śuddhireṣā purīṣasyāpyanantaram .. 44 ..
 
ardhaprasṛtimātraṃ tu prathamā mṛttikā smṛtā .
dvitīyā ca tṛtīyā ca tadardhā parikīrtitā .. 45 ..
 
biḍālapadamātraṃ tu tadūrdhvā parikīrtitā .
pañcāpāne mṛttikāḥ syustathaivāntaramṛttikāḥ .. 46 ..
 
daśa vāmakare deyāḥ sapta tūbhayahastayoḥ .
pādābhyāṃ tisṛbhiḥ śuddhirjaṅghāśuddhiśca pañcabhiḥ .. 47 ..
 
niyojayettato vipra kaṭyāṃ vai sapta mṛttikāḥ .
svadehasvedadoṣaghnā bāhyakardamaśāntaye .. 48 ..
 
bhaktānāṃ śrotriyāṇāṃ ca varṣāsvevaṃ nirūpitam .
prāvṛ ḍuktāttu vai tasmādekamṛdvyapanodanam .. 49 ..
 
śaradgrīṣmavasanteṣu nityaṃ kāryaṃ kriyāparaiḥ .
etasmādapi caikaikā parilopyā tu mṛttikā .. 50 ..
 
hemante śiśire vipra śrotriyaiḥ saṃyamasthitaiḥ .
pathi śaucaṃ prakartavyaṃ deśakālānurūpataḥ .. 51 ..
 
gandhalepamapāsyaivaṃ manaḥ śuddhyā viśudhyati .
vihitāḥ pādaśauce tu biḍālapadasaṃmitāḥ .. 52 ..
 
mṛdaścaturdvijendrāṇāṃ trirdvirekā kramāttataḥ .
varṇānāṃ śūdraniṣṭhānāṃ kaṭiśauce tathaiva hi .. 53 ..
 
sapta sapta ca ūrubhyāṃ karābhyāṃ tritayaṃ punaḥ .
sarveṣāmeva sāmānyaṃ pāṇiśaucamudāhṛtam .. 54 ..
 
antarjānugataṃ kṛtvā bhujayugmaṃ dvijottama .
caturdhā maṇibandhasthaṃ toyaṃ kṛtvā sunirmalam .. 55 ..
 
budbudādyairvinirmuktaṃ pibedvipro hṛdā tataḥ .
ekaikāṃ hrāsayenmātrāṃ varṇatrayamanukramāt .. 56 ..
 
pāṇinā kṣālitenaiva punarācāmayedbudhaḥ .
evaṃ prakṣālya vidhivadācamya prayataḥ śuciḥ .. 57 ..
 
prāṅmukhodaṅmukho vā'pi upaviśyāsanaṃ tataḥ .
arkādibhirapāmārgaiḥ kārayeddantadhāvanam .. 58 ..
 
prātarbhuktvā ca mṛdvagraṃ kaṣāyakaṭutiktakam .
bhakṣayeddantadhavanaṃ dantamāṃsānyabādhayan .. 59 ..
 
dvādaśāṅgulamātraṃ tu vakragranthivivarjitam .
payobhiḥ saha tarjanyā brahma dvādaśasaṃkhyayā .. 60 ..
 
kāṣṭhālābhe tu roge vā kartavyaṃ dantadhāvanam .
ṣoḍaśāṅguladīrghaistu vakragranthivivarjitaiḥ .. 61 ..
 
hemādinirmitairvā'pi kuśadarbhādibhistathā .
jihvānirlehanaṃ caiva gaṇḍūṣaṃ mukhadhāvanam .. 62 ..
 
kuryādācamanaṃ vipra śuddhena salilena ca .
vinā vividhasaṃparkaiḥ pañcāṅgasnānamācaret .. 63 ..
 
mukhaṃ karadvayopetaṃ pādau kaṭitalāvadhi .
strīsaṅgādyupaghāteṣu snānaṃ kuryādyathāvidhi .. 64 ..
 
adhottamāṅgāt pādāntaṃ śirasā'bhyañjayeddvija .
aṅgānyudvartya cāstreṇa caraṇāntānyanukramāt .. 65 ..
 
gomayena mṛdā vipra nirmalīkṛtya vigraham .
narāmaraprayuktāṃ prāk snānārthaṃ cāharet khalīm .. 66 ..
 
māṣacūrṇādinā dehaṃ nirhṛtya kavacaṃ smaran .
śuddhyarthaṃ prathamaṃ snātvā mantrasnānaṃ samācaret .. 67 ..
 
snāyādrājopacāreṇa divyairgandhaiḥ purā'hṛtaiḥ .
hṛnmantreṇa ca viprendra vāmahastatale tataḥ .. 68 ..
 
mṛdā'malakamānena kramaśo'bhinidhāya ca .
prāntaparvāvadhau madhye maṇibandhasamīpataḥ .. 69 ..
 
astramantreṇa mūlena kramāt pañcāṅgamantritam .
kṛtvā niyojya dikṣvapsu sarvāṅgālepanaṃ kramāt .. 70 ..
 
adha ūrdhve ca tanmantraṃ mudrābandhena saṃyutam .
tena snānaharā vighnā digvidikparisaṃsthitāḥ .. 71 ..
 
prayānti vihvalībhūtā yāvattannopasaṃhṛtam .
mṛdbhāgo mūlmantreṇa mantrito yaḥ purā sthitaḥ .. 72 ..
 
tamuccaran samādāya toyamadhye vinikṣipet .
tena taddvijaśārdūla tatkṣaṇādeva jāyate .. 73 ..
 
gaṅgātoyena saṃpūrṇaṃ yāmunena śubhena ca .
prayāgaṃ cakratīrthaṃ ca prabhāsaṃ puṣkarāṇi ca .. 74 ..
 
bhavanti sannidhībhūtā mantrasyāsya prabhāvataḥ .
tato vai viṣṇutīrthāya mantrānte padamuccaret .. 75 ..
 
sanamaskaṃ bhavettena viṣṇutīrthasya sannidhau .
anyatīrthe yadā snānaṃ kuryāttatra ca yojayet .. 76 ..
 
kevalaṃ mūlamantraṃ tu viṣṇutīrthapadaṃ vinā .
tīrthāntareṣvidaṃ nāma na saṃkīrtayate sudhīḥ .. 77 ..
 
nityasannidhitīrthasya yadyanyasyābhidhāṃ smaret .
snātasya tatra tīrthaṃ tadabhiśāpaṃ kṣaṇaṃ sṛjet .
nirjharāmbutaṭākādau sāmānyasnānakarmaṇi .
gaṅgādīnāṃ nadīnāṃ ca tīrthānāṃ ca prakīrtanam .. 79 ..
 
mantrasnānaṃ kramaiḥ samyagviṣṇutīrthāya kīrtayet .
tato'ṅgamantrajaptaṃ ca bhāgaṃ pāṇitale sthitam .. 80 ..
 
toyenāloḍya masṛṇaṃ tāpayedarkaraśmibhiḥ .
meghacchanne svakaṃ mantraṃ sūryavat khasthitaṃ smaret .. 81 ..
 
darśayitvā karau tasya tābhyāṃ sarvā'ṅgakaṃ spṛśet .
apāsya proccaran varma mṛllepaṃ vāriṇā'ṅgagam .. 82 ..
 
darbhapuñjīlamādāya dakṣiṇena kareṇa tu .
jale tvāvartya tanmantraṃ sakṛdvā bahuśo dvidhā .. 83 ..
 
tataḥ kumbhābhiṣekaṃ vā pāṇikumbhodarāmbunā .
sa hitā vartitenaiva abhiṣekaṃ tu mūrdhani .. 84 ..
 
śrotradṛgvadanaṃ nāsāṃ svakarāṅgulibhiḥ kramāt .
sthagayitvā nimajyātha sāṅgaṃ mantramathoccaran .. 85 ..
 
sakṛdvā bahuśaḥ śaktyā dhyāyejjyotirmayaṃ harim .
devaṃ hṛtpuṣkarāntasthaṃ netrayoratha cāntare .. 86 ..
 
sarvapāpanirāsārthaṃ kṛtvaivamaghamarṣaṇam .
prāṇāyāmaistribhirdvābhyāmekena niyatena vā .. 87 ..
 
samutthāyācaret paścāt sannirīkṣyārkamaṇḍalam .
mantramūrtirmahātejāḥ samuttīrya jalāntarāt .. 88 ..
 
snānavastraṃ parityajya paridhāyāmbarāntaram .
śikhayā'tha śikhābandhaṃ kṛtvā'camya yathāvidhi .. 89 ..
 
aṅguṣṭhamūlaṃ brāhmaṃ tu aṅgulyagraṃ tu daivikam .
paitṛkaṃ hastamadhyaṃ tu tīrthaṃ dakṣiṇahastajam .. 90 ..
 
brāhmeṇa tu pibettoyaṃ paitṛkena tu mārjrayet .
daivikena spṛśedaṅgān yeṣāṃ tṛptiṃ yadīcchati .. 91 ..
 
tridhā caturdhā vā vipra dvirāmṛjya mukhaṃ punaḥ .
vāmahastatalaṃ prokṣya pādayośca tale śubhe .. 92 ..
 
talena hṛdayaṃ spṛṣṭvā mukhamaṅgulibhistathā .
aṅguṣṭhānāmikāṃ kṛtvā netre spṛṣṭvā ca vāriṇā .. 93 ..
 
tenaiva tarjanīṃ kṛtvā tathā dve nāsikāpuṭe .
kaniṣṭhikāṃ tathā kṛtvā tenaiva śravaṇaṃ spṛśet .. 94 ..
 
tathaiva madhyamāṃ kṛtvā bāhudeśāvubhau spṛśet .
tenaiva nābhideśaṃ ca savairyuktaiḥ śiraḥ spṛśet .. 95 ..
 
etadācamanaṃ proktaṃ sarvakarmasu sarvadā .
sajalaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ kṛtvā ghrāṇāgragaṃ mune .. 96 ..
 
smaran hṛnmantramāghrāya sandhārya kavacaṃ lapan .
virecya samudīryāstraṃ toyakṣepeṇa vai saha .. 97 ..
 
tatastu hastayordehe nyāsaṃ kuryādyathāga mam .
hṛdā vāmakare toyamādāya galitaṃ ca tat .. 98 ..
 
vibudhānūrdhvadehasthān hlādayecchikhayā kṣipan .
smarannastraṃ kṣipedbhūmau duṣṭadoṣapraśāntaye .. 99 ..
 
antarāntarayogena hyūrdhvāntaṃ prāgadhastataḥ .
jalāñjalimathādāya sa mantreṇa hariṃ smaran .. 100 ..
 
sūryamaṇḍalamadhyasthaṃ tarpayettena vāriṇā .
sakuśordhvakaraścātha vinimīlitadṛgjapan .. 101 ..
 
sūryaṃ nirīkṣayenmantraṃ yadardhyeṇārcitaṃ purā .
tatopaviśya santarpya ā dhārāsanapūrvakam .. 102 ..
 
sāṅgaṃ saparivāraṃ ca mantraṃ tadanu vai kramāt .
indrādīn viṣṇupūrvāṃśca vāsudevādikānapi .. 103 ..
 
mūrtīrdvādaśaśaktīśca paramātmānameva ca .
pṛthivyādīni bhūtāni ṛṣīṃśca pitṛbhissaha .. 104 ..
 
ādau nāma dvitīyāntaṃ tarpayāmīti coccaran .
eṣa mantrastu nirdiṣṭastarpaṇeṣu yathākramam .. 105 ..
 
tilodakaistarpayitvā svapitṝṃśca pitāmahān .
prapitāmahasaṃjñāṃśca sadārānanutarpayet .. 106 ..
 
tarpayetsarvapitṝṇāṃ dakṣiṇābhimukhena tu .
devānāṃ ca tadanyeṣāṃ prāṅmukho vā'pyudaṅmukhaḥ .. 107 ..
 
pavitrakaṃ tyajet paścāt punarācamya mantravit .
sāyaṃ prātardiśo vandyāddhyātvā nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum .. 108 ..
 
karaśuddhisamopetaṃ digbandhaṃ cāvakuṇṭhanam .
prāṇāyāmādikaṃ kuryādbhutaśuddhisamanvitam .. 109 ..
 
mantranyāsaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā mudrāṃ badhvā smareddharim .
jalamadhye'pi yāgasya bhogaiścaivāsanādikaiḥ .. 110 ..
 
tato mantrī samabhyarcya patrapuṣpaphalairvibhum .
saṃbhave sati puṣpāṇāṃ vihitaṃ tatra cārcanam .. 111 ..
 
audakenopacāreṇa bhāvanābhāvitena ca .
tarpayedambhasā prāgvaddhomabhāvanayā'khilam .. 112 ..
 
evaṃ kṛtvā jagannāthaṃ samiddānaṃ samācaret .
juhuyācca yathāśakti tatastilaghṛtādi yat .. 113 ..
 
nyūnātiriktaśāntyarthaṃ sarvakarmasamāptaye .
pūrṇāhutyavasānāntaṃ kuryādvai jalatarpaṇe .. 114 ..
 
stutvā ca praṇamedvipra aṣṭāṅgenātha daṇḍavat .
dūrvāṃ siddhārthakopetāṃ śikhāmantrābhimantritām .. 115 ..
 
cūḍyottamāṅge śirasā upasaṃhṛtya sāsanam .
vācyaṃ jalāt svahṛdvyomni manasā niṣkalātmanā .. 116 ..
 
kṛtvābhigamanaṃ kṛtyaṃ sanyasecca vicakṣaṇaḥ .
kuryādbhogārjanaṃ paścānyāyopāyasamārjitam .. 117 ..
 
mūlena vā'stramantreṇa puṣpamūlaphalādikam .
avapannaṃ tvabhimatamanāptaṃ bhāvadūṣitam .. 118 ..
 
vyāmiśrahīnasaṃspṛṣṭaṃ śuktaṃ līḍhaṃ ca varjayet .
samyak pūrakayuktyā tu dhiyā vācakamuccaran .. 119 ..
 
apāmārgaśamīśākhāyugmaṃ saṃbhrāmya mūrdhani .
savyāpasavyayogena pṛṣṭhato'straṃ paṭhan kṣipet .. 120 ..
 
snānavastraṃ ca niṣpīḍya tataścācamya vāgyataḥ .
ityuktamaudakaṃ snānamatha māntraṃ nibodha me .. 121 ..
 
toyābhāve ca yatkuryāddurge kāle tu śītale .
gamane kṣiprasiddhau vā gurukārye'svatantratām .. 122 ..
 
prāptāṃ vā vīkṣya viprendra niśābhāge dinasya vā .
prakṣālya pādāvācamya proddhṛtena ca vāriṇā .. 123 ..
 
sthānaṃ daśa diśaḥ prāgvat saṃśodhyopaviśettataḥ .
prāṇāyāmagaṇaṃ kuryādbhutaśuddhiṃ tatastanau .. 124 ..
 
mūlamantrāditaḥ kuryāt sarvamantragaṇena tu .
kevalādudakasnānāt saṃskāraparivarjitāt .. 125 ..
 
prayāgādiṣu tīrtheṣu yatphalaṃ kurute dvija .
snānācchataguṇaṃ tasmānmantrasnānasya sattam .. 126 ..
 
dhyānasnānamatho vakṣye dvābhyāmapi paraṃ tu yat .
khasthitaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ mantramūrtiṃ prabhuṃ smaret .. 127 ..
 
tatpādodakajāṃ dhārāṃ patamānāṃ hi mūrdhani .
cintayedbrahmarandhreṇa praviśantīṃ svakāṃ tanum .. 128 ..
 
tayā saṃkṣālayet sarvamantardehagataṃ malam .
tatkṣaṇādvirajā mantrījāyate sphaṭikopamaḥ .. 129 ..
 
dhyānasnānaṃ paraṃ mantrasnānācchataguṇaṃ smṛtam .
sadhyānasnānamityuktaṃ divyasnānādikaṃ śrṛṇu .. 130 ..
 
sahātapena varṣeṇa snānaṃ divyamanantaram .
samidhāṃ dīpitānāṃ ca gomayasya huta sya ca .. 131 ..
 
sitena bhasmanā'ṅgeṣu lalāṭādiṣu ca kramāt .
yadūrdhvapuṇḍrakaraṇaṃ mantroccāraṇapūrvakam .. 132 ..
 
dāhanaṃ tu bhavetsnānaṃ śodhanaṃ paramaṃ smṛtam .
gacchatsu goṣu vātotthai rajobhirbhūmisaṃbhavaiḥ .. 133 ..
 
sparśanaṃ vapuṣaḥ snānaṃ vāyavyaṃ tadudāhṛtam .
praśaste parvatāgrādau jātayā śvetamṛtsnayā .. 134 ..
 
uccārya keśavādīni nāmānyaṅge yathākramam .
lalāṭādau yadvidhānamūrdhvapuṇḍrasya tatsa mam .. 135 ..
 
pārthivasnānamityevaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ śubham .
tasmādekatamaṃ kāryaṃ snānaṃ śraddhāpareṇa tu .. 136 ..
 
snānācamanaśaucena prāṇāyāmena deśikaḥ .
antarbahiḥ śarīrasya sādhakastu viśudhyati .. 137 ..
 
snānapūrvāḥ kriyāḥ sarvāḥ phalasaṃsiddhihetavaḥ .
tasmātsnānaṃ prakurvīta devarṣipitṛtarpaṇam .. 138 ..

Chapter - 3
. . śrīḥ .
      tṛtīyo'dhyāyaḥ .
sāstraṃ dūrvāṅkuraṃ datvā patraṃ puṣpaṃ tilāṃstu vā .
sodakānātmano mūrdhni śikhāsthāne ca sattama .. 1 ..
 
tataḥ kalaśapūrvaṃ tu ambupūrṇaṃ tu bhājanam .
samādāyāmbaracchannaṃ pāṇinā bhagavadgṛham .. 2 ..
 
ekāntaṃ nirjanaṃ yāyānmanojñaṃ doṣavarjitam .
anukūlaṃ śuciṃ dakṣaṃ saṃyataṃ samaye sthitam .. 3 ..
 
ekāyanaṃ vaidikaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ cārdhyavāhakam .
hṛnmadhyasthaṃ smaranmantraṃ prabuddhānandavigraham .. 4 ..
 
digantaramavīkṣan vai maunī saṃrodhitānilaḥ .
prāpya sthānaṃ svamantraṃ taṃ nāsāgreṇa virecayet .. 5 ..
 
uccarandvādaśārṇaṃ tu praviśyāntaḥ pradakṣiṇam .
prāsādoddeśamakhilaṃ mārjayet prokṣayettataḥ .. 6 ..
 
paricāraistu kartavyaṃ balipīṭhāntameva hi .
dvārādbāhye yathāśāstraṃ śuddhena salilena ca .. 7 ..
 
ājānupādau prakṣalya hastau cāmaṇibandhanāt .
pūrvoktena vidhānena samācamyordhvuṇḍrakaiḥ .. 8 ..
 
candanādyaiḥ sugandhairvā dharmakṣetre viśeṣataḥ .
parvatāgre nadītīre sindhutīre tathaiva ca .. 9 ..
 
valmīke tulasīmūle praśastā mṛttikā dvija .
vaśyārthī raktayā śrīcchan pītayā śāntikāmikaḥ .. 10 ..
 
śyāmayā mokṣakāmī ca śvetayā cordhvapuṇḍrakam .
vartidīpākṛtiṃ caiva veṇupatrākṛtiṃ yathā .. 11 ..
 
padmasya mukulākāramutpalaṃ mukulākṛti .
matsyakūrmākṛtiṃ caiva śaṅkhākāramataḥ param .. 12 ..
 
puṣṭipradenāṅguṣṭhena tarjanyā muktisiddhaye .
vāñchitārthapradāyinyā mune'nāmikayā'tha vā .. 13 ..
 
āyuṣkāmī madhyamayā aṅgulyā caatha devatā .
etābhiraṅgulībhistu kārayenna nakhaiḥ spṛśet .. 14 ..
 
lalāṭe vāsudevaṃ ca hṛdi saṃkarṣaṇaṃ nyaset .
pradyumnaṃ dakṣiṇe cāṃse aniruddhottarāṃsake .. 15 ..
 
jalanirmathitenaiva hyūrdhvapuṇḍracatuṣṭayam .
lalāṭe keśavaṃ vidyānnārāyaṇamathodare .. 16 ..
 
mādhavaṃ hṛdaye kuryādgovindaṃ kaṇṭhakūpake .
udare dakṣiṇe pārśve viṣṇurityabhidhīyate .. 17 ..
 
tatpārśve bāhumadhye tu madhusūdana iṣyate .
trivikramaṃ kāṇṭhakūpe vāme kukṣau tu vāmanam .. 18 ..
 
śrīdharaṃ vāmabāhau ca hṛṣīkeśaṃ tu kaṇṭhake .
apare padmanābhaṃ tu kakuddāmodaraṃ smaret .. 19 ..
 
evaṃ dvādaśanāmaṃ tu vāsudevaṃ tu mūrdhani .
yajño dānaṃ tapo homo bhojanaṃ pitṛkarma ca .. 20 ..
 
tatsarvaṃ niṣphalaṃ proktamūrdhvapuṇḍravinākṛtam .
tasmātsarvaprayatnena dhārayetsarvasiddhidam .. 21 ..
 
caturaṅgulamagraṃ tu sadāviṣṇvadhidaivatam .
mahāviṣṇvadhidaivastu granthirekāṅgulo bhavet .. 22 ..
 
viṣṇva dhidaivaṃ valayaṃ dvayamaṅgulamucyate .
pavitraṃ hastayugme cānāmikāyāṃ niyojayet .. 23 ..
 
darbhairvinā tu yatsnānaṃ vinā naivedyamarcanam .
vinodakaṃ tu yaddānaṃ tatsarvaṃ niṣphalaṃ bhavet .. 24 ..
 
arcanaṃ japahomau ca dānaṃ ca pitṛtarpaṇam .
apavitrānupāṇiścet tatsarvaṃ ca vinaśyati .. 25 ..
 
tasmāt sarvaprayatnena sadā dhāryaṃ pavitrakam .
gandhaiḥ sragbhiralaṅkārai sottarīyaiśca bhūṣitaḥ .. 26 ..
 
karṇabhūṣaṇahārādyaiḥ kaṭakairaṅgulīyakaiḥ .
alābhe tvaṅgulīyena alaṅkṛtya tu sādhakaḥ .. 27 ..
 
vadanaṃ nāsikārandhre sthagayitvā'mbareṇa tu .
svaśvāsopahataṃ caiva na bhavecca yathā dvija .. 28 ..
 
śuklavāsāḥ suveṣaśca śukladantaḥ śucivrataḥ .
tāmbūlaśuddhavadano lalāṭe cākṣatairyutaḥ .. 29 ..
 
evamuktaguṇairyukto bodhayet puruṣottamam .
śaṅkhadhvanisamopetaṃ dundubhīpaṭahasvanaiḥ .. 30 ..
 
vandibṛndotthitoccābirnānāvāgbhirmahāmate .
mahājayajayārāvaiḥ punaḥpunarudīritaiḥ .. 31 ..
 
pravodhalakṣaṇaiḥ stotrairutthāpya śayanāttataḥ .
dvāramāsādya tatrastho daśadigbandhapūrvakam .. 32 ..
 
avakuṇṭhyātha tarjanyā mantraṃ kavacamuccaran .
sthite vā kalpite tatra pūjayedbalimaṇḍale .. 33 ..
 
sarvaṃ khageśapūrvaṃ tu parivāraṃ hi sācyutam .
namasā praṇavādyena puṣpamādāya kīrtayet .. 34 ..
 
samastaparivārāya acyutāya namo namaḥ .
vāstupūruṣamanyāṃśca samabhyarcya yathākramam .. 35 ..
 
mūlamantreṇa sāṅgena niraṅgenāthavā tataḥ .
nyāsaṃ kagṛtvā trirācāryo hastatālaṃ hṛdā tataḥ .. 36 ..
 
mūlamantreṇa coddhāṭya kavāṭaṃ netramantrataḥ .
nityadīpāṃstatojjvālya hastau prakṣālya vāriṇā .. 37 ..
 
prāsādādi yadā na syāttadā deśaṃ manoharam .
āsādya kalpayenmāntraṃ gṛhaṃ tadadhunocyate .. 38 ..
 
mūlamantraṃ purā dhyāyedbrahmavat sarvagaṃ tataḥ .
vidikṣu dikṣu madhye ca jvalantaṃ bhānukoṭivat .. 39 ..
 
hṛnmantraṃ ca tadantasthamākramyākhilamātmanā .
śiromantraṃ ca tanmadhye brahmanāḍīsvarūpiṇam .. 40 ..
 
stambhabhūtaṃ tu viśvasya saṃcārādhvavadujjvalam .
śikhāmantraṃ ca sarvasmādbahiḥ prakāravat sthitam .. 41 ..
 
varmamantraṃ tu karmātmā paramātmānuvedhayet .
gavākṣadvārabhūtaṃ ca netramantraṃ ca bhāvayet .. 42 ..
 
sphuradvahnisphuliṅgormisahasraparirājitam .
sarvavighnapraśamanaṃ bahirastraṃ ca bhāvayet .. 43 ..
 
evaṃ māntragṛhaṃ dhyātvā tato dvāraṃ tu cetasā .
tribhāgīkṛtya tanmadhye bhāgamekaṃ dvidhā punaḥ .. 44 ..
 
vibhajya vāmadeśena dakṣiṇenāṅghriṇā tataḥ .
śanaiḥ śanai praviśyāntaḥ sāstramantreṇa tena vai .. 45 ..
 
dharaṇīhananaṃ kṛtvā bhagavantaṃ praṇamya ca .
manasā guruvaṃśaṃ ca tadājñāṃ mānasīmatha .. 46 ..
 
śirasā dhārayet sveṣṭaṃ phalaṃ saṃkalpya cetasā .
devāya ca nivedyai tat yāgāgārasya madhyataḥ .. 47 ..
 
prāsādaṃ vigrahaṃ klṛptvā varmamantraṃ savigraham .
tajjīvaṃ bhagavantaṃ ca dhyātvā yāgagṛhaṃ tataḥ .. 48 ..
 
saśalākaistato darbhaiḥ sahadevīvimiśritaiḥ .
saṃmārjya bahutoyena prakṣālyā'lipya gomayaiḥ .. 49 ..
 
gomayaṃ ca navaṃ grāhyaṃ bhūmiṣṭhaṃ dhenusaṃbhavam .
sajalaṃ śithilaṃ śuṣkaṃ kīṭhavacca vivarjayet .. 50 ..
 
upaliptamathāstreṇa saṃvidhya śakalaṃ tyajet .
pañcagavyena sāstreṇa vārā vā prokṣya candanaiḥ .. 51 ..
 
kuṅkumāgarukarpūraiḥ samālipya samantataḥ .
kuśadūrvākṣatāṃścaiva vikiret sthānaśuddhaye .. 52 ..
 
prāsādaṃ śodhayitvā tu tato maunaparo dvija .
deveśasyāgrato vā'pi dakṣiṇaṃ bhāgamāśrayet .. 53 ..
 
darbhe carmaṇi vastre vā phalake yajñakāṣṭhaje .
svāsanaṃ nyasyanaṃ vārbhi śca mūlamantrābhimantritaiḥ .. 54 ..
 
prokṣya choṭikayā'streṇa dadyāttacchuddhaye punaḥ .
turyādīnāṃ tu tatraikaṃ bhāvayedāsanaṃ tvatha .. 55 ..
 
turyaṃ nāma'sanaṃ pūrvaṃ kāraṇapraṇavā nvitam .
suṣuptirnāma tadvyāptāvyaktapaṅkajasaṃsthitiḥ .. 56 ..
 
svapnaḥ śeṣāhipūrvaṃ tu vahniparyantamāsanam .
kṣīrārṇavādito bhāvāsanāntaṃ jāgradāsanam .. 57 ..
 
tatra suptaṃ turīyaṃ vā karaśuddheḥ purā smaret .
svapnaṃ mānasayāgāttu pūrvaṃ turyoktakālataḥ .. 58 ..
 
jāgradāsanakalpe tu viśeṣo gṛhyatāmayam .
svadehamantravinyāsāt pūrvamabdhyādikaṃ trayam .. 59 ..
 
nyasedastrāmbunā prokṣya tāḍayitvā'strapuṣpataḥ .
tatraiva bhagavadyogapīṭhārcāyāḥ purottiram .. 60 ..
 
nyasedādhāraśaktyādi bhāvapīṭhāntamāsanam .
praṇavenātha tadvyāptiṃ smṛtvā svārṇena tena vai .. 61 ..
 
abhyarcya taduparyāsyapadmādyekatamānvitam .
yāgopaskarasaṃbhūtau bhagavantamanusmaran .. 62 ..
 
vinītān śiṣyaputrādīn snātānājñāpayettadā .
pātraśuddhiṃ tataḥ kuryādyathā tacchṛṇu sattama .. 63 ..
 
amlakalkena toyena hemaṃ tāmraṃ ca śodhayet .
rājataṃ gṛhadhūmena śāntāṅgāreṇa vā punaḥ .. 64 ..
 
bhasmamiśreṇa toyena lohayuktaṃ biśodhayet .
śaṅkhaśuktimayānāṃ ca lavaṇeva viśodhayet .. 65 ..
 
phalapatramayānāṃ ca mṛdbhiradbhiśca śodhayet .
lepagandhāpanodena śuddhirbhavati kārayet .. 66 ..
 
dravyaśuddhirbhavatyevaṃ yathāvadvidhi coditā .
athārkodayakālasya pūrvaṃ karma samārabhet .. 67 ..
 
pracchannapaṭasaṃyuktaṃ pūjākāle prapūjayet .
pāpiṣṭhānāśramabhraṣṭānnāstikān vai na darśayet .. 68 ..
 
āgamārthaṃ ca devānāṃ gamanārthaṃ ca rakṣasām .
kuryādghaṇṭāravaṃ tatra devatāhvānalāñchanam .. 69 ..
 
śaṅkhādighoṣasaṃyuktaṃ geyavādyasamanvitam .
āvāhane tathā'bhyaṅge snānārambhāvasānayoḥ .. 70 ..
 
tathā tilakadāne ca dīpe mātrānivedane .
nīrājane tvāharaṇe naivedyasya mahānasāt .. 71 ..
 
tannivedanakāle tu pūrṇāhutyavasānake .
jalāharaṇakāle ca yānārohāvarohayoḥ .. 72 ..
 
kavāṭayorvighaṭane tathā bandhe dvijottama .
eteṣu nityakāleṣu śaṅkhamāpūrayet tridhā .. 73 ..
 
pravṛttasyārcane viṣṇoḥ kṛtamaunasya tatvataḥ .
tasyāvikṣiptabuddhervai vāgdānaṃ suvirodhakṛt .. 74 ..
 
ataḥ savyabhicāraṃ tu maunaṃ varjyaṃ kriyāparaiḥ .
śubhamavyabhicāraṃ yattatkāryaṃ sarvavastuṣu .. 75 ..
 
yadaṅgasaṃketamayairavyaktairnāsikākṣaraiḥ .
kṛtamoṣṭhapuṭairbaddhairmaunaṃ tatsiddhihānikṛt .. 76 ..
 
svayameva svabuddhyā yatsarvavastuṣu vartate .
śabdairanupadiṣṭaistu tanmaunaṃ sarvasiddhidam .. 77 ..
 
karaśuddhiṃ tataḥ kuryādyathāva davadhāraya .
dve tale hastapṛṣṭhe dve sarvāścāṅgulayastathā .. 78 ..
 
astramantreṇa saṃśodhya dhyānamudrānvitena tu .
kṛtvaivaṃ karaśuddhiṃ ca sthānaśuddhiṃ samācaret .. 79 ..
 
dhyātvā devaṃ jvaladrapaṃ sahasrārkasamaprabham .
jvālākoṭisamākīrṇaṃ vamantaṃ jvalanaṃ mukhāt .. 80 ..
 
tena saṃpūrayet sarvamābrahmabhavanāntimam .
digoghaṃ prajvalantaṃ ca bhāvayenmantratejasā .. 81 ..
 
kṣmāmaṇḍalamidaṃ sarvaṃ smaret pakvaṃ ca vahninā .
mantrajena dvijaśreṣṭha mṛṇmayaṃ bhājanaṃ yathā .. 82 ..
 
sthānaśuddhirbhavatyevaṃ sudhākallolasecanāt .
bhāvayedatha digbandhaṃ kuryādāsye tu pāvakam .. 83 ..
 
kirantamastramantraṃ ca bāhubhyāṃ dakṣiṇena vā .
digvidikṣu ca sarvatra virecya svāsanādbahiḥ .. 84 ..
 
śarajālacitākāraṃ prākāraṃ bandhayedbudhaḥ .
yadvā tu pūrvavat kuryāddigbandhaṃ hṛdayādikaiḥ .. 85 ..
 
astreṇa vai vidigbandhaṃ netreṇa tu athordhvataḥ .
ādityāyutadīptena jvalatkañcukarūpiṇā .. 86 ..
 
kavacena tu tarjanyā rakṣārthamavakuṇṭhayet .
evaṃ kṛtvā tu digbandhaṃ prāṇāyāmamathārabhet .. 87 ..
 
pramāthino dṛḍhasyātha cañcalasya tu cetasaḥ .
samādhiyogyatāsiddhyai prāṇādivijayāya ca .. 88 ..
 
tamoni rharaṇārthāśca kuryāt prāṇāyatīratha .
śarīre nāḍisaṃsthānaṃ tathā prāṇādisaṃsthitam .. 89 ..
 
prāṇāyāmasvarūpaṃ ca jñātvā yāmān samācaret .
nāḍīcakraṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvanmunipuṅgava .. 90 ..
 
nāḍīnāṃ kandanābhiḥ syādutpattisthānamuttamam .
dvisaptatisahasrāṇi nāḍayo'ntarvyavasthitāḥ .. 91 ..
 
tiryagūrdhvamadhaścaiva dehaṃ vyāpya vyavasthitāḥ .
āgneyāḥ saumyarūpāśca saumyāgneyāstathaiva ca .. 92 ..
 
āgneyā ūrdhvavadanāḥ saumyasaṃjñā adhomukhāḥ .
tiryaggatā nāḍayastu saumyāgneyā udāhṛtāḥ .. 93 ..
 
nāḍīnāmapi sarvāsāṃ pradhānā daśa nāḍayaḥ .
iḍā ca piṅgalā caiva suṣumnā cordhvagāminī .. 94 ..
 
gāndhārī hastijihvā ca pūṣā caiva yaśasvinī .
alambusā kuhūścaiva ko śinī daśamī smṛtā .. 95 ..
 
suṣumnākhyā madhyanāḍī kandādūrdhvapravāhinī .
madhyanāḍyāḥ suṣumnāyā vāmadakṣiṇataḥ sthite .. 96 ..
 
iḍapiṅgalasaṃjñe dve te tu nāsāpuṭāvadhī .
purataḥ pṛṣṭhatastasyā gāndhārī hastijihvake .. 97 ..
 
vāmetarākṣyavadhike kandadeśāt samutthite .
pūṣāyaśasvinyākhye dve savyānyaśrotraniṣṭhite .. 98 ..
 
kandādvai pādamūlāntā saṃsthitā syādalambusā .
kuhūrmeḍhrāntaparyantā pādāṅguṣṭhe tu kośinī .. 99 ..
 
śukleḍā piṅgalā raktā gāndhārī pītavarṇakā .
hastijihvā kṛṣṇarūpā pūṣā syāt kṛṣṇapītakā .. 100 ..
 
yaśasvinī śyāmavarṇā babhruvarṇā hyalambusā .
kuhūraruṇasaṃkāśā kośinī hyañjanaprabhā .. 101 ..
 
evaṃ daśapradhānāstu nāḍayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ .
vāyavo daśa saṃproktāḥ śarīre nāḍiṣu sthitāḥ .. 102 ..
 
prāṇo'pānaḥ samānaśca udāno vyāna eva ca .
nāgaḥ kūrmaśca kṛkaro devadatto dhanañjayaḥ .. 103 ..
 
iḍākhyā vahati prāṇaṃ gāndhāryākhyā apānakam .
alambusā samānaṃ tu kuhūrvyānaṃ dvijottama .. 104 ..
 
udānaṃ tu suṣumnākhyā piṅgalā nāgasaṃjñitam .
pūṣā vāyuṃ tu kūrmākhyaṃ kṛkaraṃ tu yaśasvinī .. 105 ..
 
hastijihvā devadattaṃ kośinī tu dhanañjayam .
vidrumābhau prāṇanāgāvindrakopopamāvubhau .. 106 ..
 
kūrmāpānau khasaṃkāśau samānakṛkarāvubhau .
kḷñjalkasadṛśau devadattodānau dhanaṃjayaḥ .. 107 ..
 
vyānaśca phenavarṇābhaḥ sarvaśāstreṣu niścayaḥ .
atha prāṇāyatiḥsā ca niśvāsocchvāsayorgateḥ .. 108 ..
 
stambhanaṃ tatra niśvāso bāhyavātopayoginā .
ghrāṇenānayanaṃ vāyorantaḥ koṣṭhānilasya ca .. 109 ..
 
bahirniṣkāsanaṃ nāsyā ucchvāso buddhipūrvakam .
abhyantarā stambhavṛttirvāyorantaḥ prapūraṇam .. 110 ..
 
bāhyaṃ tu tadvat prathamaṃ prāṇasaṃrodhanaṃ viduḥ .
abhyantarāddvitīyastu stambhavṛttistṛtīyakam .. 111 ..
 
bāhyā tatrādhamā prāṇadhāraṇā madhyamā matā .
abhyantarā stambhavṛttiruttamā dhāraṇā matā .. 112 ..
 
sadā niśvāsarūpā tu bāhyā recakamucyate .
abhyantarā samucchvāsarūpā saṃpūrakastathā .. 113 ..
 
śvāsocchvāsanirodhātmā stambhavṛttistu kumbhakaḥ .
ekadvitribhirudghātairmṛdumadhyamatīkṣṇakāḥ .. 114 ..
 
krameṇaite bhavantyatra prāṇādernābhideśataḥ .
udgatasyāhatiḥ pūrvamudghātaḥ syāddvitīyakam .. 115 ..
 
nivṛttirudarādūrdhvaṃ tasya cātha tṛtīyakam .
anyatra nigraho'syeha mṛduḥ pūrvo'tha madhyamaḥ .. 116 ..
 
dvitīyastu tṛtīyo'tha tīkṣṇassvedādikāraṇam .
prāṇāyāmagaṇaṃ kuryāt pūrvamastreṇa recakam .. 117 ..
 
tatra dvādaśamātrastu recakaḥ pūrakaḥ smṛtaḥ .
caturviśatimātrastu ṣaṭtriṃśanmātrakaṃ viduḥ .. 118 ..
 
kumbhakaṃ cātha bhūyo'pi kevalānilaniḥsṛtiḥ .
yā sā prāṇāyatiḥ sā'pi recakākhyā vidhīyate .. 119 ..
 
mātrāvyatikramānnyūnā viparyāse tu sā'sa mā .
tasmānmātrāviśeṣeṇa jñātavyā prāṇajiṣṇunā .. 120 ..
 
jānuṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya na drutaṃ na vilambitam .
kuryādaṅgulivisphoṭaṃ sā mātrā parikīrtitā .. 121 ..
 
prāṇāyamagaṇaṃ kuryāt pūrvamastreṇa recakam .
pūrakaṃ hṛdayenātha netramantreṇa kumbhakam .. 122 ..
 
prāguktenācaredbhūyo recakaṃ dvijasattama .
vāmetarāṅgulībhyāṃ tu pidadhadvāmanāsikām .. 123 ..
 
nābhideśasthitaṃ dhyāyenmūlamantreṇa vai harim .
vāsanādoṣasaṃmiśrān daśaprāṇān sagarbhakān .. 124 ..
 
agarbhaśca sagarbhaśca prāṇāyāmo dvidhā mataḥ .
japadhyānaṃ vinā'garbhaḥ sagarbhastadyuta śca yaḥ .. 125 ..
 
agarbhādgarbhasaṃyuktaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ śatādhikaḥ .
ākṛṣyāstraṃ samuccārya dakṣiṇaghrāṇato bahiḥ .. 126 ..
 
recayedvātacakraṃ tu daśanāḍīṣvavasthitam .
mātrayaikaikayā'nyonyaṃ mocayitvā'tra pūṣi kām .. 127 ..
 
dvābhyāṃ tu piṅgalāṃ dvābhyāṃ bahirnābhyāstu recayet .
virecyaivaṃ hariṃ tāvat saṃsthāpyādāya pāvakam .. 128 ..
 
vātacakrasthitaṃ dhyāyettamevāntaḥ praveśayet .
dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhato dvāraṃ pidadhadvāmanāsayā .. 129 ..
 
hariṃ savātacakraṃ taṃ mātrābhyāmiḍayoccaran .
hṛnmantramantaḥ saṃveśya taṃ dhyātvā hṛdaye sthitam .. 130 ..
 
mātrācatuṣṭayenātha tena vātena piṅgalām .
dvābhyāṃ suṣumnāṃ gāndhārīṃ dvidvikābhistu pūṣikām .. 131 ..
 
dvābhyāṃ dvābhyāṃ hastijihvālambuse ca yaśasvinīm .
kośinīṃ ca kuhūṃ caiva kramāt saṃpūrayet gatīḥ .. 132 ..
 
nāsāpuṭādikādūrdhvaṃ netreṇāsīta kumbhavat .
ṣaṭtriṃśadbhistu mātrābhiratha nābhyagnimiśritaiḥ .. 133 ..
 
paribhramadbhiḥ sarvatra tairvātairdoṣasaṃhatīḥ .
dhyātvā nirastā nāḍīśca śodhitāstu śanaiḥ śanaiḥ .. 134 ..
 
kevalaṃ vātacakraṃ tu bahiḥ prāgvadvirecayet .
yadvā ṣoḍaśamātrā syādrecake dviguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ .. 135 ..
 
pūrakaḥ kumbhako'pi syāt sacatuḥṣaṣṭimātrakaḥ .
nāḍīstā mocayet prāgvat ṣaṇmātrābhistu piṅgalām .. 136 ..
 
nāḍīstu daśa tantrībhiḥ pañcamātrābhirarjayet .
prāṇāyāmamidaṃ proktamuttamādivibhedataḥ .. 137 ..
 
triprakāre vidhāne'tra yathāsaṃbhavamācaret .
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā pañca vā sapta vā'thavā .. 138 ..
 
bhavet prāṇajayaḥ puṃsaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ sa ucyate .
tatastu kāyaśuddhyarthaṃ varṇaṃ bhaumādi vinyaset .. 139 ..
 
bhūtaśuddhiṃ śrṛṇu mune yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ .
pṛthvyaptejonilākāśaṃ śarīraṃ bhūtapañcakam .. 140 ..
 
indrajālopamaṃ viddhi jñānādyairujjñitaṃ guṇaiḥ .
malinaṃ cāsvatantraṃ ca retoraktodbhavaṃ kṣayi .. 141 ..
 
yāvanna śodhitaṃ samyagdhāraṇābhirnirantaram .
tāvadetadayogyaṃ syānmantranyāsādivastuṣu .. 142 ..
 
pañcabhirdhāraṇābhirvā dvābhyā vā śodhayettanum .
suṣumnādakṣiṇadvārānnirgamayya hariṃ bahiḥ .. 143 ..
 
sahasraravisaṅkāśaṃ vṛttamaṇḍalamadhyagam .
taptakāñcanavarṇābhamāsīnaṃ parame pade .. 144 ..
 
mantrātmānaṃ tu taṃ dhyātvā hyupari dvādaśāṅgule .
prabhācakraṃ tu tadadhastatvādhiṣṭhātṛsaṃyutam .. 145 ..
 
niṣkalaṃ mantradehaṃ tu dhyātvā tu tadadhaḥkramāt .
turyaśrāṃ pītalāṃ bhūmiṃ cintayedvajralāñchitām .. 146 ..
 
śabdādyaiḥ pañcabhiryuktāṃ nagadrumasamākulām .
puraprākārasusariddvīpārṇavapariṣkṛtām .. 147 ..
 
saṃviśantīṃ smaredbāhyāt pūrakeṇa svavigrahe .
proccaraṃścaiva tanmantraṃ viśrāntāmatha cintayet .. 148 ..
 
jānvoḥ pādatalaṃ yāvattayā vyāptaṃ krameṇa tu .
kumbhakena dvijaśreṣṭha mantramūrtau svake tataḥ .. 149 ..
 
śanaiḥ śanairlayaṃ yātāṃ gandhaśaktau ca mantrarāṭ .
gandhaśaktiṃ ca tāṃ paścādrecakena bahiḥ kṣipet .. 150 ..
 
toyākhye ca mahādhāre tatastoyaṃ ca vaibhavam .
sasamudrasaritsrotorasaṣaṭakaṃ ca sauṣadhim .. 151 ..
 
yānyanyānyambubhūtāni bhūtāni bhuvanāntare .
ardhacandrasamākāraṃ kamaladhvajaśobhitam .. 152 ..
 
vāruṇaṃ vibhavaṃ bāhye dhyātvā tenātha vigraham .
saṃpūrya pūrakākhyena karaṇena śanaiḥ śanaiḥ .. 153 ..
 
ūrumūlācca jānvantaṃ śārīraṃ maṇḍalaṃ svakam .
tenākhilaṃ tu saṃvyāptaṃ kumbhakena smareddvija .. 154 ..
 
tanmadhye vāruṇaṃ mantraṃ dhāraṇākhyaṃ vicintya ca .
ammayaṃ vibhavaṃ sarvaṃ tanmantre vilayaṃ gatam .. 155 ..
 
tatastaṃ rasaśaktau ca sā śaktirvahnimaṇḍale .
recakena vinikṣipya tato vāhnaṃ ca vaibhavam .. 156 ..
 
trikoṇabhuvanākāraṃ dīptimadbhirvibhūṣitam .
vidyuccandrārkanakṣatramaṇiratnaiśca dhātubhiḥ .. 157 ..
 
svaprakāśaśarīraistu aśarīraiśca khecaraiḥ .
cihnitaṃ svastikairdīptairdhyātvaivaṃ vibhavaṃ mahat .. 158 ..
 
taijasaṃ muniśārdūla tanmantraṃ cātha saṃsmaret .
tanmaṇḍalāntarasthaṃ tu proccaran vai tameva hi .. 159 ..
 
praviṣṭaṃ pūrvavaddhyāyettenaiva karaṇena tu .
ānābheḥ pāyuparyantaṃ vyāptaṃ kṛtvā'vadhārya ca .. 160 ..
 
taṃ vipra vibhavaṃ sarvaṃ taijasaṃ paribhāvayet .
tanmantravigrahe śāntaṃ tanmatraṃ cānalātmakam .. 161 ..
 
rūpaśaktau layaṃ yātaṃ śaktiḥ saṃvinmayī ca sā .
tayā mantraśarīraṃ svaṃ svaśaktyā vilayīkṛtam .. 162 ..
 
recakena tu tāṃ śaktiṃ vāyvādhāre bahiḥ kṣipet .
tatastu vāyavīyaṃ vai vibhavaṃ bāhyataḥ smaret .. 163 ..
 
vṛttaṃ rājopalābhaṃ tu bimbairyuktaṃ tu taijasaiḥ .
pūrṇaṃ nānāvidhairgandhairanekaistadguṇaistathā .. 164 ..
 
svamantreṇa samākrāntaṃ dhāraṇākhyena saṃsmaret .
tathā svarūpaṃ tanmantraṃ dhyātvoccārya samāharet .. 165 ..
 
pūrvoktakaraṇenaivaṃ ghrāṇāgreṇa śanaiḥ śanaiḥ .
ākaṇṭhaṃ nābhideśāntaṃ tena vyāptaṃ tu bhāvayet .. 166 ..
 
prāguktakaraṇenaiva vāyavyaṃ vibhavaṃ tu tam .
adhiṣṭhātṛlayaṃ yātaṃ smṛtvā taṃ ca mahāmate .. 167 ..
 
sparśākhyāyāṃ mahāśaktau tāṃ śaktimavinaśvarīm .
vyāptiṃ nityāmanityāṃ ca svaśaktivibhāvānvitām .. 168 ..
 
śabdākhye tu mahādhāre nikṣipedvyomamaṇḍale .
dhyātvā'tha vibhavaṃ sarvaṃ vyomākhyaṃ vigrahādvahiḥ .. 169 ..
 
nānāśabdasamākīrṇaṃ nīrūpaṃ cāñjanaprabham .
avigrahaiḥ śabdamayaiḥ pūrṇaṃ siddhairasaṃkhyakaiḥ .. 170 ..
 
tanmadhye dhāraṇāmantraṃ vyomākhyaṃ saṃsmareddvija .
dhārayantaṃ svamātmānaṃ svasāmārthyena savadā .. 171 ..
 
śabdamātramarūpaṃ tu vyāpakaṃ vibhaveṣvapi .
dhiyā ca saṃparicchinnaṃ kṛtvā vinyasya vigrahe .. 172 ..
 
prāguktakaraṇenaiva tena vyāptaṃ ca bhāvayet .
ākaṇṭhādbrahnarandhrāntaṃ vyomākhyavibhavena ca .. 173 ..
 
sandhārya kumbhakenaiva yāvatkālaṃ tu yoginā .
dhyāyet pariṇataṃ paścāt svamantre tu mahāmune .. 174 ..
 
vyomākhyaṃ dhāraṇāmantraṃ śaktau piraṇataṃ smaret .
.. 176 ..
 
tāṃ śaktiṃ brahmarandhreṇa prayāntīmanubhāvayet .
yuktāṃ śakticatuṣkeṇa gandhādyenāvinaśvarīm .. 177 ..
 
āśrayenniṣkalaṃ mantraṃ tatvādhiṣṭhātṛsaṃyutam .
samantraṃ vibhavaṃ bhautamevamastaṃ nayet kramāt .. 178 ..
 
caitanyaṃ jīvabhūtaṃ yat prasphurattārakopamam .
bhāvanīyaṃ tu viśrāntaṃ niḥsṛtaṃ bhūtapañjarāt .. 179 ..
 
niṣprapañce pare mantre pañcaśaktyākhyavigrahe .
anena kramayogena jīva ātmānamātmanā .. 180 ..
 
īkṣeta taddhṛdākāśe acalaṃ sūryavarcasam .
sphuraddyutibhirākīrṇamīśvaraṃ vyāpakaṃ param .. 181 ..
 
tato mantraśarīrasthaḥ samādhiṃ cābhyaset param .
gandhatanmātra pūrvābhiryuktatvāt pañcaśaktibhiḥ .. 182 ..
 
heyaṃ cetthamidaṃ buddhvā yadā tatsthānabṛṃhitaḥ .
atṛpto'kṛtakṛtyaśca mantrahṛtpadmasevanāt .. 183 ..
 
ṣaṭpado hyātmatatvaśca jñānarajjvavalambya ca .
hṛtkoṭarordhvānniryāntaṃ svātmānaṃ svātmanā smaret .. 184 ..
 
bhārūpanāḍimārgeṇa mantravahneḥ śikhā hi sā .
padmasūtrapratikāśā suṣumnā cordhvagāminī .. 185 ..
 
tadbrahmarandhragāṃ smṛtvā supathā tena sattama .
śanaiḥśanaiḥsvamātmānaṃ recayejjñānavāyunā .. 186 ..
 
māntraṃ karaṇaṣaṭkaṃ ca evamavyāpakaṃ tyajet .
prāpnuyācca tadūrdhvāttu yaḥ parāt prabhuvigrahāt .. 187 ..
 
udito dvijaśārdūla tejaḥ puñjo hyanūpamaḥ .
tatprabhācakranābhisthasvānandānandananditaḥ .. 188 ..
 
evaṃ padātpadasthasya hyātmatatvasya vai tataḥ .
tatvanirmuktadehasya kevalasya cidātmanaḥ .. 189 ..
 
udeti mahadānandaḥ sā śaktirvaiṣṇavī parā .
aluptakarmakartāraṃ jīvaṃ kṛtvā tamātmasāt .. 190 ..
 
yatroditā ca tatraiva punarevāvatiṣṭhate .
tacca saṃkalpanirmuktamavācyaṃ viddhi sattama .. 191 ..
 
evaṃ svasthānamāsādya tyaktvā bhautaṃ ca vigraham .
tatra sthito dahet piṇḍaṃ śaktitanmātravarjitam .. 192 ..
 
ṣāṭkauśikamasāraṃ ca nirdaṇḍa tṛṇarūpiṇam .
icchānirmathanotthena mantrajena tu vahninā .. 193 ..
 
tenāṅghrideśādārabhya taṃ piṇḍaṃ jvalitaṃ smaret .
dakṣiṇāṅghrerathāṅguṣṭhaprāntadeśe śikhākṣaram .. 194 ..
 
dhyātvā yugāntahutabhugrūpajvālāśatāvṛtaṃ .
tena svavigrahaṃ dhyāyet prajvalantaṃ samantataḥ .. 195 ..
 
nābhikandāntaroddeśe netramantreṇa pāvakam .
dhyāyejjvālāgaṇopetaṃ ninayettena bhasmasāt .. 196 ..
 
dahanena svakaṃ deha hṛnmantraṃ bhāvayaṃstataḥ .
dehajāṃ bhāvayejjvālāṃ mantranāthe layaṃ gatām .. 197 ..
 
bhasmarāśisamaprakhyaṃ śāntāgniṃ tamanusmaret ..
tadvācakena tadbhasma yātaṃ dhyātvā itastataḥ .. 199 ..
 
tataḥ samantraṃ tadbimbaṃ pūrṇacandrāyutopamam .
dhyātvā tanniḥsṛtenaiva tvamṛtaughena cāmbarāt .. 200 ..
 
plāvayeddehajāṃ bhūtiṃ sarvaṃ dhyāyet sudhātmakam .
tatrādhāramayīṃ śaktiṃ madhye vinyasya vaiṣṇavīm .. 201 ..
 
bījabhūtāṃ ca sarvasya tadutthaṃ cāmbujaṃ smaret .
ṣaḍadhvaṃ tatvabhūtaṃ ca sitaṃ tejomayaṃ śubham .. 202 ..
 
maṇḍalatritayākīrṇaṃ sphuratkiraṇabhāsvaram .
mantrātmānaṃ ca tanmadhye dhyāyennārāyaṇaṃ prabhum .. 203 ..
 
niṣkalaṃ kevalaṃ śuddhaṃ pañcasanmantravigraham .
tanmantraśaktibhirbhūyo bhāvayenmūrchitaṃ dvija .. 204 ..
 
vyomādipañcabhūtīyaṃ māntramīśvarapañcakam .
tebhyo'tha prasarantaṃ ca vyomādyaṃ vibhavaṃ smaret .. 205 ..
 
saṃyogajanitaṃ piṇḍaṃ dhyāyedvibhavapañcakāt .
sahasrasūryasaṃkāśaṃ śatacandragabhastimat .. 206 ..
 
nirmalasphaṭikaprakhyaṃ jarāmaraṇavarjitam .
janitvaivaṃ svapiṇḍaṃ tu paramaṃ bhogamokṣayoḥ .. 207 ..
 
sādhanaṃ muniśārdūla sahajaṃ sarvadehinām .
tamāsādya krameṇaiva sisṛkṣālakṣaṇena ca .. 208 ..
 
svapadānnistaraṅgācca kṛtvā śaktyā sahodayam .
svānandaṃ ca mahānandāt svānandasyāpyapāśrayāt .. 209 ..
 
mārīcaṃ nābhasaṃ cakraṃ tasmādrūpaṃ svakaṃ ca yat .
sūryakoṭikarābhāsaṃ prasphurantaṃ svabhāsasā .. 210 ..
 
kadambagolakā kāraṃ niśāmbukaṇanirmalam .
evamātmānamānīya svasthānāt svātmanā dvija .. 211 ..
 
viśenmantraśarīraṃ svaṃ brahmarandhreṇa pūrvavat .
jyotsnānāḍīpathenaiva puryaṣṭakakajāntaram .. 212 ..
 
svavācakaṃ bhāvayan vai dhvaninā niṣkaḷena tu .
tatastu niṣkalānmantrādyāvadbhautaṃ ca vigraham .. 213 ..
 
pañcakaṃ cābhimānaṃ tu āsādyālokavigraham .
svamantrādamṛtaughena secayedvigrahaṃ svakam .. 214 ..
 
tataḥ svamantraṃ tadbimbamākṛṣya hṛdi vinyaset .
nistaraṅgā parā śaktirmahānandamayī ca sā .. 215 ..
 
svānandācca prabhācakraṃ rūpamātmīyabhāsvaram .
sauṣumnastādṛśo mārgaḥ piṇḍamantraśca niṣkalaḥ .. 216 ..
 
satyādyo mantraśaktyogho dhāraṇeśvarapañcakam .
teṣāṃ vibhavasaṅgho yaḥ piṇḍastatsāmudāyikaḥ .. 217 ..
 
smarellolīkṛtaṃ sarvamapṛthak ca pṛthak sthitam .
sthūlasūkṣmaparākhyena trividhena tu sattama .. 218 ..
 
karaṇenoditā samyak śuddhireṣā ca bhautikī .
śodhitaiḥ pañcabhirbhūtaiḥ pṛthivyādyaiḥ khapaścimaiḥ .. 219 ..
 
ghrāṇajihvākṣitvakchrotrarūpajñānendriyāṇi ca .
upasthapāyupādākhyapāṇivāgātmakāni ca .. 220 ..
 
karmendriyāṇi pañcaiva śodhitāni bhavanti hi .
tatrāpi pūrakādīnāṃ kāla āyāmavatsmṛtaḥ .. 221 ..
 
dhāraṇāpañcakenaivaṃ mukhyakalpe prakīrtitā .
anukalpe tu tāṃ vakṣye yathāvadvinibodha me .. 222 ..
 
kṣmājalānalavāyvākhyanābhasīyaṃ mahāmate .
dhāraṇāpañcakaṃ caiva saṃkṣiptaṃ vihitaṃ dvayam .. 223 ..
 
dahanāpyāyanāccaiva yadā dehāt svaśuddhaye .
nābhikṣetragataṃ dhyāyenmārutaṃ kavacena tu .. 224 ..
 
nayeddehagataṃ tena śoṣabhāvaṃ rasaṃ dvija .
nābhikandāntaroddeśe netramantreṇa pāvakam .. 225 ..
 
dhyāyejjvālāgaṇopetaṃ ninayettena bhasmasāt .
dahanena svakaṃ dehaṃ hṛnmantraṃ bhāvayaṃstataḥ .. 226 ..
 
tiṣṭhedgaganamāśritya śiromantreṇa bhāvayet .
jalaṃ muktāphalasvacchaṃ tadudbhūtamatha smaret .. 227 ..
 
śikhāmantreṇa kamalaṃ vasudhāguṇalakṣaṇam .
tadadhiṣṭhātṛbhāvena nayedātmani sattama .. 228 ..
 
dhyāyettadutthitaṃ kośaṃ bhūtatatvamayaṃ vapuḥ .
hṛdayādīn smaran pañcatatvānāṃ kāraṇātmanām .. 229 ..
 
tataḥ samācarennyāsaṃ tasmin dhyānotthite pure .
mukhyānukalpabhedena bhūtaśuddhiḥ prakrīrtitā .. 230 ..

Chapter - 4
śrīḥ .
caturtho'dhyāyaḥ .
saṃśuddhavigraho mantrī mantranyāsaṃ samācaret .
yena vinyastamātreṇa devadevasamo bhavet .. 1 ..
 
pūjādisarvakāryāṇāmadhikārī ca jāyate .
bhavedvai sarvasiddhīnāmāvirbhāvastu yena ca .. 2 ..
 
yaṃ kṛtvā nirbhayastiṣṭheddeśe duṣṭasamākule .
vijayaścāpamṛtyūnāṃ syādyena vihitena ca .. 3 ..
 
vyāpāro mānaso hyeṣa nyāsākhyo yadyapi smṛtaḥ .
na badhnāti sthitiṃ samyak tathā'pi kriyayā vinā .. 4 ..
 
karādhīnā punassā tu prāṅnyāsastu tayoḥ sthitaḥ .
atha hastadvaye nyasya dīptimaddvādaśākṣaram .. 5 ..
 
maṇibandhānnakhāgrāntaṃ tvādityātapavattataḥ .
sṛṣṭisaṃsthitisaṃhāranyāsaṃ kuryādyathāvidhi .. 6 ..
 
dakṣahastatalārambho vāmāntaḥ sṛṣṭisaṃjñitaḥ .
dakṣāṅguṣṭhādiko vāmatalāntaḥ sthitisaṃjñitaḥ .. 7 ..
 
vāmahastatalārambho dakṣānta itaraḥ smṛtaḥ .
sṛṣṭau dakṣatale tāraṃ tadaṅguṣṭhādike kramāt .. 8 ..
 
aṅgulīnāṃ tu daśake yāvadvāmakaniṣṭhikā .
vinyasya daśavarṇāṃstu nyasedvāmatale'ntimam .. 9 ..
 
sthityākhye dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhādārabhyāṅgulipañcake .
tattalāntaṃ tu tārādyaṃ varṇaṣaṭkaṃ tu vinyaset .. 10 ..
 
vāmāṅguṣṭhāttattalāntaṃ vinyaset ṣaṭkamuttaram .
saṃhārākhye'kṣaraṃ nyasya vāmahastatale'ntimam .. 11 ..
 
apyayākhyakrameṇaiva dakṣahastatalāvadhi .
tato varṇagaṇaṃ śeṣaṃ nyaset praṇavapaścimam .. 12 ..
 
tarjanyā tattadaṅguṣṭhe tattadaṅguṣṭhakena ca .
tarjanyādiṣu śākhāsu tattanmadhyamayā tale .. 13 ..
 
nyāsaṃ kuryādyathāyogaṃ tato'ṅganyāsamācaret .
ārabhya dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhācchākhāsu daśasu dvija .. 14 ..
 
kramādvāmakaniṣṭhāntaṃ dakṣiṇādi taladvaye .
hṛdādidvādaśāṅgāni bhāsvadrūpāṇi vinyaset .. 15 ..
 
dakṣiṇe madhyataḥ pajhaṃ prasphuratkiraṇojjvalam .
gadāṃ vāmatale nyasyejjvalantīṃ svena tejasā .. 16 ..
 
dakṣe mahāprabhaṃ cakraṃ śaṅkhaṃ vāmatale nyaset .
kirīṭaṃ dakṣiṇe haste śrīvatsaṃ vāmamadhmataḥ .. 17 ..
 
kaustubhaṃ dakṣiṇatale vanamālāṃ tathā'pare .
śriyaṃ dakṣiṇahaste tu puṣṭiṃ vāmatale nyaset .. 18 ..
 
aṅguṣṭhāddakṣiṇādādau vāmāntaṃ mūladeśataḥ .
gāruḍaṃ vinyasenmantraṃ daśasvaṅguliṣu kramāt .. 19 ..
 
anena vidhinā pūrvaṃ hastanyāsaṃ samācaret .
yā vibhoḥ paramā śaktirhṛtpajhakuharāntagā .. 20 ..
 
vāyavyaṃ rūpamāsthāya daśadhā saṃvyavasthitā .
icchayā svapravāheṇa pāṇimārgeṇa nirgatā .. 21 ..
 
nāḍīdaśakamāśritya tā evāṅgulayo matāḥ .
ata eva dvijaśreṣṭha śaktyākhye prabhuvigrahe .. 22 ..
 
pūrvaṃ mantragaṇaṃ nyasya tato bhūtamaye nyaset .
vigrahe mantrasaṃghātaṃ yathā tadavadhāraya .. 23 ..
 
āmūrdhnaścaraṇāntaṃ ca dvādaśārṇaṃ nyasettanau .
vyāpakatvena vinyasya pādādbhūyaḥ śiro'ntimam .. 24 ..
 
sṛṣṭisaṃsthitisaṃhāranyāsaṃ kuryāttataḥ param .
mūrdhādipādaparyantaḥ sṛṣṭinyāsaḥ prakīrtitaḥ .. 25 ..
 
pādādiśca śiro'ntastu saṃhṛtinyāsa ucyate .
yathā'bhilaṣitaṃ kuryāt sarvathā karturicchayā .. 26 ..
 
mūrdhni vaktreṃ'sayugme ca kramāt savyetare hṛdi .
pṛṣṭhe nābhau tathā kaṭyāṃ jānunoratha pādayoḥ .. 27 ..
 
krameṇa praṇavādyaṃ tu yāntaṃ dvādaśavarṇakam .
vinyasedeṣa sṛṣṭyākhyo nyāsaḥ prokto yathārthataḥ .. 28 ..
 
praṇavādyānnyasedvarṇān sthāneṣu hṛdayādiṣu .
ahgopāṅgoktamārgeṇa sthitinyāsaḥ prakīrtitaḥ .. 29 ..
 
pādayorjānunoḥ kaṭyāṃ nābhau pṛṣṭhe hṛdantare .
savyetaresayugme ca vaktre mūldhani ca nyaset .. 30 ..
 
yādivarṇāṃstu tārāntāneṣa saṃhārasaṃjñakaḥ .
tato hṛdādisthāneṣu aṅgopāhgāni vinyaset .. 31 ..
 
nyasettu hṛdaye jñānaṃ yato vyajyeta tatra tat .
aiśvaryaṃ śirasoddeśe yasmādupari tiṣṭhati .. 32 ..
 
prākṛtaṃ tātvikaṃ vā'pi sarvatra munisattam .
hṛdagnerūrdhvagāyāṃ tu śikhāyāṃ śaktimantrarāṭ .. 33 ..
 
balaṃ cākhilagātrāṇāṃ tvaggataṃ vāyunā saha .
mūrchitaṃ sarvagātrairyattadvīryaṃ hastayornyaset .. 34 ..
 
antarbodhasvarūpaṃ yat prākṛtadhvāntaśāntikṛta .
tejastattaijase sthāne nyāsakāle samasyate .. 35 ..
 
yathoktavidhinā so'yaṃ vidhirūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyate .
tataḥ pajhagadācakraśaṅkhān prāgvattu vinyaset .. 36 ..
 
kirīṭaṃ mūrdhni vinyasya vahnyarkāyutadīdhitim .
śrīvatsaṃ vakṣaso'vāme pūrṇendusadṛśadyutim .. 37 ..
 
kaustubhaṃ hṛdaye nyasya caṇḍadīdhitilakṣaṇam .
nānābjavanapuṣpotthāṃ vanamālāṃ ca kaṇṭhataḥ .. 38 ..
 
ācāṃsāddhakṣiṇe bhāge nyasyā śrīruttare tathā .
puṣṭiṃ gulphāvasāne ca garuḍaṃ corumūlataḥ .. 39 ..
 
bhāsvadrūpāṇi cāṅgāni cidekavibhavāni ca .
kirīṭādīni cānyāni sarvāṇyābharaṇāni ca .. 40 ..
 
yathā prasiddharūpāṇi svasvakāntidharāṇi ca .
mantranyāsaṃ tu kṛtvaivaṃ yathoddiṣṭakameṇa tu .. 41 ..
 
āmūlamantrāt sarvāsāṃ mudrāṇāṃ bandhamācaret .
svaṃ svaṃ udīrayanmantraṃ parameśvaravattataḥ .. 42 ..
 
saṃcintya rūpamātmīyaṃ sābhimānaṃ mahāmate .
mūlamantrābhijaptaṃ ca kusumaṃ ca śikhāvadhau .
svavigrahe tu śirasā dadyādgandhāmbubhāvitam .. 43 ..

Chapter - 5
śrīḥ .
pañcamo'dhyāyaḥ .
kṛtvaivaṃ tu tataḥ paścānmānasaṃ yāgamārabhet .
padmāsanādikaṃ badhvā nābhau brahmāñcaliṃ dṛḍham .. 1 ..
 
manasyuparataṃ kuryādakṣagrāmaṃ bahiḥ sthitam .
cittaṃ buddhau vinikṣipya tāṃ buddhiṃ jñānagocare .. 2 ..
 
jñānabhāvanayā karma kuryādvai pāramārthikam .
catuścakre navadvāre dehe devagṛhe pure .. 3 ..
 
kaṇṭhakūpadharārūḍhaṃ hṛtpadmaṃ yadadhomukham .
tatkarṇikāvanermadhyade śamāśritya bhāvayet .. 4 ..
 
nābhimeḍhrāntare dhyāyecchaktiṃ cādhārarūpiṇīm .
kālāgniṃ ca tadurdhve tu anantaṃ tasya copari .. 5 ..
 
tadūrdhve vasudhāṃ devīṃ caturbhiḥ pūritaṃ smaret .
kanda nābhyavasānaṃ ca caturdhā bhājitaiḥ padaiḥ .. 6 ..
 
nābhau kṣīrārṇavaṃ dhyātvā tataḥ padmaṃ samutthitam .
sahasradalasaṃyuktaṃ sahasrakiraṇāvṛtam .. 7 ..
 
sahasraraśmisaṃkāśaṃ tatpṛṣṭhe cāsanaṃ nyaset .
dharmaṃ jñānaṃ ca vairāgyamaiśvaryaṃ ca caturthakam .. 8 ..
 
avatārya svamantreṇa āgnoyādye catuṣṭaye .
catuṣkametadvinyasya yāvadīśānagocaram .. 9 ..
 
tatpūrvadigvibhāgādi yāvaduttaragocaram .
nyasyādharmaṃ tathā'jñānamavairāgyamanaiśvaram .. 10 ..
 
puruṣākṛtayastvete bandhūkakusumojjvalāḥ .
prāgīśānadigante tu prāgāgneyadigantare .. 11 ..
 
yātuvāruṇamadhye tu vāyavyavaruṇāntare .
ṛgvedādyaṃ catuṣkaṃ tu kṛtādyaṃ yugasaṅghakam .. 12 ..
 
īśānasomadiṅmadhye antakāgnidigantare .
yāmyarākṣasamadhye tu somasāmīraṇāntare .. 13 ..
 
tanmūrdhni kālacakraṃ tu tanmadhye'vyaktapaṅkajam .
vāyavyodbhūtanālaṃ tu vikārādhārasaṃsthitam .. 14 ..
 
bhūtānyādhāraśaktau tu tanmātrāḥ kālapāvake .
vāgādikaṃ tathaivākṣamanantaṃ vyāpta saṃsthitam .. 15 ..
 
śrotrādikaṃ dharaṇyāṃ ca manaḥ kṣīrārṇave dvija .
anantadalapadme tu ahaṅkāraḥ samāśritaḥ .. 16 ..
 
dviraṣṭakaṃ ca dharmādyamadhiṣṭāya ca dhī sthitā .
tadūrdhvapajhe prakṛtirguṇasāmyavibhāginī .. 17 ..
 
dhāmatrayāśritaḥ kālo bhāvākhye puruṣasthitiḥ .
ādheyamabjasaṃbhūta sve vikāre svarūpiṇi .. 18 ..
 
svayamādyantayo ruddhaṃ sūtre maṇigaṇo yathā .
prāgādhārātmanā caiva viśvākāratayā tataḥ .. 19 ..
 
nānāmantrātmanā hyūrdhve nistaraṅgo hi tatvataḥ .
abhyastavāsanānāṃ ca karmiṇāṃ karmaśāntaye .. 20 ..
 
tadicchāviṣkṛtānāṃ ca bhogakaivalyasiddhaye .
anādyavidyāviddhānāmiyattaiṣā hyavastuni .. 21 ..
 
nātordhve tatvadṛṣṭīnāṃ tatvato vā'sti pauṣkara .
na tiryakpṛṣṭhapūrve ca na heyādivikalpanā .. 22 ..
 
yā viśeṣavikalpaistu pratyastamitalakṣaṇā .
śaktirbhagavato viṣṇoḥ sādhārākhyā'bhidhīyate .. 23 ..
 
prāgvadāsanasāmarthyaṃ bījamādāya cecchayā .
avyaktavyaktarūpā ca yathādityakadambakam .. 24 ..
 
bhāviprasaradharmitvādviśvabījacayasya ca .
sāṃprataṃ saṃhṛtāṅgasya kūrmasaṃjñā vidhīyate .. 25 ..
 
yo viśvaṃ nirdahatyante kālavaiśvānarātmanā .
daivataṃ yasya bhagavān kūrmātmā lokapūjitaḥ .. 26 ..
 
ajahadbhagavacchakti sāmarthyaṃ punareva tat .
anantaṃ savikalpānāṃ yadviśvāṅkuramavyayam .. 27 ..
 
nayatyūrdhvaṃ yathā kūrmo grīvāṃ svātmani saṃvṛ tām .
śeṣākyaphaṇidaivatyaṃ tadanantaṃ hi gīyate .. 28 ..
 
āśrayaṃ bījabhūtānāṃ caturṇāṃ yanmahāmate .
tadgandhaviṭapastasmādvyaktimabyeti pūrvavat .. 29 ..
 
bhūrātmā bhagavān yasminnabhimānākhyadevatā .
phalaṃ rasātmakaṃ tasmādvyajyatyamṛtalakṣaṇam .. 30 ..
 
yasyābhimānikaṃ rūpaṃ kṣīrārṇavamanaśvaram .
tasmādanantaratnotthakāntiṃ kamalamabjaja .. 31 ..
 
vyaktaṃ yasya ca vai śaktirnityā dahanalakṣaṇā .
tadanantadalaṃ viddhi divyaṃ vikasitaṃ sitam .. 32 ..
 
parapūrveṇa bhedena ekadvitriguṇātmanā .
sthitā buddhirvikāraistu saha cāṣṭābhirabjaja .. 33 ..
 
yatrādhidevatātvena vāgvikārā ṛgādayaḥ .
tathā kālavikārā ye catvāraḥ kṛtapūrvakāḥ .. 34 ..
 
tatra rūpaṃ hi sarveṣāṃ sattāmātraṃ paraṃ smṛtam .
vyaktikāraṇadhānābhiḥ sāṅgābhiraparaṃ tu tat .. 35 ..
 
tṛtīyamabhimānākyadevatādehalakṣaṇam .
tasmādvai vāyudaivatyaṃ sparśatanmātrameva ca .. 36 ..
 
jātā yasya sphuṭā vyaktirnānācakrāṅgalakṣaṇā .
tasmādākāśadaivatyaṃ śabdamutpannamabjaja .. 37 ..
 
sarvāṅgasaṃhṛtā cakravyaktiryasyāmalaṃ vapuḥ .
gīyate vyomavṛttaṃ tat pradhānakamalālayam .. 38 ..
 
yasyāntasthāni bhūtāni yasmin sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam .
yasmādunmeṣapūrvaṃ hi mahatpralayapaścimam .. 39 ..
 
pravartate kālatānaṃ bhedakṛt sarvavastuṣu .
vāṅbhātreṇaiva bhinnasya abhinnasyaiva tatvataḥ .. 40 ..
 
jñānādiguṇabṛndasya brahnaṇaścaturātmanaḥ .
nityoditatvānnityatvādvyāpakatvāt paraṃ padam .. 41 ..
 
pūrṇatvāt ṣaḍguṇatvācca na kālo labdhagocaraḥ .
śabdādādityadaivatyamahaṅkāraṃ mahāmate .. 42 ..
 
manaśca candradaivatyamahaṅkārādabhūttataḥ .
buddhiḥ prakāśadaivatyā vyaktānandātmano vibhoḥ .. 43 ..
 
daḷādikarṇikāntāyāḥ sūryapūrvādikalpanā .
pradhānakamalasyaiṣā mūrtirguṇamayī smṛtā .. 44 ..
 
buddhyādīnāṃ ca tatvānāṃ kāraṇaṃ yadanaśvaram .
avyaktākhyaṃ mahābuddhe hyabhinnaguṇamūrtibhṛt .. 45 ..
 
svaguṇānadharīkṛtya svapratiṣṭhaṃ pravartate .
adyātmalakṣaṇāvṛttiḥ sarvāḥ saṃhṛtya vai hṛdi .. 46 ..
 
utpadyante hi caitasmādbhāvāḥ sarve dvijottama .
vipadyante'tra vai bhūyastasmātpajhaṃ paraṃ tvidam .. 47 ..
 
cidādityakalājālaṃ grāhyagrāhakalakṣaṇam .
saṃkrāntaṃ yatra svaṃ dhāma svasāmarthyaṃ ca vetyapi .. 48 ..
 
vimalākhyā vimalatā jñānaśakti rjñatābjaja .
prabhvyākhyā prabhutā caiva satyasaṃjñā ca satyatā .. 49 ..
 
nityākhyā nityatā caiva prakāśākhyā prakāśatā .
anantatā hyanantākhyā kalā kamalasaṃbhava .. 50 ..
 
sahānugrahaśaktyā vai jñeyā'nugrahatā parā .
dvicatuṣkaṃ kalānāṃ yat svapratiṣṭhaṃ hi vartate .. 51 ..
 
saṃvartate paraṃ caiva punareva nivartate .
parāparavibhāgena kalāstvetāścidātmanaḥ .. 52 ..
 
proktāḥ kamalasaṃbhūta yāsāmānantyamuttamam .
yathākrameṇa sarveṣāṃ dhyānamākarṇayāmalam .. 53 ..
 
śānatmujjhitaceṣṭaṃ ca sitamantarmukhaṃ sthitam .
ādheyolliṅgitākāramādhārākhyaṃ smaret prabhum .. 54 ..
 
kūrmamudrānvitaṃ kūrmavaktraṃ niṣṭhaptarukmabham .
śahkhapajhadharaṃ kūrmaṃ svastikena sthitaṃ smaret .. 55 ..
 
muñcantamaniśaṃ tejo dehādbhīṣaṇamutkaṭam .
tiryagūrdhvaṃ ca dhātāraṃ jvālājālamivoccvalam .. 56 ..
 
anantaśaśisaṃkāśamanantamatha saṃsmaret .
sahasraphaṇamālāḍhyaṃ sahasrabhujabhūṣitam .. 57 ..
 
svapāṇisaṃpuṭenaiva śobhayan svāntabhūsthalam .
sitāravindaśaṅkhākṣasūtracakrakarānvitam .. 58 ..
 
patanāśaṅkibuddhervai vitrastamanasastu ca .
mā bhairityabhayaṃ yacchannābrahnabhavanasya ca .. 59 ..
 
niḥśeṣaratnahemāṅgāṃ prābṛṭchriyamivoccvalām .
pajhāsanenopaviṣṭāṃ dhyāyet pajhāñjaliṃ dharām .. 60 ..
 
phullakundāvadātaṃ ca sitasnigdhajaṭādharam .
dhmāyamānaṃ sitaṃ śaṅkhaṃ muktādāmairalaṅkṛtam .. 61 ..
 
vistīrṇasarvāvayavaṃ vikṣiptorudvayaṃ sthitam .
vikṣiptajānupādaṃ ca saṃsmartavyaṃ payonidhim .. 62 ..
 
supavkāmraphalaśyāmapāṇipādatalojjvalam .
raktākṣaṃ ca tathā viprakīrṇakeśaṃ smitānanam .. 63 ..
 
pajhāsanenopaviṣṭamalimālāśatākulam .
pajhamudrānvitaṃ pajhaṃ sudīrghacaraṇaṃ smaret .. 64 ..
 
tuhinācchopalasvacchamuktāphalaśaśiprabhāḥ .
mṛgendraskandhavadanā dharmajñānādayaścatuḥ .. 65 ..
 
pajharāgapravālāgnisaddāḍimaphalojjvalāḥ .
antardayoparaktāśca rājarājeśvaropamāḥ .. 66 ..
 
dviraṣṭavarṣavadviddhi catvāro 'dharmapūrvakāḥ .
hemacampakakhadyotaharitāladalojjvalāḥ .. 67 ..
 
vājivaktrāḥ smṛtā vedāḥ saṃpūrṇanaralakṣaṇāḥ .
evaṃ vṛṣendravadanā yugā brahnan kṛtādayaḥ .. 68 ..
 
supavkāmrātasīpuṣpanīlābjaśukasannibhāḥ .
sarve sadvastrasatpuṣpasadalaṅkaraṇānvitāḥ .. 69 ..
 
śaṅkhapajhadharāḥ sarve varābhayakarāstu vai .
ādheyacakravinyastamastakā svātmasiddhaye .. 70 ..
 
samarpitāntaḥkaraṇāḥ parasmin mantrakāraṇe .
yugāntārkāgnisaṅkāśasvagomaṇḍalamadhyagam .. 71 ..
 
svamudrānvitapāṇiṃ ca valgantaṃ hetirāṭ smaret .
cintyamavyaktapajhaṃ ca himahemāgnibhāsvaram .. 72 ..
 
śāntamaṣṭabhujaṃ saumyaṃ saṃsthitaṃ svastikena tu .
sphaṭikopalakāntiṃ ca ciddhanaṃ dhruvamavyayam .. 73 ..
 
sarvaśaktinidhiṃ dhyāyedamūrtaṃ citprabhākaram .
sarve svavibhavāntasthāstatrādhārātmano vibhoḥ .. 74 ..
 
svasattābhāsitaṃ satvaṃ guṇasatvādvilakṣaṇam .
vibhavaṃ viddhi viprendra jvālaughaṃ kacchapātmanaḥ .. 75 ..
 
svabhogaṃ nāganāthasya bhūḥ kṣiteḥ kāñcanī tathā .
āsāramāmṛtaṃ divyaṃ vīcyoghaistu samanvitam .. 76 ..
 
kṣīrodakīyavibhavaṃ parijñeyamanaśvaram .
bījakośaṃ sakiñjalkaṃ kamalasya dalānvitam .. 77 ..
 
dharmādyasya catuṣkasya sadvivekaṃ sunirmalam .
dvi dvikasyā dharmāderavidyāvibhavaṃ mahat .. 78 ..
 
vākprapañcamaheyaṃ yat tadṛgādigaṇasya ca .
vibhavaṃ ca kṛtādīnāṃ mahatkalpāntamātruṭeḥ .. 79 ..
 
cakrasya vibhavaṃ viddhi bhramaṃ māyāśrayaṃ hi yat .
gauṇīvṛttirameyā yā vibhavaṃ prākṛtaṃ hi tam .. 80 ..
 
vimalādikalājālaṃ pauruṣaṃ vibhavaṃ smṛtam .
vibhormantrātmanascedamaśeṣamamarārcitam .. 81 ..
 
āmahanmantranāthebyo nānāmantragaṇaṃ hi yat .
svaśaktinicayopetaṃ tadviṣṇoḥ paramātmanaḥ .. 82 ..
 
vibhavaṃ kamalodbhūta jñātvaivaṃ saṃyajet sadā .
śabdavyaktistadūrdhve tu sthitārkendvagnilakṣaṇā .. 83 ..
 
tridīptibhāsvarā nāḍī tvavyaktadhvanivigrahā .
vyaktacakratrayasyordhve vartate yā mahāmate .. 84 ..
 
niḥsṛtā brahnarandhreṇa gatā sūryapathāt param .
vāyudvāreṇa pātālaṃ bhitvā yātā svagocaram .. 85 ..
 
saṅkalpaviṣayaḥ sarvastadbaddhaḥ pratitiṣṭhati .
sūtre maṇigaṇo yadvanmadhyanāḍī hyataḥ smṛtā .. 86 ..
 
lakṣyasthāne tu pūrvokte tasyāmabhyantare tu vai .
saṃpuṭe śaśisūryākhye nimeṣonmeṣalakṣaṇe .. 87 ..
 
tatrābjaṃ cārkamālambya parā vāgbhramarī sthitā .
yā sarvamantrajananī śaktiḥ śāntātmano vibhoḥ .. 88 ..
 
nadantī varṇajaṃ nādaṃ śabdavrahneti yaḥ smṛtaḥ .
akārapūrvo hāntaśca dhārā santānarūpadhṛk .. 89 ..
 
nādāvasānagagane devo'nantaḥ sanātanaḥ .
varadābhayadenaiva śaṅkacakrāhkitena tu .. 90 ..
 
trailokyadhṛtidakṣeṇa yuktaḥ pāṇidvayena tu .
śāntaḥ saṃvitsvarūpastu bhaktānugrahakāmyayā .. 91 ..
 
anaupamyena vapuṣā hyamūrto mūrtatāṃ gataḥ .
tasmādāvāhanaṃ kuryādyathā tadavadhāraya .. 92 ..
 
svaśaktyādhiṣṭhitaṃ kṛtvā svasvabhāvasvabhāvayā .
grāhyagrāhakarūpāyā evamavyaktapuṣkaram .. 93 ..
 
samāste kevalaṃ śuddhamīṣatkālalavaṃ dvija .
sāmānyacinmayo bhūtvā sāṃprataṃ śaktayaḥ kalāḥ .. 94 ..
 
asmitā lakṣaṇaṃ dharmaṃ svakaṃ samyaṅnirasya ca .
mavartate tannirāsāt ānandamatulaṃ dvija .. 95 ..
 
svaprakāśamanaupamyaṃ tamicchenmantramavyayam .
paricchedyāṃ digādyaistu prakāśākāśavartinīm .. 96 ..
 
kṛtvāśritya kalāmūrtiṃ samanantaramabjaja .
vihāyomadhyadeśaṃ ca prakāśagahanāttataḥ .. 97 ..
 
dhṛtiśaktyāsane sve'tha upaviśya yathāsukham .
vidyādehena sūkṣmeṇa bhūtadehānukāriṇā .. 98 ..
 
athānandakadambaṃ tadyatsvarūpaṃpṛthak sthitam .
rañjayecchāstradṛṣṭena vyavahāragatena ca .. 99 ..
 
svakenālambanenaiva devatālakṣaṇena ca .
maṇiryathā vibhāgena nīlapītādibhiryutaḥ .. 100 ..
 
rūpabhedamavāpnoti dhyānabhedāttathā vibhuḥ .
evaṃ pravartate samyaṅbhantrarūpaṃ parātmakam .. 101 ..
 
hṛtpuṇḍarīkamadhyasthaṃ caitanyajyotiravyayam .
kadambagolakākāraṃ viśvarūpaṃ maṇiprabham .. 102 ..
 
ratnadīpasamākāramacchinnaprasaraṃ mahat .
śrotrapūrvaiḥ kharandhraistu raśmayastasya nirgatāḥ .. 103 ..
 
chedrapūrṇādyathā kumbhānmahādīpayutāddvija .
yāti bhāsāṃ gaṇo bāhye śarīrādevameva hi .. 104 ..
 
māntro raśmisamūhastu nāḍībhiḥ prasaredvahiḥ .
apratyakṣaḥ sadākṣāṇāṃ mantrātmā yadyapi dvija .. 105 ..
 
tathā'pyanena nyāyena pratyakṣamupalabhyate .
bahiḥ sthitaṃ yadbhūtānāṃ kṣmādīnāṃ guṇapañcakam .. 106 ..
 
tena taccopalabdhavyaṃ pratyakṣeṇa parokṣakam .
tasya bhaumo guṇasthairyaṃ tadguṇena hi sā sthirā .. 107 ..
 
parasparānubhāvena saṃvittau tadupāruhet .
āhlādo yastadīyo hi sa toye copalabhyate .. 108 ..
 
tauyo guṇastu tasyāsti kathaṃ syādanyathā mune .
smṛtamātreṇa mantreṇa āhalādo manaso mahān .. 109 ..
 
rūpātmanā pariṇataḥ sa cāgnau pārameśvaraḥ .
yo rūpākhyo guṇaścāgneḥ sa mantrātmani tiṣṭhati .. 110 ..
 
tejo vinā yato dyānaṃ kutracinnopapadyate .
sparśadharmo hi yo vāyoḥ sa tadīyo mahāmune .. 111 ..
 
yo vāyavyo guṇaḥ sūkṣmaḥ sa ca mantratanau sthitaḥ .
sa cāntaḥkaraṇenaiva saṃyame syāttadutthitaḥ .. 112 ..
 
yadākāśasya śūnyatvamasti tat syāttadudbhavam .
sa mantrātmani saṃśliṣṭo guṇo hyasti mahāmate .. 113 ..
 
agrāhyatvācca karaṇaiḥ prākṛtairbhāvanāṃ vinā .
ityevaṃ mantrasāmarthyaṃ purā jñātvā yathārthataḥ .. 114 ..
 
sannidhānaṃ bhavedyena pūjākāle hyupasthite .
tasminnaṅgāni vinyasya prāk saṃpūrṇaguṇāni ca .. 115 ..
 
svamantrairarcayedeva sthānabhedaṃ vinā tataḥ .
tasmin kadambakusumasadṛśe mantragolake .. 116 ..
 
dvādaśākṣaramantreṇa abhinnena tu sāṃpratam .
vyaktimāpadyate tasmāddhyeyā hṛtpajhamadhyagā .. 117 ..
 
yā parā prakṛtirvāṇī cidrapā nirmalātmikā .
pūritādhyakṣabhāvena niṣkalena mahātmanā .. 118 ..
 
śarīramiva jīvena sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ dvilakṣaṇam .
mūlamantrāditaḥ prāgvat sarvamantragaṇasya ca .. 119 ..
 
karanyāsaṃ vinā dehe nyāsaṃ tasya ca saṃsmaret .
sṛṣṭisaṃsthitisaṃhāranyāsaṃ cāpi tathā'caret .. 120 ..
 
tataḥ khābjakhamadhyāttvapyūrdhvasthāt saṃsmareccyutām .
gaṅgāṃ bhagavato mūrdhni tenāmṛtajalena tu .. 121 ..
 
arghyādyakhilabhogānāṃ kāryā vai śubhakalpanā .
yaṃ yaṃ saṃkalpayedbhogaṃ taṃ taṃ bhāvyasudhāmayam .. 122 ..
 
patantamambarādvegādamṛtāṃśupariplutam .
sākṣādamṛtarūpaistu taistairamṛtasaṃbhavaiḥ .. 123 ..
 
bṛṃhitaṃ muditaṃ magnaṃ mantrarāṭ smaret .
tatastu devadevasya ardhyaṃ datvā yathāvidhi .. 124 ..
 
sannidhiṃ sannirodhaṃ ca sāṃmukhyaṃ ca samācaret .
hṛdayādīni cāṅgāni lāñchanaṃ kamalādikam .. 125 ..
 
bhūṣaṇaṃ ca kirīṭādyaṃ lakṣmyādyāḥ śaktayastathā .
garuḍo mūrtayo vānyā dehe devasya yāḥ sthitāḥ .. 126 ..
 
vyāpakasya tathātvena sve sve sthāne prabhātmakāḥ .
taddehasaṃsthitāḥ sarve pūjanīyāḥ krameṇa tu .. 127 ..
 
parivāraṃ vinā mantraiḥ svaiḥ svairarghyādibhirdvija .
layayāgo hyayaṃ vipra hṛdādiṣvanukīrtitaḥ .. 128 ..
 
tasmāddhatkarṇikādhāre mūrtau vā yatra kutracit .
mūlamantraśarīrasthaṃ parivāraṃ yajet sadā .. 129 ..
 
yāga eṣa layākhyastu saṃkṣiptaḥ sarvasiddhidaḥ .
mantrarāṭ karṇikāmadhye lakṣmyādyāḥ kesarādiṣu .. 130 ..
 
sākārāḥ kevalāḥ sarve yatra bhogābhidhaḥ sa tu .
kevalena ca yāgena pṛthagbhūtena nārada .. 131 ..
 
pūjanaṃ kamalādīnāmadhikārābhidhaḥ sa tu .
evaṃ kṛtvā layākhyaṃ tu yāgaṃ bhogābhidhaṃ tathā .. 132 ..
 
tataḥ kramādyajeddevaṃ bhogairamṛtasaṃbhavaiḥ .
susamastādibhiḥ samyaktāmbūlāntairyathoditaiḥ .. 133 ..
 
sarvaṃ kṛtvā yathāyogaṃ yāvadātmanivedanam .
mānasān jayaśabdāṃśca kṛtvā vijñāpayedidam .. 134 ..
 
svāgataṃ tava deveśa sannidhiṃ bhaja me'cyuta .
gṛhāṇa mānasīṃ pūjā yathārthaparibhāvitām .. 135 ..
 
jñātvā tu suprasannaṃ ta prasādābhimukhaṃ prabhum .
vistareṇa dvijaśreṣṭha mānasaṃ yāgamārabhet .. 136 ..
 
saṃkalpajanitairbhogaiḥ pavitrairakṣayaiḥ śubhaiḥ .
sāṃsparśairaupacārākhyaistathā cābhyavahārikaiḥ .. 137 ..
 
mahadrapaiḥ prabhūtaistu saptalokasamudbhavaiḥ .
yathoditaistu vidhivadutkṛṣṭataralakṣaṇaiḥ .. 138 ..
 
evaṃvidhāṃstu tān bhogān sadbhaktyā vinivedya ca .
samuccaran dhiyā mantraṃ prasannenāntarātmanā .. 139 ..
 
gajāśvadhenuyānāni suvastrālaṅkatāni ca .
nivedyacānta rmānāni grāhayantaṃ smarettataḥ .. 140 ..
 
ātmānaṃ sasutān dārān sarvasvena samāyutān .
nivedya praṇato mūrdhnā ānandāśrusamanvitaḥ .. 141 ..
 
kāmadhenumayīṃ mudrāṃ manasā mantrasaṃyutām .
badhvā saṃcintayedviṣṇoḥ sarvakāmaprapūraṇīm .. 142 ..
 
tato viśeṣayajanaṃ kalpayedacyutasya tu .
sauvarṇapuṣpasaṃpūrṇamañjaliṃ saṃprasārya ca .. 143 ..
 
mūlamantraṃ samuccārya prayatnaiḥ pūrakādikaiḥ .
dīrghaghaṇṭāravaprakhyaṃ yāvattatsaṃbhavāvadhi .. 144 ..
 
sphuradraśmicayākīrṇaṃ vahnyarkenduśataprabham .
dhyātvā nārāyaṇaṃ devamañjalau sannirodhayet .. 145 ..
 
tamañjaliṃ kṣipenmūrdhni tasmin vai mantravigrahe .
ardhyaṃ nivedayedbhūyaḥ punaḥ puṣpāñjaliṃ śubham .. 146 ..
 
mudrāṃ sandarśya mūlākhyāṃ mānasīṃ japamārabhet .
saṃkhyāhīnaṃ yathāśakti ghaṇṭākhyakaraṇena ca .. 147 ..
 
bhogasthānagatānāṃ ca lakṣmyādīnāṃ krameṇa tu .
manasā darśayenmudrāṃ japaṃ kuryāt sakṛt sakṛte .. 148 ..
 
stotramantraiḥ pavitraiśca stutvā samyak prasādayet .
evaṃ krameṇa viprendra kṛtvā yāgaṃ tu mānasam .. 149 ..
 
homaṃ tathāvidhaṃ kuryānmokṣalakṣmīpradaṃ śubham .
nābhicakrāntarasthaṃ tu dhyāyedvahnigṛhaṃ mune .. 150 ..
 
trikoṇaṃ triguṇenaiva avyaktenāvṛtaṃ pari .
dhyānāraṇiṃ tu nirmathya cidagnimavatārya ca .. 151 ..
 
suśuddhaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ dīptaṃ sadaivordhvaśikha dvija .
vāsudevātmakaṃ yasmāt sa vasatyantarātmasu .. 152 ..
 
proccarenmūlamantraṃ tu yāvacchabdasya gocaraḥ .
tatrasthamāhareddivyamāhlādājyāmṛtaṃ param .. 153 ..
 
brahnasarpissamudrādyannistaraṅgāt paricyutam .
gṛhītvā'mṛtamārgeṇa brahyarandhreṇa saṃviśet .. 154 ..
 
hṛdayānmadhya mārgeṇa cinmayena sadīptinā .
prollasantaṃ smarenmantraṃ vrahnaśaktyupabṛṃhitam .. 155 ..
 
svakāraṇāgnau nābhisthe ya ūrdhvendhanavat sthitaḥ .
svabhāvadīptabrahnāgnau paritaścodarojjvalam .. 156 ..
 
smṛtvā yantraṃ tu tanmūrdhni patamānaṃ dvijāmbarāt .
cintayedā mṛtaṃ tvājyaṃ purāvaccāhṛtaṃ dvija .. 157 ..
 
cidagnimevaṃ santarpya nābhau mantrasvarūpiṇam .
jvālāgrāvasthitaṃ caiva bhūyo hṛtpaṅkaje smaret .. 158 ..
 
proccārayaṃśca mantreśaṃ plutaṃ dhyānasamanvitam .
kṛtvaivamekasandhānaṃ sthānadvayagatasya ca .. 159 ..
 
viṇṇormantrasvarūpasya nānāmantrātmakasya ca .
sarvaṃ tu vinyaset paścāttasmin karmakṛtaṃ ca yat .. 160 ..
 
toyapuṣpākṣataiḥ pūrṇaṃ bhāvayeddakṣiṇaṃ karam .
tanmadhye niṣkalaṃ mantraṃ saṃsmaret kiraṇākulam .. 161 ..
 
yāgotthāṃ phalasaṃpattiṃ lakṣmīrūpāṃ vicintya ca .
mūlamantraṃ samuccārya pāṇimadhye tathā smaret .. 162 ..
 
bhūyaśca niṣkalaṃ mantraṃ tasyāmupari bhāvayet .
saśīrṣe jānunī bhūmau kṛtvā viṣṇornivedayet .. 163 ..
 
prasādābhimukhenātha tena taccātmasātkṛtam .
bhāvanīyaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha parituṣṭena cādarāt .. 164 ..
 
nirvṛtte puruṣārthe tu hṛdaye bāhyato'pi vā .
kramānmantragaṇaṃ smṛtvā yātaṃ mantreśvare layam .. 165 ..
 
mantravyaktiṃ svasaṃkalpaśaktāvatha śamaṃ nayet .
saha saṃkalpaśaktyā vai vidyāmūrtiṃ svakāṃ tataḥ .. 166 ..
 
svakalāsu layīkuryāt kalājātaṃ tathā'tmani .
prāgvadānandasandohaparipūrṇaṃ tu jāyate .. 167 ..
 
bahiryajāmīti yadā saṃkalpaṃ manasā kṛtam .
tadā saṃhṛtya tāṃ vyaktimāste madhyāhnasūryavāt .. 168 ..
 
visarjayennataṃ yāvanna kṛtā bāhyataḥ kriyāḥ .
nyasanīyo hyasau yasmānmaṇḍalādiṣu vastu ṣu .. 169 ..
 
sṛṣṭikameṇa saṃhṛtya ādhāraṃ yat puroditam .
jñānināṃ vigalatyeṣa svabhāvāttatvavedinām .. 170 ..
 
niṣkiyāṇāṃ mahābuddhe niṣpannānāṃ svakarmaṇā .
vikāsameti cānyeṣāṃ nityākāraratātmanām .. 171 ..
 
mantrakriyāratānāṃ ca nānātvenā samātmanām .
dhṛtamacyutaśaktyā vai hyaparicyutasattayā .. 172 ..
 
sadvi kalpasvarūpaṃ ca viśvāsanamidaṃ dvija .
vidhṛtaṃ vibhunā vyāptaṃ svasāmarthyena yadyapi .. 173 ..
 
tatrāpi taccharīrāṇāṃ jīvānāṃ tannivāsinām .
svaśaktyānugṛhītānāṃ tamākramya mahāmate .. 174 ..
 
nānāmantrātmanā tvāste tasminnānāvidhātmani .
ityevamuktamādhārasvarūpaṃ hi yathā sthitam .. 175 ..
 
jāyate yatparijñānāt karmiṇāṃ karmasaṃkṣayaḥ .
ayaṃ yo mānaso yāgo jvaravyādhilayāpahaḥ .. 176 ..
 
pāpopasargaśamano bhavābhāvakaro dvija .
satatābhyāsayogena dehapātāt pramocayet .. 177 ..
 
yastvevaṃ parayā bhaktyā sakṛdācarate naraḥ .
kramoditena vidhinā tasya tuṣyāmyahaṃ mune .. 178 ..
 
yājakānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ pradhānatvena vartate .
tārayet svapitṝn sarvān yātāneṣyāṃśca sāmpratam .. 179 ..
 
kiṃ punarnityayukto yastadbhāvagatamānasaḥ .
mantrārādhanamārgasthaḥ śraddhābhaktisamanvitaḥ .. 180 ..
 
na tasya punarāvṛttiḥ sa yāti paramaṃ padam .
jñātvaivaṃ yatnato nityaṃ kuryādyāgaṃ tu mānasam .. 181 ..
 
idaṃ rahasyaṃ paramaṃ mayoktaṃ te'dya nārada .
nāśiṣyāṇāṃ ca vaktavyaṃ nābhaktānāṃ kathaṃcana .. 182 ..
 
atyantabhavabhītānāṃ bhaktānāṃ bhāvitātmanām .
idaṃ rahasyaṃ vaktavyaṃ samyagbhāvaṃ parīkṣya ca .. 183 ..

Chapter - 6
śrīḥ .
ṣaṣṭho'dhyāyaḥ .
purā'nena vidhānena kṛtvā yāgaṃ tu mānasam .
karmaṇā bhaktiyuktena bahirvṛttau yajettataḥ .. 1 ..
 
sanakaḥ .
bhagavaṃstvatprasādena jñāto hyajñānanāśanaḥ .
jñānavijñānasahito hṛdyāgaḥ sarvasiddhidaḥ .. 2 ..
 
kimarthaṃ bāhyataḥ pūjā kāryā vai pratimādiṣu .
etadācakṣva bhagavannatra me saṃśayo mahān .. 3 ..
 
śāṇḍilyaḥ .
bāhyotthā vāsanā vipra bahujanmārjitā dṛḍhā .
lolīkṛto'nayā hyātmā śuddho'śuddhasvarūpayā .. 4 ..
 
yā mantraviṣayā śuddhā kriyāśāntasvarūpadā .
samutthānavināśārthaṃ tasyāḥ saṃparikīrtitā .. 5 ..
 
sa bāhyābhyantarābhyāṃ ca kriyābhyāṃ tanmayo bhavet .
dṛḍhotthavāsanānāṃ ca tānavaṃ syācchanaiḥ śanaiḥ .. 6 ..
 
yanmayaḥ sādhako vipra dehasthaḥ sāṃprataṃ bhavet .
tanmayo dehapātāt syādityetat kathitaṃ mayā .. 7 ..
 
atha bāhyotthayāgasya vidhānamavadhāraya .
devaṃ hṛtkamalākāśe tejorūpatayā sthitam .. 8 ..
 
tasmāt sthānāt samānīya taṃ kuryānnetramadyagam .
vāsudevābhidhānaṃ tu prāguktaṃ ca samāśrayet .. 9 ..
 
tato locanayugmena stabdhena dvijasattama .
japan locanamantraṃ tu avalokyākhilaṃ tu tam .. 10 ..
 
sthāpito ya upārjitya saṃbhāro hyudakādikaḥ .
dhyāyeddakṣiṇapāṇau tu astramādityasannibham .. 11 ..
 
dravyadoṣagaṇaṃ tena dagdhvā tanmantramuccaran .
saṃcintya bhasmabhūtaṃ tu taṃ sarvaṃ dvijasattama .. 12 ..
 
dagdhadoṣamathāpyāyya vāmahasta gatena tu .
hṛdā pūrṇendutulyena amṛtāsāravarṣiṇā .. 13 ..
 
tanmantramuccaran paścāt kāntimantaṃ vicintayet .
dagdhamāpyāyitaṃ sarvamatha caivaṃ samācaret .. 14 ..
 
pracaṇḍakiraṇavrātairbhāskarīyairdahet purā .
saṃcintya bhasmabhūtaṃ taṃ tataḥ pūrṇenduraśmibhiḥ .. 15 ..
 
āpyāyyāmṛtakalloladhārāpātena sattama .
kāntimaccintayedbhūyo yaddagdhaṃ bhānunā tataḥ .. 16 ..
 
badhdvā kāmadughāṃ mudrāṃ sravantīṃ mantrasaṃyutām .
gorūpāṃ himaśailābhāṃ nirādhārapade sthitām .. 17 ..
 
tayā tadamṛtīkuryādbhogajālaṃ yathāsthitam .
nirmalo dravyasaṅghaśca yāgayogyo bhavettadā .. 18 ..
 
gālitenāmbunā pūrṇaṃ svāhṛtenāmbunā saha .
svottare varmaṇā sthāpya kumbhaṃ sarvopayogi yat .. 19 ..
 
upārjitaṃ purā yadvai yāgopakaraṇaṃ mahat .
tat sarvaṃ dakṣiṇe kṛtvā madhye bhadrāsanaṃ nyaset .. 20 ..
 
pratimālakṣaṇādhyāye vakṣyate tasya lakṣaṇam .
yatkiñcit patrapuṣpādyaṃ paridṛśyeta pīṭhagam .. 21 ..
 
pāṇinā tat samāhṛtya śucisthāne nidhāya vai .
gavyairvā cāmarairvālaiḥ śikhipakṣaiḥ kuśairatha .. 22 ..
 
saṃmārjya bhadrapīṭhaṃ tu vāsasā susitena vā .
bahunā vastrapūtena vāriṇā tadanantaram .. 23 ..
 
prakṣālya dvādaśārṇena praṇavādyantagena tu .
evamārādhanādhāraṃ kṣālayitvā ca vāriṇā .. 24 ..
 
tattāvadastrapuṣpeṇa kuryādvighnagaṇojjhitam .
ārādhyo'yamathāropya tatra mantramayīṃ śubhām .. 25 ..
 
sarvopakaraṇopetāṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutām .
pratimāṃ dhātupāṣāṇanirmitāmātmasiddhaye .. 26 ..
 
aṣṭāṅgena namaskṛtya dadyādarghyaṃ tu mūrdhani .
anulepanasaṃyuktaṃ tataḥ puṣpāñjaliṃ śubham .. 27 ..
 
sāṅgaṃ sāvaraṇaṃ bhaktyā pūjayet puruṣottamam .
yadvārghyapādyācamanairdevamabhyarcya vai tataḥ .. 28 ..
 
bhuktamarghyādikaṃ tasmādapanīyābhivādya ca .
samarpya viṣvaksenasya saṃśodhya mṛdunā dvija .. 29 ..
 
uśīravaṃśakūrcena kṣālayedgandhavāriṇā .
uccaran mūlamantraṃ vā kuryānmārgatrayaṃ vibho .. 30 ..
 
sudhaute devadevasya vāsasī paridhāpayet .
citrasthādbhagavadbimbādbhuktapuṣpādikaṃ hi yat .. 31 ..
 
apanīya tu tat kuryādvāsasā reṇumārjanam .
yadvā prāgyāgabhavanapraveśānantaraṃ dvija .. 32 ..
 
nyasya bhadrāsanādyaṃ tadanyadanyat samācaret .
yadvā tadātane kāle nyasya bhadrāsanādikam .. 33 ..
 
ādyaṃ mārgatrayaṃ kṛtvā yathoktavidhinā tataḥ .
yogapīṭhārcanārambhe bimboktaṃ sarvamācare t .. 34 ..
 
athārghyādīni pātrāṇi prakṣālyāstreṇa vāriṇā .
samāpūrya sugandhena jalena hṛdayena tu .. 35 ..
 
dravyāṇi nikṣipetteṣu yathoktakramayogataḥ .
bhadrāsanasya koṇeṣu purato vāsasāstṛte .. 36 ..
 
bhūtale vā'tha pātrāṇi ādhāropari vinyaset .
svapūrvaniyamenaiva udakpaścimakoṇagam .. 37 ..
 
arghyāmbukalaśaṃ nyasya tataḥ prāguttarāntare .
nyasedācamanīyākhyamāgneye snānasaṃjñitam .. 38 ..
 
vinyasya pādyasaṃjñaṃ tu pade dakṣiṇapaścime .
agrato vāpi tanmadye nyasedarghyaṃ dvitīyakam .. 39 ..
 
agnikoṇe tvarghyapātraṃ pādyamaiśānakoṇake .
ācāmaṃ naiṛte bhāge snānārthaṃ vāyave tathā .. 40 ..
 
īśvaraprāgvaśādarghyamāgneyādiṣu koṇake .
mukhyāmukhyārghyapādyādikramāddravyāṇi nikṣipet .. 41 ..
 
candanaṃ śaśibāhlīkadūrvāsiddhārthakāni ca .
sākṣatāni kuśāgraṇi taṇḍulāni tilāni ca .. 42 ..
 
kāñcanaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ ratnāni ca phalāni ca .
kadalīphalapūrvāṇi pradhāne'rghye vinikṣipet .. 43 ..
 
dvitīye dadhimadhvājyakṣīrabinducatuṣṭayam .
kuśāgreṇa sabāhlīkaṃ sapuṣpaṃ tila taṇḍulam .. 44 ..
 
dūrvāṃ ca viṣṇukāntāṃ ca śyāmākaṃ śaṅkhapuṣpakam .
padmakaṃ kundareṇuṃ ca pādyapātre vinikṣipet .. 45 ..
 
elālavaṅgatakkolaiḥ sahajātiphalāni ca .
candanaṃ ca sakarpūraṃ kṣipedācamanīyake .. 46 ..
