vitānairdhvajikābhiśca tuhgairyavanikāpaṭaiḥ .. 60 ..
 
kṣaumairnānāvidhairvastrairghaṇṭācāmaradarpaṇaiḥ .
vyālambidarbhamālābhiḥ kadaḷīpanasādibhiḥ .. 61 ..
 
sugandhapuṣpamālābhiḥ sauvarṇairmañjarīgaṇaiḥ .
saphalaiḥ kadaḷīpūganāḷikerādibhūruhaiḥ .. 62 ..
 
pradīpaiḥ prakaraiḥ puṣpaiḥ sitādyairvarṇakairapi .
toraṇairdvārakuṃbhaiśca savatsaiḥ surabhīgaṇaiḥ .. 63 ..
 
maṇḍitaiḥ khalu śrṛhgādau kṣaumasragbhūṣaṇādibhiḥ .
evamādyairalaṃkṛtya yathāśobhaṃ tu maṇṭapam .. 64 ..
 
tṛtīye vāsare pūrve karmāhāddivasakṣaye .
ṛtvigbhirdeśikendrastu kṛtasandhyāvidhikramaḥ .. 65 ..
 
praviśya maṇṭapaṃ prāgvat puṇyāhoktipurassaram .
arcanaṃ vāsudevasya sahomaṃ prāk samāpya ca .. 66 ..
 
yāgālayaṃ tu sarvatra gavyairabhyukṣya pañcabhiḥ .
dravyāṇi yāgayogyāni tattatsthāne niyojayet .. 67 ..
 
prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvarayāṃ pūrvāhne dehaśuddhaye .
uptaromanakhaśmaśrurbhūpatirniyataḥ śuciḥ .. 68 ..
 
dhautadantaśca susnātaḥ pariśuddhāmbarāvṛtaḥ .
sitālepanapuṣpādyairañcitaḥ saṃsmaran harim .. 69 ..
 
upoṣito ghṛtaṃ prāśya brāhnaṇairvedapāragaiḥ .
pārāyaṇamṛcāṃ śrṛṇvannāsīta sapurohitaḥ .. 70 ..
 
niśāmukhe pravṛtte tu ṛtvigbirdeśikottamaḥ .
praviśedyāgasadanaṃ kṛtvā dvārsthārcanaṃ sudhīḥ .. 71 ..
 
tristhānasthaṃ jagannāthaṃ yajeddīkṣāvidheḥ samam .
puṇyāhaṃ pūrvamuccārya ṛtvigbhiḥ kuṃbhamudvahan .. 72 ..
 
kuṃbhamaṇḍalayoḥ pūjāṃ vistareṇa samāpya ca .
svakuṇḍe havanaṃ kuryāt samidbhiḥ saptabhiḥ purā .. 73 ..
 
śāntihomaṃ tataḥ paścānmadhukṣīrādibhiḥ kramāt .
pratyekaṃ śatasaṅkhyaṃ ca pūrṇāntaṃ mūlamuccaran .. 74 ..
 
svamārgeṇa tu saṃskṛtya guruḥ kuṇḍagaṇaṃ tataḥ .
teṣu prabhavayogena homārthaṃ dikṣu yojayet .. 75 ..
 
caturo vāsudevādināmnā ekāyanān dvijān .
taiḥ svaśākhoditairmantraiḥ hotavyaṃ tu krameṇa tu .. 76 ..
 
ṛgādyāṃścaturo vedān vidikkuṇḍeṣu vinyaset .
mantrairarcitaliṅgaistu svaśākhotthaisca pāvanaiḥ .. 77 ..
 
homaṃ kuryādyathāyogaṃ puṃsūktenaiva vā dvija .
bhūḥ svāheti bhuvaḥ svāhā svaḥ svāheti tathaiva ca .. 78 ..
 
bhūrbhuvassuvaḥsvāheti mantrairvā vahnidkkramāt .
bhūḥ puruṣāya svāhā bhuvaḥ puruṣāya svāhā .. 79 ..
 
svaḥ puruṣāya svāhā bhūrbhuvassvaḥ puruṣāya svāhā .
etaiścaturbhirmantrairvā juhuyāddikkrameṇa tu .. 80 ..
 
sāstrāṇāṃ lokapālānāṃ kumudādigaṇasya ca .
aṣṭānāṃ mahgaḷānāṃ ca prāgvat syāt sthāpanādikam .. 81 ..
 
pālāśādisamidbhedāścarubhedāśca pūrvavat .
pratikuṇḍaṃ ca kuṃbhānāṃ sthāpanādyaṃ tu pūrvavat .. 82 ..
 
caturṇāṃ ṛṅnayādīnāṃ tathā caikāntināmapi .
niveśanādikaṃ kāryaṃ puroditavidhānataḥ .. 83 ..
 
evaṃ krameṇa saṃpādya tadante bhūpatiṃ guruḥ .
prāśayet pañcagavyaṃ tu kuśodakasamanvitam .. 84 ..
 
bhagavatpādatoyaṃ ca sarvapāpaharaṃ śubham .
bhakṣayeccaruśeṣaṃ tu koṣṭhasaṃśodhanāya ca .. 85 ..
 
kṛtvā dakṣiṇapīṭhe tu śālibhāraistu viṣṭaram .
navasaṅkhyaistadūrdhve tu mārgaṃ carma tu vinyaset .. 86 ..
 
vyāghrajaṃ vā tadūrdhve tu darbhānāstīrya sākṣatān .
prāgagrānudagagrān vā tasminnāropya bhūpatim .. 87 ..
 
pūrṇodakuṃbhāṃścaturaḥ prāgvadvastrādibhūṣitān .
caturdikṣvapi saṃsthāpya teṣvarcyā mūrtayaḥ kramāt .. 88 ..
 
caturvidhāni cānnāni tāsāṃ dadyāt krameṇa tu .
tato homaśca kartavyaḥ kuṇḍeṣu prākkrameṇa tu .. 89 ..
 
tato būpasya purataḥ upaviśyāsane guruḥ .
taddehasthitatatvānāṃ śuddhiṃ kuryādvidhānataḥ .. 90 ..
 
prāk teṣāṃ vilayaṃ kṛtvā tataḥ sṛṣṭiṃ samācaret .
kuryāt kautukabandhaṃ ca prāgvattasyāpi cātmanaḥ .. 91 ..
 
svarṇasañcayamāhṛtya tintriṇīmiśravāriṇā .
nirmalīkṛtya saṃprokṣya vīryamantreṇa tatpunaḥ .. 92 ..
 
udak dik saṃsthite pīṭhe śālibhāraistribhiḥ kṛte .
pīṭhe niveśyādhivāsya vāsolaṅkārapūrvakam .. 93 ..
 
anyacca sarvaṃ saṃsthāpya varmaṇā cāvakuṇṭhayet .
tataścakrābjamālikhya tvanyadvā maṇḍalaṃ śubham .. 94 ..
 
ratnajairdhātujairvāpi varṇakaiḥ paripūrayet .
gītanṛttādikaiḥ stotraiḥ śaṅkhavādyādinisvanaiḥ .. 95 ..
 
maṅgaḷairvividhaiścānyairjāgareṇa nayenniśām .
divyādyāyatane kāryaṃ viśeṣayajanaṃ vibhoḥ .. 96 ..
 
tataḥ karmadine brāhne muhūrte deśikaḥ svayam .
kṛtvā snānādikaṃ sarvaṃ nityakarmavidhānataḥ .. 97 ..
 
tato yajedviśeṣeṇa kuṃbhasthaṃ jagatīpatim .
maṇḍalasthaṃ krameṇaiva vividhairbhogasañcayaiḥ .. 98 ..
 
aupacārikasāṃsparśahṛdayaṅgamasaṃjñitaiḥ .
paramānnādikaistatra prabūtairannasañcayaiḥ .. 99 ..
 
evamiṣṭvā tato'gnisthaṃ vibhuṃ santarpayet kramāt .
samitsaptakapūrvaistu mūlena saghṛtaistilaiḥ .. 100 ..
 
sahasramāhutīnāṃ tu śataṃ vā'pi samācaret .
sarvavighnavināśārthamastreṇāpi tathācaret .. 101 ..
 
ṛtvijaśca svakuṇḍeṣu juhuyuḥ pūrvavat kramāt .
patitāsu ca pūrṇāsu sarvakuṇḍeṣu vai kramāt .. 102 ..
 
saṃsnāpya mūlamantreṇa puṃsūktena tathaiva ca .
suprakṣāḷitapāṇyaṃghriṃ svācāntaṃ paribhūṣitam .. 103 ..
 
niśādhivāsitaiḥ sarvairvastramālyānulepanaiḥ .
sarvairābharaṇaiścaiva mahārghairvividhairapi .. 104 ..
 
khaṅgakheṭakahastaṃ ca samādāya guruḥ svayam .
muhūrte śobhane prāpte pāṇinā pṛthivīpatim .. 105 ..
 
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā tu sarvamaṅgaḷasaṃyutam .
kalaśasthaladikkuṃbhasarvakuṇḍeṣu saṃsthitam .. 106 ..
 
vibhuṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya kārayitvā namaskriyām .
brāhnaṇāgryānanujñāpya tulāṃ nītvā pradakṣiṇam .. 107 ..
 
tasyāḥ paścimadiksaṃsthe bhūyaḥ prāgānanaṃ dhaṭe .
āropayenmūlamantraṃ sāṅgamāvartayan guruḥ .. 108 ..
 
divyān balādikān mantrān tathā sūktaṃ tu pauruṣam .
prākpātre bhūpatisamaṃ nikṣipet svarṇasañcayam .. 109 ..
 
niśādhivāsitaṃ tveṣa tulābhāraḥ samo bhavet .
evaṃ vā'pi tulābhāre prāk dhaṭe vinyasennṛpam .. 110 ..
 
pratyaṅmukhaṃ paścime tu nikṣipet svarṇasañcayam .
śataniṣkādhikaḥ śreṣṭho madhyamo'rdhādhiko bhavet .. 111 ..
 
śatapādādhikaḥ sa syāttulābhāraḥ kaniṣṭhakaḥ .
tatkāle ṛṅbhayādyāśca catvāro dikṣu saṃsthitāḥ .. 112 ..
 
svaśākhāḥ samadhīyīran vidiśāsu ca saṃsthitāḥ .
sadbrahnajñā adhīrayan śākhāḥ paramapāvanāḥ .. 113 ..
 
śaṅkhakāhaḷabheryādivādyāni vividhāni ca .
vādayeyuḥ samantācca tattadvādyaviśāradāḥ .. 114 ..
 
gītaṃ tu vividhaṃ kuryuḥ gītaśāstraviśāradāḥ .
vividhāni ca nṛttāni kuryuśca parito diśaḥ .. 115 ..
 
anyacca maṅgaḷaṃ yadyata tattat sarvaṃ tu kārayet .
tatastu sarvakuṇḍeṣu śāntihomaṃ ca kārayet .. 116 ..
 
tilairājyaiśca bahubhiḥ śatamaṣṭottaraṃ kramāt .
bhūpatirmanasā dhyāyet bhagavantaṃ janārdanam .. 117 ..
 
ekanāḍīṃ tadardhaṃ vā āsīta nṛpatirdhaṭe .
tato'varuhya vai tasmāt praṇameddaṇḍavaddharim .. 118 ..
 
tatastu bhūṣaṇairvastrairbhūṣayedbhūpatirgurum .
suvarṇadakṣiṇāṃ dadyācchataniṣkāṃ tu tatsamām .. 119 ..
 
ṛtvigbhyastu tadardhaṃ vā ye cānye tatra karmaṇi .
niyojitāstu sāhāyye tebhyaḥ karmānurūpataḥ .. 120 ..
 
dravyāṇi dadyānnṛpatirvastrāṇi vividhāni ca .
suvarṇasañcayāṃstāṃśca bhūṣaṇāni ca bhūpatiḥ .. 121 ..
 
svayaṃ vyaktādike sthāne dadyādbhagavato vibhoḥ .
dānāt phalaviśeṣaṃ tu samākarṇaya sāṃpratam .. 122 ..
 
svayaṃ vyakte vibhoḥ sthāne yo dadyādbhūpatirhareḥ .
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sarvāmayaviyojitaḥ .. 123 ..
 
sarvasaṃpatsamṛddhaśca sarvadeśādhipo bhavet .
bhuṅkte ca vividhān bhogāniha loke paratra ca .. 124 ..
 
koṭikoṭiguṇaṃ dānaṃ tathaiva ca phalaṃ bhavet .
dānaṃ yaddivyāyatane tadanantaguṇaṃ bhavet .. 125 ..
 
ārṣe ca saiddhāyatane dānaṃ lakṣaguṇaṃ bhavet .
sadviprakalpite dānaṃ sahasraguṇitaṃ bhavet .. 126 ..
 
satkṣatrakalpite sthāne dānaṃ śataguṇaṃ bhavet .
sadvaiśyakalpite sthāne tadardhaguṇitaṃ bhavet .. 127 ..
 
sacchūdrakalpite dattaṃ dviṣaṭkaguṇitaṃ bhavet .
ananyaśaraṇairvarṇaiḥ sthāne tu parikalpite .. 128 ..
 
dānaṃ daśaguṇaṃ proktaṃ varṇairvyāmiśrayājibhiḥ .
nirmitāyatane dattaṃ tat pañcaguṇitaṃ bhavet .. 129 ..
 
dāne mukhyavidhiḥ proktastvanukalpamataḥ śrṛṇu .
tatra ye śrotriyāḥ prāptā vaighṇavā brāhnaṇottamāḥ .. 130 ..
 
suvarṇasañcayādyaṃ ca tebhyo dadyādyathākramam .
yāgopakaraṇaṃ sarvamācāryāya pradāpayet .. 131 ..
 
yaḥ kuryādbhūpatiḥ kaścit anyo vā dhanavān sakṛt .
tulābhārāhvayaṃ karma sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate .. 132 ..
 
rogairanabibhūtaśca bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ .
yaḥ kuryānniyamenaiva karmaitat prativatsaram .. 133 ..
 
tasya puṇyaphalāvāptiṃ kaḥ śaknotyabhivarṇitum .
tatkāle bhagavadyāgaṃ catuḥsthānārcanānvitam .. 134 ..
 
divyādyāyatane samyak kārayet pṛthivīpatiḥ .
tadanyasmin dine vipra snāpayet puruṣottamam .. 135 ..
 
sahasrakalaśaiḥ samyak puroditavidhānataḥ .
yadvānyasnapanenaiva tattatkālocitena vai .. 136 ..
 
catusaḥthānārcanaṃ tatra viśeṣāt kārayennṛpaḥ .
mahāhavirnivedyaṃ ca viśeṣeṇaiva kārayet .. 137 ..
 
tatrāpi deśikādibhyo dadyādvai dakṣiṇāṃ kramāt .
dīnāndhakṛpaṇānāthān bālavṛddhakṛśāturān .. 138 ..
 
bhojayecca vidhānena dravyādīnyapi dāpayet .
vividhāni ca bījāni śālyādīnyapi dāpayet .. 139 ..
 
bandīkṛtāṃśca visṛjet kārāgṛhaniveśitān .
eṣa te kathito vipra tulābhāravidhiḥ kramāt .. 140 ..
 
hiraṇyagarbhādyanyeṣvapyevameva samācaret .
evaṃ kuryāttulābhāraṃ yaḥ sakṛdbahuśo'pi vā .. 141 ..
 
sarvapāpavimokṣastu tasya syānnātra saṃśayaḥ .
yo vā bhagavato'rthe tu mātāpitrorgurostu vā .. 142 ..
 
svaprāṇāṃstyajatāṃ bhaktyā viprādīnāṃ mahāmate .
nimittī tu bhavettasya tulābhārādikena ca .. 143 ..
 
bahuśo'nuṣṭhitenaiva samyageva tu karmaṇā .
anyairvā vihitairvipra prāyaścittaiḥ suduṣkaraiḥ .. 144 ..
 
brahnahatyo'tthadoṣasya śuddhirbhavati vā na vā .
prāṇatyāgaḥ kṛtastena viṣvarṇthe yanmahātmanā .. 145 ..
 
tasmānna niṣkṛtirvipra bhavettasya nimittinaḥ .
brāhnaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyā viṣṇvarthe maudgalāstu vā .. 146 ..
 
parityajeyuḥ svaprāṇān bhagavadbhaktisaṃyutāḥ .
bhṛgvādibhirupāyaistu pañcabhirvā viṣādikaiḥ .. 147 ..
 
anyaisteṣāṃ bhavet sadyau vājapeyādijaṃ phalam .
sakāmasya tu niṣkāmaḥ prāpnuyāt paramāṃ gatim .. 148 ..
 
mahātmanastu tān viddhi viṣṇvarthe tyaktajīvitān .
ātmahatyotthadoṣaiste na lipyante kadācana .. 149 ..
 
ātmahatyotthadoṣāḥ syuranyeṣāṃ sarvadā dvija .
evaṃ bhagavadarthe tu prāṇatyāge kṛtādaraḥ .. 150 ..
 
yamuddiśya tyajet prāṇān taṃ vidyādbrahnaghātakam .
mukhyavipre mṛte tasya taddoṣaḥ syāccaturguṇaḥ .. 151 ..
 
kṣatriye brahnahatyotthadoṣastu triguṇo bhavet .
nimittinaḥ sa doṣaḥ syāddviguṇaḥ saṃsthite viśi .. 152 ..
 
nimittine mṛte śūdre doṣa ekaguṇo bhavet .
evaṃ doṣavivṛddhistu bhavedvipre nimittini .. 153 ..
 
nimittini kṣatriyādāvekaikaguṇavardhanāt .
bhavet pūrvoktadoṣastu atārthe nāsti saṃśayaḥ .. 154 ..
 
evaṃ mṛte vipramātre doṣa ukto nimittinaḥ .
mukhyadoṣaḥ pañcaguṇo brahnacāriṇi saṃsthite .. 155 ..
 
gṛhasthe yajvani mṛte sa doṣaḥ ṣaḍguṇo bhavet .
vānaprasthe mṛte mukhyadoṣaḥ saptaguṇo bhavet .. 156 ..
 
sannyāsāśramaniṣṭhe tu saṃsthite tu nimittinaḥ .
syānmukhyadoṣo'ṣṭaguṇa evaṃ tu kathito mune .. 157 ..
 
nimittino doṣavṛddhiḥ viṣṇvarthe maraṇe sati .
evaṃ nimittabhūtānāṃ dvijādīnāṃ na niṣkṛtiḥ .. 158 ..
 
tatra yat brāhnaṇairuktaṃ vivekanirataissadā .
sarvaśāstrārthatatvajñaiḥ tat kuryādavicārataḥ .. 159 ..

Chapter - 21
śrīḥ .
ekoviṃśā'yoyaḥ .
śāṇḍilyaḥ .
mune hiraṇyagarbhādau viśeṣo vakṣyate'dhunā .
hemagarbhavidhānaṃ tu prathamaṃ kathyate mayā .. 1 ..
 
sanakaḥ .
yadyadatrocyate karma tulābhāre'pi noditam .
sādhāraṇaṃ bhavettattat sarveṣāmapi kramaṇām .. 2 ..
 
tulābhārādikānāṃ tu vibhavādyānuguṇyataḥ .
prāgvanmaṇṭapanirmāṇaṃ pīṭhādiparikalpanam .. 3 ..
 
pratiṣṭhoditamārgeṇa kuryādvā maṇṭapādikam .
yadvāṣṭasaptaṣaṭpañcacatustrikaravistṛtam .. 4 ..
 
triṃśadaṅagulamānaṃ tu golakaikaikahānitaḥ .
unnataṃ madhyapīṭhaṃ syāt tattatkṣetrānusārataḥ .. 5 ..
 
caturhastaṃ samārabhya ṣaṭṣaṭgolakahānitaḥ .
vistṛtaṃ pārśvayoḥ pīṭhadvitayaṃ parikalpayet .. 6 ..
 
viṃśatyaṃgulamānācca dvidvikāṃgulahānitaḥ .
tadunnatiryathā sā'ntye sārdhahaste daśāṃgulā .. 7 ..
 
dvayoktamānādardhaṃ vā bhavet sarvatra connatiḥ .
pīṭhānāmantarāḷaṃ tu kalpayet karasaṃmitam .. 8 ..
 
karārdhaṃ vardhayedvāpi bhavedyāvaccatuṣkaram .
antarāḷaṃ bhavettāvadyathā vā nātisaṅkaṭam .. 9 ..
 
yathoditeṣu māneṣu yathābhimatamānataḥ .
kuryāt kuṇḍagaṇaṃ cāpi lakṣaṇenopalakṣitam .. 10 ..
 
āsthānamaṇṭapādye tu yathaitat kalpayettadā .
madhyapīṭhoditaṃ karma tatrade vāsane bhavet .. 11 ..
 
tadudak dakṣayoḥ pīṭhadvayamuktapramāṇataḥ .
prākdikkuṇḍasya vai prācyāṃ pīṭhaṃ kuryāt smaṃ śubham .. 12 ..
 
saptaṣaṭpañcahastaṃ vā catustridvikaraṃ tu vā .
ekahastocchritaṃ vā'pi tadardhocchritameva vā .. 13 ..
 
tasyopariṣṭāt kartavyaṃ hemagarbhaniveśanam .
tulābhāroditaṃ karma pīṭhoparyathavā caret .. 14 ..
 
yadvā kuṃbhādiyajanaṃ adhivāsanakarma ca .
maṇṭape kalpayitvā tatprapāyāṃ vā samācaret .. 15 ..
 
hemagarbhaniveśaṃ tu prapāyāṃ vā samācaret .
kuṃbhayāgādikaṃ rūpaṃ karturicchānurūpataḥ .. 16 ..
 
tulābhārādike'nyasmin dinepyevaṃ samācaret .
tataḥ kuryācca sauvarṇamekāṃgulaghanaṃ dṛḍham .. 17 ..
 
adhaḥ pātraṃ cordhvapātraṃ yathāsaṅgatayostayoḥ .
sukhāsanaṃ syānnṛpatervistṛtaṃ kalpayettathā .. 18 ..
 
adhaḥ pātraṃ suvarṇaānāṃ sahasreṇa palena vā .
yadvā niṣkasahasreṇa tadardhenordhvapātrakam .. 19 ..
 
evaṃ pātradvayaṃ kuryāt sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam .
vibhave sarvapātrāṇi kuryāddhemamayāni ca .. 20 ..
 
adhivāsadinoktaṃ tu tulābhāravadācaret .
pātradvayasyodak pīṭhe hyadhivāsaṃ samācaret .. 21 ..
 
tataḥ karmadinoktaṃ tu prāgvat kṛtvā krameṇa tu .
indradikkalpite pīṭhe bhārairdvādaśabhirmune .. 22 ..
 
śālīnāṃ viṣṭaraṃ kṛtvā tabūrdhve taṇḍulān nyaset .
tadardhamānāṃstasyordhve tadardhāṃstu tilān nyaset .. 23 ..
 
śālibhiḥ samabhārān vā taṇḍulāṃśca tilān nyaset .
adhivāsepyevameva bhavedvittānusārataḥ .. 24 ..
 
evameva bhavedvāpi tulābhārādikarmaṇi .
mārgaṃ vā vyāghrajaṃ carma śālyāderantarāntarā .. 25 ..
 
vinyasennavavastraṃ vā vibhave tritayaṃ tu vā .
anyacca maṅgaḷaṃ kuryādvastraveṣṭanapūrvakam .. 26 ..
 
adhaḥ pātraṃ tadūrdhve tu nyaset prāgadhivāsitam .
muhūrte śobhane prāpte gṛhītvā bhūpatiṃ guruḥ .. 27 ..
 
susnātaṃ bhūṣitaṃ prāgvadvastramālyādibhūṣaṇaiḥ .
mahārghairvividhaiścāpi khaḍgakheṭakavarjitam .. 28 ..
 
prāgvattatvopasaṃhāraṃ kṛtvā jīvāvaśeṣitam .
saṅkhatūryaninādādyaiḥ sahacātra niveśayet .. 29 ..
 
adhasthe prāṅmukhaṃ yadvā vinyaset pratyagānanam .
varmaṇā vinyasedūrdhve hyūrdhvapātramadhomukham .. 30 ..
 
tadaṇḍāntaḥ samāsīne tasmiṃstasyāgrato guruḥ .
upaviśyāsane prāgvat tatvotpattiṃ samācaret .. 31 ..
 
aṇḍājjātaṃ tu taṃ smṛtvā tatastasmāttu bhūpatim .
snānapīṭhe samāveśya maṅgaḷadravyavāsitaiḥ .. 32 ..
 
navabhiḥ pañcabhirvāpi kuṃbhairudakapūritaiḥ .
vastrādiveṣṭitaiḥ kuryādabhūpaterabhiṣecanam .. 33 ..
 
kalpayet prokṣaṇaṃ vā'pi ṛtvigbhiḥ saha deśikaḥ .
kṛtvā tatastaṃ khācāntaṃ bhūṣaṇādivibhūṣitam .. 34 ..
 
praṇāmaṃ kārayedbhūyo bhūyo bhagavato vibhoḥ .
jātakarmādisaṃskāraṃ jātārthaṃ juhuyāt kramāt .. 35 ..
 
tilairājyaiśca bahubhiḥ sarvasaṃpūraṇāya ca .
sarvadoṣavināśāya tataḥ pūrṇāṃ ca pātayet .. 36 ..
 
bhūṣaṇāni ca te pātre nṛpo dadyāddharervibhoḥ .
dānāt phalaṃ ca pūrvoktaṃ vibhorāyatane sadā .. 37 ..
 
svayaṃvyaktādike kuryāttulābhārādi karma ca .
tadā'pi bhūpasya phalaṃ bhaveddānoditaṃ kramāt .. 38 ..
 
anukalpe tadardhaṃ tu dadyādbhagavato vibhoḥ .
ardhaṃ dadyādbāhnaṇemyo tulābhāre tathaiva ca .. 39 ..
 
tulābhārāhvayaṃ karma hemagarbhābhidhaṃ ca yat .
etaddvayaṃ tu mukhyaṃ syāt sarveṣāmapi karmaṇām .. 40 ..
 
krameṇa vakṣyamāṇānāṃ tilaparvatapūrvakam .
anyattu sakalaṃ karma tulābhāravadācaret .. 41 ..
 
hemaniṣkasahasraṃ vai dadyādvai gurudakṣiṇām .
tadardhaṃ śataniṣkaṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā yathāvasu .. 42 ..
 
daśaniṣkaṃ tadardhaṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā'tha dakṣiṇām .
ācāryāya pradadyādvai na kadācidadakṣiṇam .. 43 ..
 
tulābhārādikaṃ karma sarveṣāmapi ṛtvijām .
dakṣiṇā tu tadardhā syāt tadardhā paricāriṇām .. 44 ..
 
anyeṣāṃ tu yathāśakti tato'nyasmiṃstu vāsare .
kuṃbhamaṇḍalakuṇḍasthavibhoḥ kuryādvisarjanam .. 45 ..
 
viśeṣārcanasaṃyuktaṃ tato'nyasmindine tu vā .
evaṃ sarvatra vai kuryādvisarjanavidhiṃ dvija .. 46 ..

Chapter - 22
śrīḥ .
dvāviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ .
sanakaḥ .
saṃprokṣaṇavidhānaṃ me prabrūhi munisattama .
prāyaścitteṣu sarvatra praśasto yastu pūrakaḥ .. 1 ..
 
śāṇḍilyaḥ .
prāsādapratimāpīṭhe pramādādeva dūṣite .
samāhite yathāpūrvaṃ pūjālope viśeṣataḥ .. 2 ..
 
caṇḍālapatitodakyāsūtikādiśavādibhiḥ .
sūtakairmṛtakairvā'pi nityāśaucaiśca garhitaiḥ .. 3 ..
 
śilpibhirvedavāhyaiśca mūrkhairajñātajātibhiḥ .
viṇmūtrarudhirāpeyaretobhirdūṣite sati .. 4 ..
 
janane maraṇe nṝṇāṃ mandire rāṣṭrasaṃkule .
śvasṛgālakharādyaiśca vāyasaśyenajātibhiḥ .. 5 ..
 
spṛṣṭe bimbe tu saṃdṛṣṭe tantrāṇāṃ saṅkare sati .
evamādiṣu sarveṣu saṃprokṣaṇavidhirbhavet .. 6 ..
 
dauṣairupahataṃ jñātvā prāsādapratimādikam .
asaṃprokṣyārcanaṃ kurvan rājānaṃ rāṣṭram̈añjasā .. 7 ..
 
devatāyatanaṃ grāmaṃ nāśayennātra saṃśayaḥ .
tasmāt saṃprokṣaṇaṃ kārya prāsādapratimādiṣu .. 8 ..
 
purā saṃprokṣaṇadinaṃ rājarāṣṭrābhivṛddhidam .
niścayīkṛtya kālajñaiḥ purastāduktavāsare .. 9 ..
 
aṃkurānarpya vidhivat pascāt saṃśodhite gṛhe .
sarvatra gomayāmbhobhiḥ puṇyāhoktipurassaram .. 10 ..
 
saṃprokṣya pañcabhirgavyaiḥ kuśodakasamanvitaiḥ .
mūlaberādibimbānāṃ ṣaḍbhiḥ siddhārthakādibhiḥ .. 11 ..
 
pavitrāvartitairadbhirbahuśaḥ kṣāḷane kṛte .
pradhānadinapūrvasyāṃ rātryāṃ yāgādimaṇṭape .. 12 ..
 
toraṇadvārakalaśavitānadhvajaśobhite .
dīkṣādhivāsavat kṛtvā kuṃbhe vai maṇṭapasthale .. 13 ..
 
pūjanaṃ vibhavenaiva japāntaṃ mūlamandire .
kṣīrādyaiḥ pañcaviṃśadbhiḥ snāpayeddhruvakautukam .. 14 ..
 
lepabhittipaṭasthasya purastādbhadraviṣṭare .
karmārcāmathavā kūrcaṃ darpaṇe pratibimbitam .. 15 ..
 
saṃsnāpya vidhivat kuṃbhaiḥ sthāpitairagramaṇṭape .
utsavārcādi bimbānāmahgānāmāśrayātmanām .. 16 ..
 
pūjanaṃ snapanaṃ kāryaṃ pāścātyaṃ yāgamaṇḍape .
tatrasthe havanaṃ kuṇḍe śaṅkhacakrādilakṣaṇe .. 17 ..
 
madhukṣīrādibhiḥ kāryaṃ sahasraśatasaṅkhyayā .
karmabimbaṃ vinānyeṣāṃ bimbānāmaṅgarūpiṇām .. 18 ..
 
dakṣiṇe maṇṭapasyātha śayanaṃ kalpayenmahat .
tilataṇḍulaśālīnāṃ bhārairvastrādibhiḥ saha .. 19 ..
 
tadūrdhve śāyayedarcāṃ vidhivadbaddhakautukām .
saṃpūjya kambaḷādyaiśca chādayettāṃ sitādibhiḥ .. 20 ..
 
varṇakairmaṇḍalaṃ kuryāccakrāmburuhabhūṣitam .
yāvat prabhātasamayaṃ bimbasthasya samīpataḥ .. 21 ..
 
deśiko mūlamantrasya japenaiva nayenniśām .
prabātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ kṛtasandhyāvidhirguruḥ .. 22 ..
 
catuḥsthānārcanaṃ kṛtvā pūrvavat snapanānvitam .
muhūrte śobhane prāpte navavastrapariṣkṛtam .. 23 ..
 
sottarīyopavītaṃ ca kṛtakautukabandhanam .
samastatatvavinyastamabhyarcyārghyādibhiḥ kramāt .. 24 ..
 
tāsu svahṛdayāmbhojāt puṣpāñjalipurassaram .
agrāhyamaparicchedyamamūrtamamalaṃ mahat .. 25 ..
 
nityaśuddhamanaupamyaṃ susūkṣmamacalaṃ sphuṭam .
saccidrūpaṃ ca sāmānyaṃ bhāsvaraṃ sudṛḍhaṃ mahat .. 26 ..
 
tejastu saṃkramayyātha daṇḍavat praṇipatya tu .
vinivedya vibhoḥ sarvaṃ kṛtaṃ karma dvijottamāḥ .. 27 ..
 
utthāpyotsavabimbādīn pūrvavanmaṅgalaiḥ saha .
mahākumbhaṃ ca purato vāhayan mūrtipādibhiḥ .. 28 ..
 
karakāstraṃ samādāya tvācāryaḥ purato vrajet .
śalākāmātrayā'cchinnadhārayā secayan bhuvam .. 29 ..
 
prādakṣiṇyena dhāmāntaḥ praveśya munipuḍgavāḥ .
mahotsavoktamārgeṇa kumbhaprokṣaṇamācaret .. 30 ..
 
dvārāvaraṇadevāṃśca ālayaśrayavartinaḥ .
khageśaviṣvaksenādīn parivārāṃśca sarvasaḥ .. 31 ..
 
kumbhāvaśiṣṭatoyena prokṣayet sarvataḥ kramāt .
avaśiṣṭaṃ kumbhatoyaṃ balipīṭhe'bhiṣecayet .. 32 ..
 
evaṃ samprokṣya vidhivat prāsādāntaḥ praviśya ca .
karasthaṃ kautukaṃ cātha hṛdayena visṛjya tu .. 33 ..
 
gobhūhemādikaṃ datvā sarvadoṣapraśāntaye .
devamarghyādinābhyarcya havirantaṃ viśeṣataḥ .. 34 ..
 
brāhnaṇān bhojayet paścāt sahasraṃ śatameva vā .
sadyo vā sakalaṃ tvevaṃ kuryāt saṃprokṣaṇaṃ vibhoḥ .. 35 ..
 
puṣpāṃkurapuraskaṃ tu tattaddoṣapraśāntaye .
na tithirna ca nakṣatraṃ kālavelā na vidyate .. 36 ..
 
sadyaḥ samprokṣaṇaṃ viprāḥ niśi vā divase'pi vā .
prāyaścittavilambe tu kuryāt kālanirīkṣaṇam .. 37 ..
 
iti samprokṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ sarvaṃ cāpi dvijottamāḥ .} .
sthāpanaṃ pañcagavyasya sarvābyudayasādhanam .. 38 ..
 
nāgayoga iti khyātaḥ sārparkṣakaraṇakṣamaiḥ .
ṛkṣeṇa vānayorekayogasyānnāgasaṃjñitaḥ .. 39 ..
 
purā tanniścayīkṛtya kartavyamiti sattamaiḥ .
tadarthamaṃkurānarpya dravyāṇi samupāharet .. 40 ..
 
manaśśilāṃ harītālamañjanaṃ śyāmasīsake .
saurāṣṭraṃ rocanaṃ caiva gairikaṃ pāradaṃ tathā .. 41 ..
 
ādāya dhāturatnāni pajharāgapurassaram .
muktāphalaṃ pravāḷaṃ ca vajraṃ vaiḍūryasaṃjñitam .. 42 ..
 
gomedaṃ puṣyarāgaṃ ca mahānīlaṃ ca gāruḍam .
ratnānyetāni saṃgṛhya bījāni samupāharet .. 43 ..
 
śālinīvārakaṃkūni priyaṃgutilamāṣakān .
mṛdgāṃśca yavaveṇūṃśca yavasākhyānyanantaram .. 44 ..
 
hiraṇyaṃ rajataṃ tāmramāyasaṃ trapusīsakam .
sauvarṇaṃ kūrmarūpaṃ ca sauvarṇaṃ cakramambujam .. 45 ..
 
rājataṃ pāñcajanyaṃ ca samāhṛtya tataḥ param .
kadaḷīpanasāmrāṇāṃ bilvāmalakayorapi .. 46 ..
 
dāḍimīmātuḷuṅgasya nāḷikerasya kālataḥ .
pavkāni samupāhṛtya phalāni ca tataḥ param .. 47 ..
 
candanāgarukarpūrakuṃkumādīnyupāharet .
koṣṭhaṃ māṃsī haridre dve murāśaileyacampakān .. 48 ..
 
vacākaccoramustāni hrīberośīrajānyapi .
mallikājātivakuḷanandyāvartakacaṃpakān .. 49 ..
 
pāṭalīpajhakalhārāṇyupāhṛtya tataḥ param .
vastrādīni sitādīni mālyāni ca viśeṣataḥ .. 50 ..
 
śālipūrvāṇi dhānyāni kuśadūrvādikānyapi .
bilvāśvatthakadambāmrapallavādīni yānyapi .. 51 ..
 
haviḥ pākopayogyāni taṇḍulādīni sattama .
homadravyāṇi sarvāṇi pajhapatrāṇi mṛṇmaye .. 52 ..
 
dvādaśāṅguḷavistīrṇe pavkāpavke ghaṭe dṛḍhe .
nṛhareḥ pūjanārthaṃ tu kuṃbhaṃ sakarakaṃ bṛhat .. 53 ..
 
evamādīni cānyāni purā'hṛtya vidhānataḥ .
gṛhṇīyāt pañcagavyāni mṛtpātre nūtane śubhe .. 54 ..
 
gomūtraṃ gomayaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi mastu ca pañcamam .
kapilāyā jarāyā vā pañcagavyaṃ praśasyate .. 55 ..
 
tayorabhāve cānyāsāṃ gavāṃ gavyaṃ vidhīyate .
nārtāyā na ca garbhiṇyā na vṛddhāyāḥ kadācana .. 56 ..
 
nāvatsāyā upādeyaṃ dhenormūtraṃ śakṛddvayam .
bhuviṣṭhaṃ gomayaṃ grāhyaṃ soṣṇaṃ kṛmyādyadūṣitam .. 57 ..
 
niṣpīḍya samyaggṛhṇīyādgomayasya rasaṃ punaḥ .
sadyastaptaṃ ghṛtaṃ śuddhamahorātroṣitaṃ dadhi .. 58 ..
 
kṣīraṃ grāhyamataptaṃ ca daśāhājjanmanaḥ param .
gomūtraṃ viṣṇugāyatryā gandhadvāre ti gomayam .. 59 ..
 
āpyāyasve ti ca kṣīraṃ dadhikrāvṇṇe ti vai dadhi .
ghṛtaṃ śukramasī tyevaṃ dravyāṇi saha yojayet .. 60 ..
 
viṣṇugāyatriyā yadvā pañcopaniṣadaistu vā .
parameṣṭhī śakṛnmantro gomūtrasya tu pūruṣaḥ .. 61 ..
 
viśvamantro bhaveddadhno nivṛttissarpiṣobhavet .
payasaḥ sarvamantraḥ syāt sarveṣāṃ vāṣṭavarṇakamam .. 62 ..
 
prokṣaṇe snapane pañcagavyamantrā udīritāḥ .
sarvadoṣopaśāntyarthaṃ saṃprāpte sthāpane sati .. 63 ..
 
saudarśananṛsiṃhasya hṛdādyairnetrapaścimaiḥ .
aṅgamantraiḥ prakalpyāni kṣīrāntāni śakṛdrasāt .. 64 ..
 
dadhi dviguṇamāghārāt pīyūṣaṃ triguṇaṃ tataḥ .
ṣaḍguṇaṃ mūtrametasmācchakṛdvāri caturguṇam .. 65 ..
 
sthāpane kathitaṃ mānamabhiṣekavidhāvapi .
bhūmisaṃśodhanārthaṃ tat prokṣayo pañcakaṃ samam .. 66 ..
 
gomayena samaṃ mūtraṃ dadhi syāddviguṇaṃ tataḥ .
dadhnaścaturguṇaṃ sarpiḥ sarpiṣoṣṭaguṇaṃ payaḥ .. 67 ..
 
prāśane pañcagavyānāṃ pramāṇamidamīritam .
sthāpanaṃ snapanaṃ hyetat sarvāghaughavināśanam .. 68 ..
 
brahnakūrcasamopetaṃ hanyādāgāminaṃ tvagham .
tadbidhānaṃ samāsena śrṛṇu vakṣyāmi tatvataḥ .. 69 ..
 
cūrṇena yavaveṇubhyāṃ sametaṃ tu kuśodakam .
brahnakūrcamitikhyātaṃ vaiṣṇavāstraughasaprabham .. 70 ..
 
kuśodaṃ dvividhaṃ proktaṃ śuṣkāśuṣkavibāgataḥ .
aśuṣkamatha niṣpīḍya vastreṇa rasamāharet .. 71 ..
 
prahṛtya śuṣkamudake prakṣipya jalamāharet .
pavitraṃ mantramuccārya mūlaṃ vāstrasamanvim .. 72 ..
 
gomūtrasaṃmitaṃ mānādgṛṇḍīyāttat kuśodakam .
śakṛdrasapramāṇena cūrṇaṃ tatra miyojayet .. 73 ..
 
cakrāstramantramuccārya gāyatryā biṣṇusaṃjñayā .
dhyātvā ca cakranṛhariṃ tadgavyeṣu niyojayet .. 74 ..
 
yadvā pṛthak sthāpayitvā pañcagavyaiḥ kuśodake .
hṛdayādyastraparyantairabhimantrya ca yojayet .. 75 ..
 
praśastaṃ prāśanaṃ tābhyāṃ prātaḥ sarvāghanāśanam .
iti samyak samākhyātaḥ pañcagavyavidhistava .. 76 ..
 
maṇṭape'tha purā klṛpte yāgasnapanasiddhaye .
paścagavyādhivāsārthaṃ yajanaṃ prārabhedguruḥ .. 77 ..
 
pūrvedyuḥ karmadivasāt trisnāyī samupoṣitaḥ .
ahirbudhnye muhūrte tu ṛtvigbhiḥ pāñcarātrikaiḥ .. 78 ..
 
puṇyāhaṃ prāgvaduccārya gavyairabhyukṣayet sthalīm .
sadravyāmastramantreṇa prāgbhāge dhānyaviṣṭare .. 79 ..
 
daśāramaṣṭapatraṃ tu cakrābjaṃ bhūpurāntake .
vilikhya karṇikāmadhye trikoṇakṛtasaṃpuṭe .. 80 ..
 
mahākumbhaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya sūtravastrādiveṣṭitam .
karakeṇa samopetaṃ dikpālakalaśānvitam .. 81 ..
 
pūritaṃ dadhimadhvājvakṣīrayuktena vāriṇā .
pippalādidaḷopetaṃ gandhasragbhiralaṃkṛtam .. 82 ..
 
sakūrcaṃ saphalaṃ sarvaratnahemasamanvitam .
sarvauṣadhisamopetamakṣatairapi cārcitam .. 83 ..
 
pradīpya taijase pātre mṛṇmaye vā ghṛtena tu .
kāpilena caturdikṣu dīpaṃ netrābhimantritam .. 84 ..
 
sthāpayeddhānyapīṭhasthacakrāmburuhamadhyataḥ .
kumbhasya purataḥ prāgvadupaviśyāsanopari .. 85 ..
 
prāṇāyāmādikaṃ kṛtvā bhūtaśuddhiṃ yathāvidhi .
saudarśananṛsiṃhasya mantraṃ karaśarīragam .. 86 ..
 
sāṅgaṃ vinyasya hṛdaye cakrāmburuhamadhyagam .
nādāvasānagaganādavatārya parādinā .. 87 ..
 
mūrtimantraṃ svamantreṇa bhāvanāmṛtajaiḥ śubhaiḥ .
arghyādyairakhilairbhogairabhyarcya praṇavena tu .. 88 ..
 
prīṇayitvā tathā hutvā nābhikuṇḍagatānale .
bahirabhyarcayet kuṃbhe madhyasthe cakravārije .. 89 ..
 
samāvāhyaṃ svamantreṇa mūrtairarghyādibhiḥ kramāt .
japāvasānaṃ vidhivat kuṇḍe krābjalakṣaṇe .. 90 ..
 
cakre vā paṅkaje śaṅkhe turyaśre sthaṇḍile'pi vā .
samidbhiḥ saptabhirhutvā pūrṇāntaṃ tadanantaram .. 91 ..
 
candanena prasūnaisca guggulvagaruṇā'pi ca .
dugdhena dadhinā kṣaudraguḍakhaṇjānvitena ca .. 92 ..
 
śālyādīnāṃ tathā bījaiḥ pāyasādyaiśca sarpiṣā .
hutvā'tha pūrṇayā tṛptiṃ nītvā samyak samarpya ca .. 93 ..
 
tataḥ kalaśaniṣṭhasya purastācchodhite sthale .
sarvadhānyamaye pīṭhe likhite cakrapaṅkaje .. 94 ..
 
svāstṛte navavastreṇa chādite cordhvataḥ kuśaiḥ .
prāguktaṃ kumbhamādāya dvādaśāhgulasaṃmitam .. 95 ..
 
bahirantaśca saṃkṣālya sūtreṇāveṣṭya pūrvavat .
candanādyaiḥ samālipya praṇavena samāhitaḥ .. 96 ..
 
cakrābjakarṇikāmadhye vinyasettamadhomukham .
tato mānena tattulyamapavkaṃ mṛṇmayaṃ ghaṭam .. 97 ..
 
saṃprokṣya pañcagavyena sāstreṇa kuśavāriṇā .
caturguṇena sūtreṇa pajhairantarmukhairdaḷaiḥ .. 98 ..
 
bandhayitvā tu sudṛḍhamāsyavarjaṃ samantataḥ .
taṃ ca tenaiva vinyasya japaṃstāramavāṅmukham .. 99 ..
 
stṛṇīyādūrdhvato darbhān kumbhayoḥ parameṣṭhinā .
prokṣayedarghyatoyena prāṅmukhaḥ puruṣātmanā .. 100 ..
 
viśvamantreṇa vikiredakṣatāni tadūrdhvataḥ .
uttānayennivṛtyā tau pāṇibhyāmuttarāntimam .. 101 ..
 
sarpiṣāṣṭottaraśataṃ viṣṇugāyatriyā hunet .
sarvātmanā'tha saṃspṛśya saṃpātājyena mantravit .. 102 ..
 
dravyāṇi pavkakumbhe'smin hṛnmantreṇa niyojayet .
mṛtkandadhāturatrāni bījalohaphalāni ca .. 103 ..
 
candanādīni puṣpāṇi tathā sarvauṣadhīni ca .
kuśapallavadūrvāśca pūrayitvā tadūrdhvataḥ .. 104 ..
 
yojayet pañcagavyena prāhmukhaḥ sakuśodakam .
arcayitvā'rghyagandhādyaiḥ sāṅgaṃ mūlaṃ samuccaran .. 105 ..
 
ācchādya navavastreṇa dadyādbhūtabaliṃ tataḥ .
devatāyatanagrāmanagareṣvapi pattane .. 106 ..
 
sthāpanāspadamāsādya śobha naṃ pañcagavyakaiḥ .
tatra madhye khanecchvabraṃ mūlamantramudīrayan .. 107 ..
 
aṅguṣṭhodaramāvṛtya tridhā sūtreṇa veṣṭayet .
tenaiva bhrāmayenmadye sthāpya tatrāvaṭaṃ khanet .. 108 ..
 
hastamānamadhastācca ṣaḍaṅgulasamanvitam .
saṃprokṣyaṃ pañcagavyena tatra ratnādikaṃ nyaset .. 109 ..
 
śeṣaṃ dhyātvā tadūrdhve tu abyarcyārghyādibhiḥ kramāt .
vāsasā'cchādya digbandhamācaredastramuccaran .. 110 ..
 
saṃspṛśya gavyaṃ kumbhābhyāṃ dhyātvā mūlaṃ japedguruḥ .
prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ kṛtvā snānādikīḥ kriyāḥ .. 111 ..
 
kumbhasthaṃ nṛhariṃ pūjya japāntaṃ pūrvavarmanā .
puṇyāhavācanaṃ kṛtvā muhūrte śobhane guruḥ .. 112 ..
 
pajhapatrāvṛtaṃ kumbhaṃ śvabre tāreṇa vinyaset .
paritaḥ sarvadhānyena pūriyatvā'calaṃ yathā .. 113 ..
 
pañcagavyaṃ samuddhṛtya ghaṭasthaṃ kavacaṃ lapan .
tenaiva pūrayet kumbhaṃ śvabrasthaṃ mūlamuccaran .. 114 ..
 
samabhyarcyārghyapuṣpādyaiḥ pūrayenmṛdbhirāhṛtaiḥ .
nṛsuktaṃ bhadrasūktaṃ ca svastisūktaṃ ca pāṭhayet .. 115 ..
 
śāntihomaṃ tataḥ kuryāddravyaiḥ pūrvoditaiḥ kramāt .
śataṃ śatārdhaṃ pādaṃ vā yathāśakti samācaret .. 116 ..
 
dakṣiṇā gurave deyā pratiṣṭhāphalamicchatā .
iti te pañcagavyasya sthāpanaṃ parikīrtitam .. 117 ..
 
sarvotpātapraśamanaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam .
sarvasaukhyapradaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvopadravavāraṇam .. 118 ..
 
sarvorogyapradaṃ nityaṃ putrapautravivardhanam .
yadyat kāmayate mantrī tattadāpnotyasaṃśayam .. 119 ..

Chapter - 23
śrīḥ .
trayoviṃśo'yāyaḥ .
sanakaḥ .
praśaṃsitaṃ purā brahnan sudarśananṛsiṃhayoḥ .
ekarūpaṃ mahāyantrasthāpanaṃ sthiralakṣaṇam .. 1 ..
 
vistareṇa samācakṣva mayi sānugraho yadi .
śāṇḍilyaḥ .
purā nārāyaṇenoktaṃ puṇye badarikāśrame .. 2 ..
 
brahnaṇaḥ śīrṣavicchedamahāpātakaśāntaye .
pṛcchataḥ śaṅkarasyātha sarvapāpāpanodanam .. 3 ..
 
so'pi taṃ vistarācchrutvā kailāsaśikharopari .
pratiṣṭhāpya vidhānena yantre viṣṭarasaṃsthite .. 4 ..
 
kalpāntānalasūryābhamubhayānanamavyayam .
sarvalokamayaṃ sarvadevatāmayamadbhutam .. 5 ..
 
sarvādhāramanādhāraṃ sarvaśaktikriyātmakam .
duṣṭadoṣagaṇaṃ sarvaṃ nirdahantaṃ svatejasā .. 6 ..
 
samārādhyā'cireṇaiva pūtabhāvo'bhavadbhavaḥ .
tathānye purūhūtādyā vidyāmenāmavāpya ca .. 7 ..
 
śaṅkarāt pūrṇasaṃjñānāt svadigbhāgānapālayan .
prajāpālanaśīlānāṃ bhūpānāmetadarcanam .. 8 ..
 
nairantaryeṇa kartavyamanyathā jāyate'dhṛtiḥ .
jāyate kathameteṣāmupapātakināmapi .. 9 ..
 
akurvatāṃ jagatsthityai maryādāyā vilokanam .
kurvatāṃ svasvaduṣprāpaṃ bhūpatīnāṃ tu kiṃ punaḥ .. 10 ..
 
tathānyeṣāṃ dvijātīnāṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam .
pratiṣṭhāpyārcanīyaṃ tat sarvakāmasamṛddhidam .. 11 ..
 
tadvidhānaṃ viśeṣeṇa śrṛṇu guhyatamaṃ param .
divyādyāyatane citre prāṅkaṇādau tu kutracit .. 12 ..
 
grāmādau tu nadītīre vipine parvatopari .
prāsādaṃ maṇḍapaṃ vā'tha sacitraṃ sarvatomukham .. 13 ..
 
prākpaścimānanaṃ vā'tha sagavākṣakavāṭakam .
ekāditalasaṃyuktaṃ cakralāñchanalāñchitam .. 14 ..
 
mukhabhadrasamopetamārohaṇasamanvitam .
saprākāraṃ samāpādya prāsādābhyantare tate .. 15 ..
 
bhadraviṣṭaramadyasthabhūpure vajralāñchite .
śeṣādibhirdikṣu madhye ṣaṭkoṇapurabhūṣite .. 16 ..
 
savāyubījavāyavyamaṇḍalena virājitam .
daśāracakramadhyasthadaḷāṣṭakakajāntare .. 17 ..
 
sthāpayettaṃ mahāyantraṃ lakṣaṇenopalakṣitam .
ādvādaśāṅgulānmānādekaikāṅgulavardhitāt .. 18 ..
 
ādvādaśāṅgulāntāni mānāni syustrayodaśa .
teṣvekaṃ niścayīkṛtya karturicchāvaśena tu .. 19 ..
 
pādādyuṣṇīṣaryantaṃ dviṣoḍhā vāṣṭadhā bhavet .
berārdhamānamādāya svabāgārthaṃ samantataḥ .. 20 ..
 
sūtreṇa karṇikāvṛttaṃ madhyasthena tato bahiḥ .
ekaikāṃśāni pajhāni ṣaṭ bhavanti yathākramam .. 21 ..
 
catuṣpatraṃ bhavedādyamaṣṭapatramanantaram .
dviraṣṭakesaraṃ vidyāt tṛtīyaṃ ṣoḍaśacchadam .. 22 ..
 
dvātriṃśatkesaraṃ turyaṃ dvātriṃśaddaḷabhūṣitam .
aṣṭāṣṭakesaropetaṃ tathāsaṅkhyadaḷaṃ bahiḥ .. 23 ..
 
tat kesaravinirmuktaṃ aṣṭapatraṃ tathā bahiḥ .
bhūpurādīni sārdhena saṃpuṭāntāni bāhyataḥ .. 24 ..
 
dvābhyāṃ dvābyāṃ tathāśābyāṃ bahirāvaraṇadvayam .
pūrvasmin keśavādyāṃśca viṣṇvādyāṃśca tato bahiḥ .. 25 ..
 
jagatsthitau samudyuktānṛṣīkeśajanārdanāt .
bahiścakragadādīnāmaṃśaṃ teṣāmadhordhvataḥ .. 26 ..
 
bhāgadvayaṃ tatastyaktvā vārāhanarasiṃhayoḥ .
samantādbhūpurasyā'tha bhogārthaṃ yantrakalpane .. 27 ..
 
mahāyantrasya vistāre vibhakte pañcadhā'thavā .
saptadhā madhyabāhyasthairnālāṃstryaṃśaiḥ prakalpayet .. 28 ..
 
kiñcidviṣṭarapīṭhoccān nāḷānāmadhikāyatiḥ .
varāhavadanākārā pārśvayormūlavistṛte .. 29 ..
 
dakṣiṇādyanupātena tvāmūlādagrapaścimam .
pramāṇamevaṃ buddhvā'tra lohadāruśilādikam .. 30 ..
 
samāharedyathāśāstraṃ pramāṇena yathāvidhi .
saṃpādyā phalakākārā bhāgaikena ghanā dṛḍhā .. 31 ..
 
syāt ṣaḍaṃśaghanā śailī caturaṃghaśanā'thavā .
ākarṇikāvanerbāhyacaturaśrapurākṛtiḥ .. 32 ..
 
pramāṇāduttamādasmānmadhyamādhamavāñchayā .
tryaṃśenārdhena vā kuryānmukhyakalpamudīritam .. 33 ..
 
beroṣṭhaṃ dviguṇīkṛtya tatpramāṇena kalpayet .
phalakāmadyatastyaktvā lambamānaṃ yathāpurā .. 34 ..
 
śeṣaṃ dviraṣṭadhā bhaṅkhtvā karṇikārdhena tadbahiḥ .
prāgvadāvṛtipajhāni bhūpurādīnyatha tribhiḥ .. 35 ..
 
tatastribhistribhiḥ kāryaṃ mūrtīnāmāvṛtidvayam .
ardhena caturaśraṃ tu mūrtīnāmāvṛtidvayam .. 36 ..
 
ekaikaṃ tryaṃśasambhūtaṃ pramāṇena yathā bhṛśam .
kalpayet keśavādyāṃśca viṣṇvādyāṃśca dviraṣṭadhā .. 37 ..
 
kuryādvaikāvṛtau buddhyā saṃmantrya dhyānayogataḥ .
madhyataḥ karṇikāyāṃ tu paridhau candramaṇḍalam .. 38 ..
 
tanmadhye tārakaṃ kuryāt tanmadhyena sudarśanam .
bhujaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiryuktamaṣṭābhirvā'nalaprabham .. 39 ..
 
piṅgalocanakeśāḍhcaṃ raktāmbaradharaṃ vibhum .
daṃṣṭrākarāḷavadanavivarodbhūtapāvakam .. 40 ..
 
kuṭilabhrukuṭībhaṅgabhaṃgurāḷakaṣaṭpadam .
lalāṭalocanodgīrṇajvālājvalitadiṅmukham .. 41 ..
 
ūrdhvajvālāgaṇālīḍhakirīṭataṭaśobhitam .
śrīvatsakaustubhoraskaṃ graiveyakavirājitam .. 42 ..
 
pādāvalambinīṃ divyāṃ dadhānamupavītavat .
pratyālīḍhena tiṣṭhantaṃ cakrākramaṇarūpiṇā .. 43 ..
 
pādayordakṣiṇāṃguṣṭhaprāntarekhāt tathetarāt .
pārṣṇeḥ svamadhyato mānaṃ dehalabdhāṃgulena ca .. 44 ..
 
catvāriṃśat sāṣṭakaṃ syāt pratyālīḍhaṃ cirānvitam .
mukhyadakṣiṇahastādimukhyavāmakarāvadhi .. 45 ..
 
dviraṣṭabāhubhirdhatte prādakṣiṇyakrameṇa tu .
śaktiṃ khaṅgaṃ tathā cāgni maṅkuśaṃ daṇḍakuntake .. 46 ..
 
paraśuṃ ca sahasrāraṃ daraṃ ca saśaraṃ dhanuḥ .
pāśaṃ halaṃ tato vajraṃ gadāṃ ca musalaṃ tathā .. 47 ..
 
triśūlametānyastrāṇi pratyekaṃ vīryavanti ca .
duṣpradharṣaṃ bhayaghnāni vahantamarisūdanam .. 48 ..
 
anyathāṣṭabhujo dhatte mukhyadakṣakarādikaiḥ .
pajhāṃ kuśau ca musalaṃ cakra matyugratejasam .. 49 ..
 
śaṅkhaṃ ca saśaraṃ cāpaṃ pāśaṃ kaumodakīṃ kramāt .
kṛtvaivamardhacitraṃ tu navatālena śilpinā .. 50 ..
 
pādayorantare tasya tiṣṭhataḥ karṇikāvanau .
śāntipuṣṭivaśīkāravidveṣākarṣamāraṇān .. 51 ..
 
ucchāṭanaṃ vā yaḥ kartumicchet sādhakasattamaḥ .
tasya sādhyaṃ likhenmantrī śaktyā saṃpuṭitaṃ vibhoḥ .. 52 ..
 
indubimbasya paryante ṣaṭkoṇaṃ kramaśo likhet .
prāgādikoṇaṣaṭke tu pravartakanivartake .. 53 ..
 
mantrākṣarāṇi sādīni sabindūni ca vai purā .
upakramya ca varmāstre likhedantarmukhānamūn .. 54 ..
 
bahiḥ koṇāntarāḷeṣu prokto'yaṃ dakṣiṇāditaḥ .
ācakrādīnyathāṅgāni jvālācakrāntimāni ca .. 55 ..
 
caturdaḷāgre prāgādau varmāstre ca sabinduke .
tadantarāḷeṣvantasthā bindunā cāntarānanāḥ .. 56 ..
 
kesareṣvaṣṭapatrasya svarānanyāṃśca bindubhiḥ .
daḷeṣvaṣṭākṣarārṇaāṃni tathā bhūtāni tadbahiḥ .. 57 ..
 
dviraṣṭapatrakiñjalkanicaye prākprayogataḥ .
kādisāntāni varṇāni sabindūni yathāpurā .. 58 ..
 
taddaḷeṣu dviṣaṭkārṇaḥ varmāstre śirasā saha .
ṣoḍaśākṣara ityukto dvātriṃśatkesarādike .. 59 ..
 
ānuṣṭubhaṃ mahāmantraṃ nṛvarāhanṛsiṃhayoḥ .
bahiraṣṭāṣṭapatreṣu pātāḷanṛharermanum .. 60 ..
 
prāgvaladakṣaraśo nyasya tato'ṣṭadaḷapaṅkaje .
nārasiṃhaṃ tathāṣṭārṇaṃ tadbāhyasthe tu bhūpure .. 61 ..
 
saptadvīpasamudrāḍhye vajraiḥ koṇeṣu lāñchite .
prāgādyāsu mahādikṣu pārthivaṃ bījamuttamam .. 62 ..
 
tannāmamantrasaṃyuktaṃ antasthāḥ koṇabhūmiṣu .
tataḥ sapārthivaṃ bījaṃ koṇābhyantarabāhyayoḥ .. 63 ..
 
tadbahiḥ prātilomyena svaraṣoḍaśakaṃ nyaset .
sakārādīni kāntāni tathābhūtāni tadbahiḥ .. 64 ..
 
paritontyayugenaiva sādhyanāmavidarbhaṇam .
kṛtvā prati prayogeṇa bahirbhūpurasaṃpuṭāt .. 65 ..
 
pāśāṃkuśābyāmāveṣṭya dvābyāṃ vā bahubhistu vā .
puroditakrameṇaiva svasthāne keśavādayaḥ .. 66 ..
 
bāhyāvaraṇa bhūmiṣṭhāḥ prāgādyāsu ca viṣṇavaḥ .
tatkoṇeṣu hṛṣīkeśaḥ tacchidreṣu janārdanāḥ .. 67 ..
 
kalpanīyāśca tanmantrāḥ praṇavādyā yathākramam .
sajīvāḥ saṃjñayopetā namaskārasamanvitāḥ .. 68 ..
 
amukaṃ rakṣa rakṣeti tadante sādhyabhūṣitāḥ .
prāgādidikṣu tadbāhye tvantasthāścāṣṭabhiḥ saha .. 69 ..
 
yaśau raṣau lasau cātha vahāvapi sabindukau .
vilikhet punarapyetānaiśānyā'nala paścimam .. 70 ..
 
pāśāṅkuśābyāmāveṣṭya dvābhyāṃ vā bahubhistathā .
adhastānnṛvarāhaṃ ca sarvordhve nṛharermanum .. 71 ..
 
kramaśaḥ keśavādīnāṃ dhyānaṃ cākarṇayāmalam .
keśavaḥ svarṇavarṇo'bjaśahkhacakragādādharaḥ .. 72 ..
 
nārāyaṇo nīradābhaḥ śaṅkhacakragadābjadhṛk .
mādhavo'vjagadāśaṅkhacakrī nīlābjasannibhaḥ .. 73 ..
 
govindo dhavalaścakragadāśahkhapayojadhṛk .
viṣṇurgadāmbujadaracakrī bandhūkasaprabhaḥ .. 74 ..
 
raktascakradarāmbhojaśaṅkha dhṛṅnadhusūdanaḥ .
trivikramaścakragadāpajhaśaṅkhī japāruṇaḥ .. 75 ..
 
śahkhacakragadāpajhadharaḥ syādvāmano'ruṇaḥ .
pajhacakragadāśaṅkhī śrīdharaścandrasaprabhaḥ .. 76 ..
 
vidyutprabho hṛṣīkeśo gadācakradarābjadhṛk .
gadābjacakravidyābhṛtpajhanābho'ruṇaprabhaḥ .. 77 ..
 
dāmodaraḥ pajhaśaṅkhagadācakradharo'ruṇaḥ .
mukhyadakṣakarāmbhojāt mukhyavāmakarāvadhi .. 78 ..
 
pajhādikaṃ dhārayanta āyudhānāṃ catuṣṭayam .
kirīṭakaustubhadharā vanamālāvibhūṣitāḥ .. 79 ..
 
pītāmbaradharāḥ sarve prasannavadanekṣaṇāḥ .
karuṇāpūrṇahṛdayā jagaduddharaṇodyatāḥ .. 80 ..
 
yantratejo'sahiṣṇūnāṃ narāṇāṃ tāpaśantaye .
āsārairamṛternityaṃ secyantaḥ samantataḥ .. 81 ..
 
viṣṇuḥ prācyādidigbhāge hṛṣīkeśā vidiksthitāḥ .
janārdanāśchidragatāścāṣṭapāde caturbhujāḥ .. 82 ..
 
pṛṣṭadakṣiṇavāmābhyāṃ cakraśahkhadharāstathā .
mukhyavāmakareṇaiva varadā vā'bhayapradāḥ .. 83 ..
 
viṣṇavo dakṣiṇairmukhyairjvalatpāvakabhīṣaṇāḥ .
cakrakaumodakīśārhgān dhārayantaḥ sakhaḍgakān .. 84 ..
 
vahnyādikoṇadeśasthā hṛṣīkeśāḥ suvarṇabhāḥ .
śaṅkhaṃ halaṃ ca musalaṃ vahantaḥ śūlapaścimam .. 85 ..
 
prāgāgneyādikacchidradeśasthāśca janārdanāḥ .
jvalanmaratakābhāśca vīkṣamāṇāśca diksthitān .. 86 ..
 
daṇḍaṃ kuntaṃ ca śaktiṃ ca pāśaṃ cāṅkuśameva ca .
vajraṃ paraśusaṃjñaṃ ca tathā śatamukhānalam .. 87 ..
 
dadhānāḥ susamaiḥ sthānairutthitāḥ svastikādinā .
sukhāsīnāstu vā sarve kevalā vā saśaktikāḥ .. 88 ..
 
saṃkalpyāḥ tadadhaḥ sarvayajñāṅgaḥ sūkarānanaḥ .
kṛṣṇapiṅgaḷavarṇaābhaḥ puṇḍarīkanibhekṣaṇaḥ .. 89 ..
 
paścimābyāṃ ca pāṇibhyāṃ pūrvavaccakraśaṅkhabhṛt .
mukhyena dakṣiṇenaiva bhītānāmabhayapradaḥ .. 90 ..
 
bhūmyāḥ svāṅke niṣaṇṇāyā vāmenāsleṣatatparaḥ .
parastānnaharirdevastuhinācalasannibhaḥ .. 91 ..
 
karairaṣṭabhiratyugraḥ pṛṣṭhato dakṣiṇāditaḥ .
śaṅkhacakrāmbujagadāḥ khaḍgaṃ ca saśaraṃ dhanuḥ .. 92 ..
 
dhatte ṣaḍbhistu mukhyābhyāṃ hiraṇyakaśipuṃ ruṣā .
vidārayaṃśca svāṅkasthaṃ nakharaiḥ krakacopamaiḥ .. 93 ..
 
uddhṛtya sāmbujaṃ pāṇi kevalaṃ vā'bhayapradaḥ .
hiraṇyarudhirasrotaḥ paṅkitorasthalaḥ śubhaḥ .. 94 ..
 
sarvānetān sajīvena śaktibījena veṣṭayet .
bahiḥ prācyādidigdeśe sākārānastravigrahān .. 95 ..
 
cakrakaumodakīśārhganandakān vilikhedimān .
keśavādyāstathāstrāntāścatustriṃśattu mūrtayaḥ .. 96 ..
 
svatantraṃ kalpayenmantrī yadvā cāvaraṇakṣitau .
kṛtvaivaṃ prāhmukhaṃ yantramaparāṅgaṃ prakalpayet .. 97 ..
 
karṇikāvalayaṃ kuryāt prākpramāṇena madhyataḥ .
tadantare koṇaṣaṭkaṃ prakāśāhlādasaṃpuṭam .. 98 ..
 
tridhā vibhajya tadbāhyaṃ kṣetrārdhaṃ ca tadantare .
triraṣṭayedumbarāhye kamalaṃ dvādaśacchadam .. 99 ..
 
caturviṃśaddalaṃ cakraṃ nābhinemitrayānvitam .
prathibhiścāvṛtaṃ bāhye nemisthaistasya bāhyataḥ .. 100 ..
 
śaktibhiśca jayādyābiraṣṭābhiḥ parivāritam .
pūrvaṃ dvādaśapatrābjakarṇikāmadhyakalpite .. 101 ..
 
trikoṇasaṃpuṭākāre prakāśāhlādalakṣaṇe .
ṣaṭkoṇe lakṣayeddevaṃ kalpāntahutabhukprabham .. 102 ..
 
nṛpañacavastraṃ jñānādigumapūrṇamahārṇavam .
trilocanaṃ caturbāṃhuṃ catuścakradharaṃ param .. 103 ..
 
yogapaṭṭapinaddhāṅgaṃ jānvārūḍhabhujadvayam .
śrīvatsakaustubhoraskaṃ bhūṣitaṃ makuṭādibhiḥ .. 104 ..
 
hāraśekharakeyūrakaṭakairnūpurāntimaiḥ .
bhaktānāṃ svānuraktānāṃ siddhāntaniratātmanām .. 105 ..
 
aśokaviṭapicchāyānyājenārtivināśanam .
sādhusaṃrakṣaṇodyuktaceṣṭitaṃ hṛṣṛmānasam .. 106 ..
 
adhastāccaraṇāmbhojāt sādhyaṃ bījapuṭīkṛtam .
vilikhya koṇaṣaṭkeṣu prāgādyeṣu trikaṃ trikam .. 107 ..
 
sudarśananṛsiṃhasya mantrārṇāni yathākramam .
tadaṅgāni ca tadbāhye koṇābhyantarabhūmiṣu .. 108 ..
 
likhedāvṛttiyogena kṣārṇaṃ prathijaṇeṣu ca .
prāgādi cakrabāhye tu jayā candraprabhāvinī .. 109 ..
 
navadūrvāṅkuraśyāmā mohinī vijayā tataḥ .
rājopalaprabhā kāntā hlādinī pāṭalaprabhā .. 110 ..
 
ajitā kanakaprakhyā māyā nīlotpalaprabhā .
raktā' parājitā siddhirdhūmravarṇā svakaṃ patim .. 111 ..
 
vīkṣamāṇāśca satataṃ nīlotpalavilocanāḥ .
navayauvanalāvaṇyavibhavenopabṛṃhitāḥ .. 112 ..
 
karaṇḍamakuṭopetāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ .
vicitrakṣaumavasanāḥ sarvartukusumānvitāḥ .. 113 ..
 
dvibhujā dakṣahastasthapuṣpamālābhyalaṃkṛtāḥ .
vāme candrāṃśusahkāśa cāmaravyajanodyatāḥ .. 114 ..
 
bhūpaccarau nṛsiṃhasya bhīmograu bhīṣaṇadyutī .
daṃṣṭrākarāḷavadanau jvalatpāvakalocanau .. 115 ..
 
nīlanīradasaṃkāśau dvibhujau daṇḍacakriṇau .
udagrakāyāvatyugrau vīkṣayantau parasparam .. 116 ..
 
raktāmbaradharau raktakusumasragvimaṇḍitau .
saṃpādyaivaṃ mahāyantraṃ sudarśananṛsiṃhayoḥ .. 117 ..
 
sthāpayedvidhivanmantrī madhye prāsādamaṇṭape .
kṣmāparigrahamārabhya saṃpanne sarvakarmaṇi .. 118 ..
 
vinyaste viṣṭare yantre pratiṣṭhāpya vidhānataḥ .
traikālyamarcanaṃ kāryaṃ tallakṣaṇamathocyate .. 119 ..
 
taddairghyaṃ yantravistārādadhikaṃ dvādaśāhgulam .
vibhakte yantravistāre saptadhā vā'tha pañcadhā .. 120 ..
 
ekaikamantayostyaktvā bhāgairmadhyagatairataḥ .
pañcabhirvā tribhiḥ kāryā viṣṭarasya tu vistṛtiḥ .. 121 ..
 
ekaikaṃ madhyataḥ sthāpya pārśvayoḥ saṣaḍaṅgulam .
yantrapārśvasthanāḷābhyāṃ suṣiradbayamācaret .. 122 ..
 
śiṣṭāni mārjayenmantrī caturaśraprasiddhaye .
tricatuḥpañcadhā vā'tha yantrocchrāye vibhājite .. 123 ..
 
tattadekāṃśamānena kāryaḥsyādviṣṭarocchrayaḥ .
pīṭhavattadalaṃkṛtya pañcāhgaiḥ parito bahiḥ .. 124 ..
 
tadūrdhve viṣṭaraṃ yantraṃ kalpayettadvidhiṃ śrṛṇu .
pīḍamadhyagataṃ bhāgaṃ madhyasthena tu tantunā .. 125 ..
 
karṇikārthaṃ paribhrāmya śeṣe ṣoḍhā vibājite .
dviraṣṭakesaropetamaṣṭapatrābjamastake .. 126 ..
 
bhāgena tadbahistadvada daśāraṃ cakramujjvalam .
vāyumaṇḍalamadhyena ṣaṭkoṇaṃ tu bahistribhiḥ .. 127 ..
 
vajrāṅkitaṃ koṇabhūṣu bhāgārdhena tu bhūpuram .
yantramadyamanāḷasya niveśārthaṃ tu madhyataḥ .. 128 ..
 
vedhayet tatpramāṇena sādhyanāma samantataḥ .
vilikhya tadbahirveṣṭya kesarāṇāṃ dviraṣṭake .. 129 ..
 
ṣoḍaśārṇaṃ nṛsiṃhasya taddviṣaṭkākṣarāvadhau .
huṃphaṭsvāhā samopeto nṛhareḥ ṣoḍaśākṣaraḥ .. 130 ..
 
prāgādyaṣṭadaleṣvasya mantramānuṣṭubhaṃ param .
catuṣṭayakrameṇaiva pratyekasmin daḷe nyaset .. 131 ..
 
bahirdaśāracakrasya prāgarādyeṣu mantrapam .
saudarśananṛsiṃhasya hanaśabdasamanbitam .. 132 ..
 
vilikheddvandvayogena bāhye vāyavyamaṇḍale .
vilikhedvartuḷākāre vāyavyaṃ bījamuttamam .. 133 ..
 
varma cāstrasametaṃ ca vilikhedantarāntarā .
bāhyasthe koṇaṣaṭke tu likhedāgneyamakṣaram .. 134 ..
 
kalpayet pratikoṇaṃ tu vahnijvālāsamanvitam .
koṇeṣu bhūpurasyāntaḥ pārthivaṃ bījamullikhet .. 135 ..
 
aṅkāro'tha vidigbhāge parito bhadrapīṭhavat .
kaṇṭhadeśaṃ samāśritya dvau dvau prācyāṃ diśi kramāt .. 136 ..
 
anyonyamabhivīkṣantau kalpayeduttamottame .
yantrasandhāraṇodyuktau vyāttāsyāvugralocanau .. 137 ..
 
anantaguḷikau prācyāṃ yāmyāyāṃ śaṅkhavāsukī .
satakṣako mahāpajhaḥ pratīcyāṃ uttare tathā .. 138 ..
 
kārkoṭakastathāpajho viśeṣastatra kathyate .
vibhajya karṇikābhūmerbhūpurāntaṃ vidhāntare .. 139 ..
 
nṛsiṃhayantraṃ kurvīta bāhyato yantraviṣṭaram .
dikṣu nārāyaṇāstrāṇi tatra kūrcamayāni ca .. 140 ..
 
sitādidhātujairvarṇaiḥ kuṅkumādyairvimiśritaiḥ .
vilikhenmukhyamūrtyādi yathāśobhaṃ mukhadvaye .. 141 ..
 
sudarśananṛsiṃhābhyāṃ varṇaśobhā samīritā .
karṇikā kanakaprakyā kesarāṇyaruṇāni tu .. 142 ..
 
pāṇḍuraktāni patrāṇi bhūpurāṇi samantataḥ .
kanakābhāni kāryāṇi mūrtīnāṃ prāgudīritam .. 143 ..
 
cakranābidvayaṃ kuryāddhemapūrvāruṇaprabham .
śaradākāśasaṃkāśānyarāṇi aruṇamantaram .. 144 ..
 
hemakundasitaṃ kuryāt kramānnemitrayaṃ śubham .
pītena vā vaḷarkṣeṇa likhenmantrākṣarāṇi vai .. 145 ..
 
pajhakesarapatreṣu bhūpureṣu samantataḥ .
ṣaṭkoṇāntarabāhyeṣu cakranābhyaranemiṣu .. 146 ..
 
pṛthak kṛtāni varṇāni māntrāṇyantarmukhāni ca .
tāradvayāntarasthāni binduyuktāni cāntataḥ .. 147 ..
 
lekhyānyetāni sarvatra mukhyapraṇavasaṃpuṭam .
prākārasamupetāni namaskārānvitāni ca .. 148 ..
 
kuryānnārāyaṇāstrāṇi kūrcāni haritāṇi ca .
baddhāni pajhapāśena tato hayamukhāni ca .. 149 ..
 
bhūrjapatre vilikhyeta kuṃkumāgarujai rasaiḥ .
haricandanakarpūragavyapañcakasādhubhiḥ .. 150 ..
 
suvarṇasūcyā vidhivat samāpya guḷikākṛtim .
suvarṇapaṭṭenāvṛtya pratiṣṭhāpya vidhānataḥ .. 151 ..
 
rakṣyāṇāmāyurārogyadhanadhānyādivṛddhaye .
putrapautrādisantānavijayeṣṭādisiddhaye .. 152 ..
 
dhārayecchirasā mantrī sādhusaṃrakṣaṇe rataḥ .
yantrametat samākhyātaṃ sudarśananṛsiṃhayoḥ .. 153 ..
 
sthāpanaṃ sarvamūrtīnāṃ yathāvat prāgudīritam .
tathaivaitat pratiṣṭhāpya trikālaṃ vaikakālikam .. 154 ..

Chapter - 24
śrīḥ .
caturviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ .
sanakaḥ .
mune samyak samākhyātaṃ sudarśananṛsiṃhayoḥ .
pūrvāparamukhaṃ yantraṃ nānāmantrārṇapūritam .. 1 ..
 
madhyamārabhya mantrāṇāṃ sāṅgānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ param .
nyāsārthamarcanārthaṃ ca samācakṣva yathākramam .. 2 ..
 
śāṇḍilyaḥ .
sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ tvayā prājñārahasyāmnāyalakṣitam .
sanaka tvaṃ śrṛṇuṣvātra mantrajātaṃ yathāsthitam .. 3 ..
 
saṃkarṣaṇāt purā tuṣṭācchaṃkareṇa mayā'pi ca .
hitāya sarvalokānāṃ yantrarūpaṃ guṇottaram .. 4 ..
 
sugupte bhūtale śuddhe varṇacakraṃ paristaret .
akārādikṣakārāntaṃ sarvārṇamayarūpiṇam .. 5 ..
 
svakṣanābhyaranemībhiḥ prathibhiścāpyalaṃkṛtam .
kāraṇaṃ sarvamantrāṇāṃ akṣe praṇavamālikhet .. 6 ..
 
akārādyā visargāntāḥ svarā nābhyaṅgamāśritāḥ .
kakārādīni bhāntāni tadarāṇāṃ triraṣṭake .. 7 ..
 
mādihāntāni nemau tu kṣārṇaṃ prathigaṇe sthitam .
śabdabrahnamayaṃ cakraṃ purā varṇagaṇaṃ tataḥ .. 8 ..
 
praṇavādyairnamontaiśca saṃjñābhiḥ kramaśastataḥ .
vinyasya mātṛkāyantraṃ svaṃ devaṃ vidhivadguruḥ .. 9 ..
 
samabhyarcyārghyapuṣpādyairmātṛkāmantravigraham .
tataḥ samuddharenmantrān sarvābhimatasiddhidān .. 10 ..
 
jetuṃ śaktā'tmano yātu sṛṣṭisthitilayonmukhī .
kiyāśaktiḥ samuddiṣṭā saṃkalpajananī purā .. 11 ..
 
kālarūpamadhiṣṭhāya tayaitadbṛṃhitaṃ jagat .
kālacakraṃ jagajjakraṃ tasmāt saudarśanaṃ vapuḥ .. 12 ..
 
tamadhiṣṭhāya sā śaktirjīvabhūtā vyavasthitā .
vinākṛtaṃ tayā sarvamasatkalpamidaṃ bhavet .. 13 ..
 
tasmāt samuddharecchaktimagnīṣomasamaprabhām .
akṣādhārāṃ tu vai nityāmanādyantāṃ ca vaiṣṇavīm .. 14 ..
 
pūrvaṃ nemyantimadvandvaṃ tadādyaṃ sānaladvayam .
nābhituryāntimadvābhyāṃ piṇḍametadalaṃkṛtam .. 15 ..
 
saudarśanamahāśaktiḥ sarvasiddhipradāyinī .
jīvabhūtā ṣaḍarṇasya prakāśānandarūpiṇī .. 16 ..
 
hṛdayādyaṅgasidhyarthaṃ piṇḍametat svarojjhitam .
dīrghairādyaistribhiścāntyairbhedayennetrapaścimam .. 17 ..
 
praṇavādīni caitāni kuryādvai hṛdayādibhiḥ .
namaḥ svāhā vaṣaḍḍhuṃphaṭvauṣaḍbhirjātibhiḥ saha .. 18 ..
 
kamānniyojanīyāni vijñānādiguṇaiḥ saha .
śakteḥ prakṛtirūpasya ṣaḍarṇasyoddhṛtiṃ śrṛṇu .. 19 ..
 
pūrvavat samupāhṛtya cāntime dvayamantimam .
tatrāṣṭaṃ satṛtīyaṃ syāt sārṇaṃ sāntyaṃtatontimam .. 20 ..
 
sapañcamasvaraṃ tacca kuryānnebhyādyabhūṣitam .
paścādekādaśārārṇayuktaṃ taddviguṇāragam .. 21 ..
 
antyārṇamavimuktaṃ tu kuryāt pañcamaṣaṣṭhayoḥ .
ayaṃ saudarśano mantraḥ ṣaḍarṇaḥ samudīritaḥ .. 22 ..
 
tṛtīyaḥ pañcamaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ pratyekaṃ tryakṣaraḥ smṛtaḥ .
anye'varṇasamopetā varṇāḥ syurdvyakṣarāstrayaḥ .. 23 ..
 
eṣa kālātmano viṣṇorviśvarūpasya vācakaḥ .
satārayā ca śaktyāyamaṣṭārṇaḥ parikīrtitaḥ .. 24 ..
 
kṣetrakṣetrajñayuktyā tu yathā prakṛtigaḥ pumān .
sthūlasa6kṣmātmako dhyeyastathā saudarśano hariḥ .. 25 ..
 
darśanaṃ paratatvasya syāttadākhyānadarśanam .
tanniṣṭhānāmidaṃ nityamajñānatimirāpaham .. 26 ..
 
chinatti saṃśayaṃ teṣāṃ samu pāyapravṛttaye .
rūpāntaramidaṃ tasya saṃśayacchedakāriṇaḥ .. 27 ..
 
nūnaṃ varṇāśramācāraniṣṭhānāmānanena tu .
bhinatti dūṣakān jantūn svakavidyāprabhāvataḥ .. 28 ..
 
lāñchitānāmanenāśu bhaktānāṃ bhāvitātmanām .
karastho vijayastu syādiha loke paratra ca .. 29 ..
 
kiṃ punarviṣaye yantre sthāpite pūjite sati .
mune mantraprabhāvo'yamevamuktaḥ parantapa .. 30 ..
 
lakṣaṇaṃ hṛdayādyasya mantrasyāsya kramācchṛṇu .
prāgeva hṛdayādīnāṃ mantrārṇāni yathākramam .. 31 ..
 
vinyasedbījabhūtāni tārānte bindunā tataḥ .
āvisūnāṃ kramādante tathā sūryākṣaradvayāt .. 32 ..
 
mahāsudarśanajvālāpadayorantime'pi ca .
cakrāyeti padaṃ ṣoḍhā śirontaṃ yojayet kramāt .. 33 ..
 
vijñānādiguṇaupetaiḥ turyāntairhṛdayādibhiḥ .
namaḥ svāhādijātyantaiḥ prāguktavidhinā likhet .. 34 ..
 
dhyeyānyākāravarttīni bogasthāneṣu mūlavat .
varṇabhūṣaṇavastrāstrabhujasaṃsthānaceṣṭitaiḥ .. 35 ..
 
varmāstrejñeyamantrasya caramārṇadvayaṃ smṛtam .
namo nārāyaṇāyeti syādaṣṭārṇaṃ satārakam .. 36 ..
 
asya sāṅgānyupāṅgāni mantrārṇairbindubhuṣitaiḥ .
caramārṇena śeṣāṇi caraṇāntānyapi kramāt .. 37 ..
 
guṇaiśca hṛdayādyaiśca turyādyairjātibhissaha .
svarūpaṃ ṣoḍaśārṇasya mantrasya prāgudīritam .. 38 ..
 
hṛdayādipadāntāni kalpanīyāni pūrvavat .
tatra dvādaśamaṃ bījaṃ huṃphaṭsvāhānta muccaret .. 39 ..
 
vibhorvarāhavaktrasya mantramānuṣṭubhaṃ śrṛṇu .
svarādyaṃ pañcamaṃ varṇamekībhūtaṃ samaṃ purā .. 40 ..
 
prāgvarṇamevamuddhṛtya jātimādyāṃ samāharet .
arāntaṃ tat tṛtīyaṃ ca tadante nemipañcamam .. 41 ..
 
nābhyekādaśamopetamaraṣoḍaśakaṃ tataḥ .
varāharūpāya padaṃ tadūrdhvaṃ vyāhṛtitrayam .. 42 ..
 
pataye padamante'sya bhūpatitvamanantaram .
me dehīti tataḥ paścāddāpayeti padaṃ tataḥ .. 43 ..
 
śirasā saha mantro'yaṃ dvātriṃśārṇaḥ prakīrtitaḥ .
aṅgāni kalpayedasya vibhaktaiḥ pañcadhā padaiḥ .. 44 ..
 
kramaśaḥ saptabhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ saptabhiścātha saptabhiḥ .
pañcabhirvarṇa saṃbhūtaiḥ praṇavādyairguṇottaraiḥ .. 45 ..
 
hṛdayādyastraparyantaisturyāntairjātibhiḥ saha .
aṅgaklṛptiriyaṃ proktā mantrasyāsya sulocana .. 46 ..
 
śaktiḥ svāhāsya bhūrbījaṃ parijñeyaṃ tatopari .
mantraṃ nṛsiharūpasya prāksaṅkhyārṇaṃ samuccaret .. 47 ..
 
puro dayādyaṃ agrāntaṃ nābhyarṇāntādyasaṃyutam .
kavīnāṃ madhyamaṃ pūrvaṃ ramāyāḥ saṃmatāntaram .. 48 ..
 
svāhāntaṃ viṣṭarādyaṃ ca kṛṣṇāntaṃ corupūrvakam .
nābhipañcadaśārṇena saṃyutaṃ tadanantaram .. 49 ..
 
pūjāntaṃ lorghvakaṃ vādyamanantāntaṃ sabindukam .
sahasrādyaṃ apūrvāntaṃ sarvatontamataḥ param .. 50 ..
 
mukuṭādyaṃ mukhāntaṃ ca nemyādyarṇasanvitam .
kinnarāntaramādāya ṛchayādyarṇopari sthitam .. 51 ..
 
asyantaṃ bindusaṃyuktaṃ harerādyaṃ samaṃ tataḥ .
gaṃbhīramadhyaṃ dhiṣaṇamadhyamaṃ karṣaṇāntimam .. 52 ..
 
nābhyantādyena saṃyuktaṃ tato bhadrādyameva ca .
unnidrāntamanusvāraṃ amṛtābhyantaraṃ dvidhā .. 53 ..
 
tayorante'mṛtāntaṃ syāt vāyuṃ tasyopari sthitam .
tato'nnāntyaṃ ramāntaṃ ca ramyāntaṃ haṃ samuddharet .. 54 ..
 
evamānuṣṭubho mantraḥ kīrtito nṛhareḥ paraḥ .
pañcamaṃ sasa kāntādyaṃ bījamasya prakīrtitam .. 55 ..
 
śaktiścaivaṃ savijñeyamindupūrvaṃ sabindukam .
pādaiścaturbhiḥ sarvaiśca praṇavādyairanukramāt .. 56 ..
 
pañcāṅgānyasya mantrasya hṛdayādīni kalpayet .
pādānte yojayedetānanantātmana ucyate .. 57 ..
 
tataḥ priyātmane iti jyotirātmane ityapi .
turyo māyātmane iti mantre candrātmane padam .. 58 ..
 
jñānādihṛdayādīni jātyantāni yathāpurā .
pātāḷanṛharermantraścāṣṭāṣṭākṣara ucyate .. 59 ..
 
kramāt svarāntapūrvābhyāṃ yuktaṃ prathyarṇamuccaret .
aradvidaśakaṃ paścāt nemyādyaṃ protamosvarāt .. 60 ..
 
arāntaṃ ca tṛtīyaṃ ca tadante nemipañcamam .
nābhyekādaśamopetamakṣaraṃ ṣoḍaśāragam .. 61 ..
 
binduyuktaṃ tataḥ śāntaharerekhābhiranvitam .
kuśeśayāntamagnīti ca tadante netra pūrvakam .. 62 ..
 
trāturādyaṃ yaśādyaṃ ca sādyaṃ parvatamadhyamam .
aṣṭārabhaṃ samādāya nemipañcakasaṃsthitam .. 63 ..
 
ravinemipadaṃ paścācchāntādyaṃ yamalādikam .
dvinavāraṃ ca sāntaṃ ca dvayametadvidhoccaran .. 64 ..
 
araikaviṃśaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca dvikametattathoccaran .. 65 ..
 
nemitṛtīyamakṣāntaṃ bhavetāṃ pūrvavaddvidhā .. 66 ..
 
krameṇa bhūṣayedetamante varmāstraśīrṣakaiḥ .. 67 ..
 
pātāḷanṛharermantraḥ catuṣṣaṣṭyarṇakaḥ smṛtaḥ .. 68 ..
 
bījamādyakṣaraṃ proktaṃ śaktiḥ svāhā ca sānugā .. 69 ..
 
aṅgāni kalpayet kṣārṇaiḥ pūrvavat svarabhūṣitaiḥ .. 70 ..
 
ante bindusamopetaiḥ praṇavādyairanukramāt .. 71 ..
 
jñānādyastrāvasānaiśca turyāntairhṛdayādibhiḥ .. 72 ..
 
pūrvavat samupetāni namaḥ svāheti jātibhiḥ .. 73 ..
 
nārasiṃhamathāṣṭārṇamantraṃ sarvārthasiddhidam .. 74 ..
 
namasaḥ praṇavādyasya naretyarṇamathāntime .
siṃhāyeti padānto'yaṃ nṛsiṃhāṣṭārṇa īritaḥ .. 75 ..
 
kṣauṃ bījamasya nābhyarṇastṛtīyaḥ śaktirucyate .
kalpayeddhṛdayādīni bījenaiva yathā purā .. 76 ..
 
kramaśaḥ keśavādīnāṃ mantrāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ śrṛṇu .
navamaṃ cāṣṭamaṃ nemāvarādyaṃ mātṛkāntimam .. 77 ..
 
tridhaikaikaṃ kramāt kṛtvā bījadvādaśakaṃ yathā .
paunaḥ punyena sarveṣāṃ yalavān yojayedadhaḥ .. 78 ..
 
nābhiṣaṣṭhasvarordhvasthānaṅkayedvindunopari .
tārādihṛdayāntāni saṃjñābhisturyayā saha .. 79 ..
 
keśavaḥ prathamo vācyastato nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ .
mādhavaścaiva govindo viṣṇuśca madhusūdanaḥ .. 80 ..
 
trivikramo vāmanākhyaḥ śrīdharaḥ pajhalocanaḥ .
hṛṣīkeśaḥ pajhanābho dāmodara iti śrutaḥ .. 81 ..
 
bījairdīrghasvaropaitaiḥ prāgvadaṅgāni kalpayet .
teṣāṃ śriyādikāntānāṃ śrṛṇu mantrānanukramāt .. 82 ..
 
mātṛkāntaytrayaṃ kṣādyaṃ caturdhā prasterat purā .
viṣvaksuyojyānyarṇāni tvadhobhāge yathākramam .. 83 ..
 
agnyambupṛthivīvārivarhnibhūjvalanā kramāt .
vāridvayaṃ ca somaṃ ca pārthivadvitayaṃ tataḥ .. 84 ..
 
yojayedanalaṃ varṇaṃ ṣaṭsaptāṣṭasu mūrdhani .
adhonavadvādaśayoḥ sarveṣāṃ cordhvataḥ punaḥ .. 85 ..
 
svaraśaktyā sametena nābhyantādyena bhūṣayet .
svarajātyādiyuktāni bījāni hṛdayādayaḥ .. 86 ..
 
bahiścakragadāśārṅgakhaḍgādyairdikṣu bheditāḥ .
viṣṇavo vāsudevādyā eteṣāṃ vācakān śraṇu .. 87 ..
 
ādye cānte svare nābhau samuddhṛtya satārake .
pūrve cakradharāyeti saṃjñayā viṣṇave namaḥ .. 88 ..
 
anye gadādharāyeti tṛtīye śārṅgadhāriṇe .
khaṅgadhāriṇa ityante caturthasya niyojayet .. 89 ..
 
dviṣaṭkārṇena coddiṣṭā viṣṇaūnāṃ vācakāḥ pṛthak .
sāṅgānyupāṅgānyeteṣāṃ mantrādyaiḥ prāgvadācaret .. 90 ..
 
bījāni yāni viṣṇūnāṃ vilomena svarāntimān .
tānyuktāni hṛṣīkeśavyūhānāṃ samudīritāḥ .. 91 ..
 
janārdhanānāṃ vakṣyante mantrāḥ prācyānalāntarāt .
ikārādīni catvāri caikārādīnyanukramāt .. 92 ..
 
kuryāt praṇavapūrvāṇi teṣāmante yathā purā .
pūrvaṃ daṇḍadharāyeti sarveṣāṃ namasā nyaset .. 93 ..
 
hṛdādicaraṇāntāni mantrārṇaistu yathā purā .
nṛsiṃhakroḍayormantraste prāgeva pradarśitaḥ .. 94 ..
 
antasthāśca tatoṣṭārṇo varṇānte ca svarā halaḥ .
suprasiddhāḥ samākhyātāstvaparāṅge nibodha tu .. 95 ..
 
sudarśanaṣaḍarṇasya prāksthamarṇacatuṣṭayam .
purāhṛtya tataḥ paścāttannetrādye calāntime .. 96 ..
 
nemisthaṃ pañcamaṃ vraṇaṃ araṣoḍaśakopari .
neminābhyostṛtīye ca viyojya tadanantaram .. 97 ..
 
nemyādyaṃ sānalaṃ hāntaṃ nābhyantā ttaddvayāṅkitam .
piṇḍametannṛsiṃhasya viddyudvarṇasamanvitam .. 98 ..
 
siṃhāntyaṃ hṛdayādyaṃ ca dvidhoddhṛtya dvayaṃ tataḥ .
varmāstre ca śiro jātyāyukteyaṃ dvinavākṣaram .. 99 ..
 
asyaiva daśāmo bījaṃ hanādyaṃ śaktirucyate .
ṣaḍaṅgamasya tārādyaṃ hṛdayādyaṃ kramācchṛṇu .. 100 ..
 
auṃkārarahitaṃ bījaṃ ṣoḍhā kṛtvā yathā purā .
svarairādyairvisargāntairnapuṃsakavivarjitaiḥ .. 101 ..
 
yojayitvā tadūrdhve tu padāni kramaśo nyaset .
cakrarājapadaṃ pūrve jvālācakrapadaṃ tataḥ .. 102 ..
 
jagaccakrapadaṃ paścādasurāntakasaṃjñitam .
pañcamaṃ dīptacakrākhyamante māhāsudarśanam .. 103 ..
 
caturthyantaṃ niyojyānte paścājjñānādibhistathā .
turyāntairhṛdayādyaiśca svāhādyābhiśca cātibhiḥ .. 104 ..
 
dvādaśārṇe nṛsiṃhasya bījaṃ pūrvaṃ mune śrṛṇu .
nemisaptamamādāya prāgarārṇopalakṣitam .. 105 ..
 
yuktaṃ svarāntyapūrvābhyāṃ kuryādbījaṃ paraṃ tvidam .
natipraṇavamadyasthamekavīraṃ mahāprabham .. 106 ..
 
sarveṣāṃ siṃhamantrāṇāṃ dhyānabhedātmanāmidam .
jīvabhūtaṃ svarūpasya vācakaṃ viddhi kāmadam .. 107 ..
 
mūrtimantrān śrṛṇuṣvātha dvādaśākṣaramaṇḍitam .
praṇavaṃ hārdayījātiḥ turyāntaṃ bhagavatpadam .. 108 ..
 
nārasiṃhāya dadyādvai padaṃ pañcākṣaraṃ tataḥ .
viśvattrātṛnṛsiṃhasya mantreyaṃ dvādaśākṣaraḥ .. 109 ..
 
tārāntasyeda ..................daśākṣaraḥ .
vakṣyante hṛdayādīni netrāntāni yathākramam .. 110 ..
 
ṣoḍhāsya bījaṃ tārādyamākārādisamanvitam .
bindunāṅkitameteṣāṃ yojanaṃ prāgvadācaret .. 111 ..
 
ahgopāhgamayī vyāptiḥ savījairdvādaśākṣaraiḥ .
sabindubhirguṇādyaiśca kalpayaṃ vā natibhiḥ saha .. 112 ..
 
vyāpako'yaṃ nṛsiṃhasya mūrtibhedagatasya ca .
sāṅgo mantraḥ samuddiṣṭaḥ sarvābhimatasiddhidaḥ .. 113 ..
 
akṣamadhyagatā varṇā varṇitāścakramadhyagāḥ .
saṃjñāḥ sabinduprāgvarṇā natipraṇavamadhyagāḥ .. 114 ..
 
turyāntāśśaktisaṃghasya jayādyasya tu vācakāḥ .
bhīmogrābhyāṃ ca bhūtābhyāṃ tathā mantradvayaṃ bhavet .. 115 ..
 
viṣṭare'bhiniviṣṭānāṃ mantrāṇāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ śrṛṇu .
sādhyanāmasvarūpaṃ tu vyāpakaṃ vakṣyate punaḥ .. 116 ..
 
tārānte bījaṃ śaktiśca daivataṃ tasya cettataḥ .
śāntiṃ puṣṭiṃ ca vaśyaṃ ca vijayaṃ caivamādikam .. 117 ..
 
dvitīyāntaṃ samuccārya kuruvīpsānvitaṃ tataḥ .
yaṃccha yaccha padāntaṃ vā prākasthitaiḥ praṇavāntimaiḥ .. 118 ..
 
aṅkayedavasāne ca sādhyalakṣaṇamīritam .
dviraṣṭavarṇaṃ nṛharermantramānuṣṭubhaṃ param .. 119 ..
 
pūrvameva samuddiṣṭhaṃ bāhye vāyavyamakṣaram .
varmāstrajātiyuktaṃ ca vāhnaṃ pārthivamakṣaram .. 120 ..
 
vistareṇa purā proktaṃ tasmānneha pratanyate .
vakṣyate yantra dhartṝṇāṃ nāgānāṃ kṣādyamānvitam .. 121 ..
 
bindusvarānvitaṃ bījaṃ praṇavādyaṃ tataḥ param .
yuktaṃ pratyekasaṃjñābhisturyāntābhirnamo'ntimam .. 122 ..
 
iti śeṣādināgānāṃ mantrā samyagudīritāḥ .
śaktyā satārayā yāntraiḥ saudarśanaṣaḍakṣaraiḥ .. 123 ..
 
ekaikaṃ bhedayedvarṇamaṣṭārṇasyordhvato'pyadhaḥ .
nārāyaṇāstramantro'yaṃ kalpāntahutabhukprabhaḥ .. 124 ..
 
abhidhāyākṣaraṃ pūrvaṃ cakrādyastragaṇasya tu .
yuktaṃ vahnivisargābhyāṃ bījaṃ vā praṇavānvitam .. 125 ..
 
tataḥ saṃjñā caturthyantā yojanīyā phaḍantimā .
cakrādiṣoḍaśāstrāṇāmiti mantrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ .. 126 ..
 
jñātvaivaṃ yantramāhātmyaṃ yorcayedvidhipūrvakam .
digbandha vahṇiprākāra gāyatryā vāhanādikaiḥ .. 127 ..
 
yāgopakaraṇairmantrairbhoga dāna vivarjitaiḥ .
kramāt sarvaphalāvāptirmantrasiddhiśca jāyate .. 128 ..
 
daśadigbandhamantrāṇāṃ vakṣyate lakṣaṇaṃ purā .
oṃ pūrvaṃ puruṣāyeti svāhāntaṃ tadanantaram .. 129 ..
 
astreṇa bandhayāmīti svāhāntaṃ ca ṣaḍakṣaram .
iti digbandhamantro'yamīrito duṣṭadoṣahṛt .. 130 ..
 
praṇavaṃ prāk samuddhṛtya manuṃ vāgnijāyayoḥ .
āyāntaṃ vinyaseccakraṃagniprākārasaṃjñitam .. 131 ..
 
kīrtitāṃ cakragāyatrīṃ śrṛṇu cakraprasādanīm .
jātipūrvaṃ puraskṛtya cakrāyeti samuddharet .. 132 ..
 
dvitīyaṃ viṣṇugāyatryā nṛsūktādyakṣaratrayam .
tetrābyāṃ padamādāya nemipūrbāntayojitam .. 133 ..
 
dhīmahīti tadante no viniveśyo'nivāritaḥ .
gāyatryantaṃ samuddhārya tadante caturakṣaram .. 134 ..
 
saudarśanī samuddiṣṭhā gāyatrī tārakākṣarā .
satārakā purā ceyaṃ bhavedekākṣarādhikā .. 135 ..
 
tāradvayaṃ puroddhṛtya paramaṃ padamuddharet .
dhāmetivasthitaṃ cātha nemyādyaṃ dvinavārakam .. 136 ..
 
dvidaśāragataṃ varṇaṃ nābhipañcamamūrdhani .
tatastu gṛhakāmyayo iti pañcārṇamuddharet .. 137 ..
 
yutaṃ nemidvitīyena dvinavāragataṃ tataḥ .
ṣoḍaśāragataṃ varṇaṃ dvitīyasvarasaṃyutam .. 138 ..
 
nemipañcamavarṇaṃ ca ṣoḍaśāragataṃ punaḥ .
nābhidvitīyasaṃbhinnaṃ nemyantaṃ tārapaścimam .. 139 ..
 
tṛtīyasvarasaṃyuktaṃ tṛtīyaṃ nemimaṇḍalāt .
nemyantamāsvaropetamarāntaṃ ca svarāntaram .. 140 ..
 
svaraṃ tṛtīyaṃ saṃyojya tataśca dvinavāragam .
nyūnaviṃśāragordhvaṃ taddvinavākṣaramūrdhani .. 141 ..
 
svaraṃ tṛtīyaṃ saṃyojya tataśca dvinavāragam .
punarmantraśarīreti praṇavāntaṃ tato namaḥ .. 142 ..
 
punaśca namasā yukto mantra āvāhanocitaḥ .
pradāne sarvabhogānāṃ mantraste saṃprakāśyate .. 143 ..
 
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuccārya sarvabhogaikakāraṇam .
nemyantaṃ bindusaṃyuktaṃ tridhedaṃ padamapyatha .. 144 ..
 
gṛhāṇeti śiro'ntoyaṃ bhogadānasya vācakaḥ .
āvāhane tathārcāyāṃ visarjanavidhau tathā .. 145 ..
 
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuddhṛtya saṃbodhya bhagavanniti .
mantramūrtepadaṃ dadyāt svapadaṃ ca dvitīyayā .. 146 ..
 
āsādaya kṣamasveti praṇavāntaṃ samuddharet .
paraprayuktamantrāṇāṃ śaktihrāsanatatparaḥ .. 147 ..
 
samastavīryamantrāḍhyaṃ mune mantravaraṃ śrṛṇu .
praṇavaṃ pūrvamuddhṛtya praṇavādyaṃ sabindukam .. 148 ..
 
ṣaḍarṇasyāstramantraprākṣaḍarṇaṃ praṇavojjhitam .
proktasyārṇadvayaṃ pūrvaṃ cakrarājapadaṃ tataḥ .. 149 ..
 
sarvaśabdaṃ dahadvandūpūrvaṃ duṣṭabhayaṃkaram .
cintāmūlaṃ padaṃ paścādbhindi bhindīti vai tataḥ .. 150 ..
 
dvidhā vidāraya padaṃ mantraṃ hrāsaya hrāsaya .
bhakṣayeti padadvandvaṃ bhūtānīti tataḥ param .. 151 ..
 
trāsaya trāsayetyante varmāstre ca śirontime .
ekasaptatimantro'yaṃ śaktihrāsākhya īritaḥ .. 152 ..
 
mantramānuṣṭubhaṃ vakṣye sarveṣāmabhayapradam .
bhagavanniti saṃbodhya sarveti padamuddharet .. 153 ..
 
vijayeti padaṃ paścāt sahastrāreti tatparam .
aparājiteti śaraṇaṃ padaṃ tvāmityanantaram .. 154 ..
 
prapanno'smīti tatpaścāddvitīyāntaścaśrīkaram .
śrīpadādyaṃ tataḥ paścāt sudarśanamiti kramāt .. 155 ..
 
prapattiriti vikhyātā sarbapāpakṣayaṃkarī .
vakṣye nṛsihyagāyatrīmaparāṅgasya pūjane .. 156 ..
 
vajreti dvyakṣaraṃ pūrvaṃśrṛṅkhalāyetyataḥ param .
āyāntaṃ tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭreti vijhaheti padaṃ tataḥ .. 157 ..
 
vajreti dvyakṣarasyānte nakhāyeti ca dhīmahi .
ādyaṃ ca caramādyaṃ ca gāyatryāḥ padamuddharet .. 158 ..
 
siṃheti savisargaṃ ca gāyatryantaṃ tato nyaset .
ācareduktamantrābhyāmāvāhanavisarjane .. 159 ..
 
digbandhaṃ ca sahāstreṇa prāguktena samācaret .
anyeṣāmaṅgamantrāṇāṃ viniyogo yathā purā .. 160 ..
 
iti nigaditametanmantrajālaṃ yathāva .
nmukhayugaḷasamete yantrarāje niviṣṭam .. 161 ..
 
hṛdibahirapi bhogairyāni yojyāni tāni .
prakaṭayatu kadācit kaṣṭabuddheḥ parasya .. 162 ..

Chapter - 25
śrīḥ .
pañcaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ .
sanakaḥ .
bhagavan samyagākhyātaṃ sudarśananṛsihnayoḥ .
mantrarūpaṃ mahāyantraṃ bhajatāmīpsitapradam .. 1 ..
 
tasmādbhajanarūpaṃ ca vada sānugraho'si me .
śāṇḍilya .
hitāya sarvalokānāṃ yantrametadudāhṛtamū .. 2 ..
 
vidhinā pūjito yena sarvaṃ tena samāpyate .
mayā te śrotukāmāya vaṣyate yajanakramaḥ .. 3 ..
 
prāgvatsnānādikaṃ kṛtvā praviśya yajanālayam .
prakṣālya pādāvācamya sottarīyaḥ svalaṃkṛtaḥ .. 4 ..
 
dhṛtordhvapuṇḍraḥ kusumaiḥ dvārsathānabhyarcya pūrvavat .
kavāṭoddhāṭanaṃ kṛtvā praviśyābhyantare vibhum .. 5 ..
 
praṇipatya ca gāyatryā pāṇiprakṣāḷanādimam .
arcāyāṃ viṣṭare yantre kṛtvā mārgatrayaṃ tataḥ .. 6 ..
 
prāsādaṃ śodhayitvā'sya purataḥ phalakādike .
prokṣite cāstramantreṇa saṃmukhaṃ rucirāsane .. 7 ..
 
samāsīnaḥ svapārśvastha yājñīyaṃ cādhivāsanam .
karaśuddhiṃ sthānaśuddhiṃ kṛtvā'streṇa yathāpuram .. 8 ..
 
pāṇibhyāmuktamantreṇa saṃyuktenāstramudrayā .
pūjāsthānagadān vighnān bāhyato'dṛśyavigrahān .. 9 ..
 
virecya bandhanaṃ kuryāt dikṣu caiva vidikṣu ca .
kavacenāvakuṇṭhyātha prāṇānāyamya pūrvavat .. 10 ..
 
tatvāni copasaṃhṛtya dehasthānyātmanā saha .
sarvatatvavinirmuktaṃ vigrahaṃ kevalaṃ tataḥ .. 11 ..
 
śodhayeddhāraṇābhiśca śoṣaṇādyābhirūrdhvataḥ .
turyādyante pade devaṃ sudarśanatanuṃ smaret .. 12 ..
 
balātmanā'sya marutā kavacena tanuṃ svakām .
śoṣayitvā daheddehaṃ dakṣāṃguṣṭhādya ṣataḥ .. 13 ..
 
kalpāntapāvakajvālā sahasrāyutadīdhitim .
bhāvayitvā śikhāmantraṃ tena dagdhamanusmaret .. 14 ..
 
dṛnmantraṃ pūrṇacandrābhamamṛtāsāravarṣiṇam .
vāmāṃguṣṭhāgrato dhyātvā secitaṃ tena bhāvayet .. 15 ..
 
viniyuktāṃstato mantrān varmādyāṃ choṣaṇādiṣu .
mantreśvare layaṃ yātāniti sañcintya bhāvayet .. 16 ..
 
ānandāmṛtasaṃpūrṇaśītāṃśuśatasaprabham .
tatprāntairamṛtaughaiśca bṛṃhitāṃ bhāvayettanum .. 17 ..
 
tasmāttatvāni vinyasya saṃhṛtāni yathākramam .
svātmanā tāmadhiṣṭhāya mantranyāsaṃ samācaret .. 18 ..
 
akārādikṣakārāntamātṛkāṃ mantramātaram .
vinayset karayoḥ pūrvaṃ vigrahecakramāllapan .. 19 ..
 
kṛtvaivaṃ vyāpakanyāsamādityātapasaprabhaḥ .
dakṣetarakrameṇaiva śākhāsu talayorapi .. 20 ..
 
aṃguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhāntamekaikasyāscatuścatuḥ .
evaṃ dviviṃśakaṃ nyasya talayordaśakaṃ tataḥ .. 21 ..
 
madhye ca tri catuṣke ca pañcakaṃ pañcakaṃ tathā .
praṇavadvayamadhyasthānyevaṃ nyastvā karadvaye .. 22 ..
 
vyāpakanyāsapūrvaṃ tu svaśarīre'pi vinyaset .
mūrdhnaḥ pādatalaṃ yāvat pāṇibyāṃ tapanāṃśuvat .. 23 ..
 
vyāpayitvā tato nyāsaṃ pṛthageva samācaret .
keśānte vaktravṛtte ca netrayoḥ śravaṇadvaye .. 24 ..
 
ghrāṇarandhradvaye gaṇḍadvaye dakṣetarakramāt .
uttarādharayogena dantayostacchadadvaye .. 25 ..
 
mūrdhni nyaset svarānanyān savisargānanantaram .
kavargaṃ dakṣiṇe bāhau sandhipañcagataṃ kramāt .. 26 ..
 
vāme tathā cavargaṃ ca pādayordakṣiṇāditaḥ .
sandhigau ṭatavargau ca pūrvavattundapārśvayoḥ .. 27 ..
 
pṛṣṭhe nābhau ca hṛdaye pavargaṃ dhātusaptake .
yādisāntāni varṇāni hakāraṃ hṛdayāntare .. 28 ..
 
kṣakāraṃ hṛdayākāśe nyastvaivaṃ mātṛkāṃ purā .
tataḥ śaktyā paḍarṇaṃ tu nyaset karaśarīragam .. 29 ..
 
karanyāsaṃ purāviddhi tacchṛṇuṣva munīśvara .
puṭīkṛtena tārābhyāṃ mantreṇaiva śaśaktinā .. 30 ..
 
nakhāntaṃ maṇibandhādyaṃ prāgvat pāṇidvayaṃ mṛjet .
ādyante tāraśaktyāḍhcaiḥ ṣaḍbhirvarṇaiḥ sabindukaiḥ .. 31 ..
 
aṅguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhāntaṃ nyastvā madhyamaparvasu .
vinyaset karajāgreṣu caramaṃ varṇameva ca .. 32 ..
 
evamarṇāni vinyasya hṛdayādīni vinyaset .
mūlāgraparvasvaṅgāni varṇanyāsakrameṇa tu .. 33 ..
 
pāṇibhyāmālabheddehamāmūrdhnaścaraṇāvadhi .
kṛtvaivaṃ vyāpakanyāsamaṅganyāsaṃ samācaret .. 34 ..
 
mūrdhni vaktre ca hṛdaye nābhau guhye ca pādayoḥ .
sṛṣṭinyāso bhavedeṣa syādaṅgopāṅgavat sthitiḥ .. 35 ..
 
pādayorguhyake nābhau hṛdi vaktre ca mūrdhani .
pādādiśca śiro'ntstu saṃhṛtinyāsa ucyate .. 36 ..
 
hṛdi mūrdhni śikhāyāṃ tu skandhayoḥ karamadhyataḥ .
netrayornyasanīyāni svairmantrairuditaiḥ kramāt .. 37 ..
 
hṛdayādīni vinyasya paścāt pāṇitaladvaye .
vinaysedastrasaṃghaṃ ca aṣṭakaṃ vā dviraṣṭakam .. 38 ..
 
kirīṭaṃ kaustubhaṃ mālāṃ śrīvatsaṃ ca yathāpuram .
dakṣiṇottarayoraṃse icchāśaktiṃ svapārśvayoḥ .. 39 ..
 
ūrumūle manastatvaṃ nyastvā mantramayaṃ svakam .
bhāvayedahamityantaḥ sudarśanavapurhariḥ .. 40 ..
 
gāyatryā vartayedbāhye svātmānaṃ cakramudrayā .
cakrajvālāvaliṃ vipra parito maṃtravittamaḥ .. 41 ..
 
bhāvanājanitaṃ yāgamācaredādicoditam .
niyamya karaṇagrāmaṃ prāgvad vai jñānagocare .. 42 ..
 
āsanaṃ kalpayenmāntramāmūlādhṛdayāvadhi .
ādhāraśakterārabhya cidbhāvāsanapaścimam .. 43 ..
 
puroktaṃ bāvayedūrdhve mantraiśvaryaṃ triviṣṭapam .
sādhāraṇamidaṃ jñeyaṃ sudarśananṛsiṃhayoḥ .. 44 ..
 
pṛṣṭhabhāge'vatīrṇābhyāṃ bahirvā hṛdayāmbare .
viṣṭarāsanasahkalpakārye bhāvāpanopahṛt .. 45 ..
 
hṛtpajhakarṇikordhvasthā śabdabrahnamayī purā .
akṣagarbhagataṃ nādaṃ nadantī mantragarbhitam .. 46 ..
 
śaktiḥ śāntātmano viṣṇoḥ sādhakaiśca vaśīkṛtā .
śabdaśaktiḥ samudgītā viṣṭarārkakhamadhyagā .. 47 ..
 
varṇatvaṃ samanuprāptā santatirnādarūpiṇī .
akārādikṣakārāntavarṇapārāvasānataḥ .. 48 ..
 
nistaraṅge pare vyomni kalanārahite śubhe .
turyātīte pade devaḥ prakāśānandabṛṃhitaḥ .. 49 ..
 
sadbrahnavāsudevākhyaḥ pūrṇaṣāḍguṇyavigrahaḥ .
mahāvibhūtisaṃpūrṇaḥ savaśaktimayaḥ prabhuḥ .. 50 ..
 
saṃśāntaparamānandasvarūpaḥ satatoditaḥ .
śaṅkhacakrāhkitanurvaradābhayapāṇikaḥ .. 51 ..
 
sahasrasūryasaṅkāśaḥ sahasrendugabhastimān .
svaprakāśaiḥ kirīṭādyaiḥ nūpurāntairalaṃkṛtaḥ .. 52 ..
 
śrīvatsakaustubhopeto vanamālāvirājitaḥ .
pītakauśeyabasanaḥ prasannavadanekṣaṇaḥ .. 53 ..
 
dantapaṃktiśaśijyotsnāvidyotitadigantaraḥ .
sevitaśca śriyā puṣṭyā viśeṣābyāṃ samantataḥ .. 54 ..
 
śaṅkhacakrādidivyāstraiḥ sarvatattvātmakaiḥ sadā .
vijñānabhāvanābhāvyo nirāśīḥkarmakāribhiḥ .. 55 ..
 
abhyāsayogasiddhyarthaṃ bahirantaśca nityaśaḥ .
bimbapīṭhādiklṛpteṣu vṛttisthāneṣu teṣu ca .. 56 ..
 
paravyūhādirūpeṇa pūjitaḥ sarvamṛcchati .
tato nityoditastatvāt prakāśāhlādalakṣaṇāt .. 57 ..
 
sādharmyalakṣaṇaṃ prāpya bhaktānugrahakāmyayā .
kriyāśaktimadhiṣṭhāya ja gaduddharaṇodyatām .. 58 ..
 
cidaṃśaṃ prādurabhavat prakāśānandabṛṃhitam .
durdarśanaṃ prakāśena sādhusantāpakāriṇām .. 59 ..
 
āhlādena svabhaktānāṃ sudarśanamitīritam .
ṣaḍadhvordhvagato devo bhūtvā kālānalātmanā .. 60 ..
 
bhaktānāṃ duritaṃ hanti cintito nṛharirhariḥ .
yena saṃpūjitāvetau tejasātīva nirbharau .. 61 ..
 
sa tejasvī ca bhū tātmā sarvatra ca sukhī bhavet .
jñātvaivaṃ mantrasadbhāvamārabhedyajanakriyām .. 62 ..
 
parasmādbhagavattatvāccitsvarūpaṃ parātmakam .
manasā mantramuccārya viṣṭarordhve'vatārya ca .. 63 ..
 
vācyavācakabhāvena dvidhā saudarśanaṃ vapuḥ .
sākāro vācyarūpaḥ syānmantrarūpastu vācakaḥ .. 64 ..
 
praśastau tāvubhau syātāṃ parāparavibhāgataḥ .
vācyarūpaṃ paraṃ vidyādaparaṃ mantrayantritam .. 65 ..
 
jñātvaivamudayaṃ kuryāt parasūkṣmādibhāvanam .
jyotīrūpaṃ paraṃ vidyāt nādāntāhlādalakṣaṇam .. 66 ..
 
cicchaktilakṣaṇaṃ sūkṣmaṃ śiraḥpāṇyādigarbhitam .
liṅgamātraṃ prakāśāḍhcaṃ bhāviprasaradharmi yat .. 67 ..
 
saḥ sthūlo vyaktarūpaḥ syādvācyavācakarūpayoḥ .
mantrāṇāṃ śabdarūpāṇāṃ tisro'vasthāḥ parādikāḥ .. 68 ..
 
paśyantyādyāḥ parijñeyāḥ svaṃ paraṃ tvaparaṃ tridhā .
ādyastatraiva tāraḥ syāddvitīyo bījasaṃjñitaḥ .. 69 ..
 
tṛtīyaḥ padamantrādyastviti bhāvyo bhavennṛbhiḥ .
sānnidhyaṃ saṃmukhībhāvaḥ sannirodho'pi pūrvavat .. 70 ..
 
mantranyāsādikaṃ kṛtvā layabhogārcanaṃ tathā .
sakarṇikesaradaḷasaṃyukteṣvambujeṣvapi .. 71 ..
 
bhūpurādiṣu sarvatra mantrāṇāṃ liṅgarūpiṇām .
mūrtīnāṃ keśavādīnāṃ mantrāṇāmarcanaṃ tataḥ .. 72 ..
 
prāguktairvidhivanmantrairbhogayāgavadācaret .
śirordhve devadevasya bhāvayedindumaṇḍalam .. 73 ..
 
tatsrutairamṛtaughaiśca kuryādarghyādikalpanam .
ṣoḍaśairupacārairvā dviguṇairvā caturguṇaiḥ .. 74 ..
 
rājavatprīṇanaṃ kṛtvā homaṃ kuryāttathāvidham .
nābhicakrakṛte kuṇḍe ṣaṭkoṇe guṇamekhale .. 75 ..
 
nirmathya bhāvanodbhatāmaraṇiṃ jñānarajjunā .
samutpādya ca cidvahniṃ sarvasaṃskārasaṃskṛtam .. 76 ..
 
sadaivordhvaśikhaṃ dīptaṃ śuddhaṃ bhagavadātmakam .
nābikuṇḍagataṃ jñātvā tejaḥ śaktyupabṛṃhitam .. 77 ..
 
hṛdabjagaganordhvasthaṃ mūlamantraṃ samuccaret .
plutadhyānasamopetaṃ satyānte'smin layaṃ gate .. 78 ..
 
nistaraṅge pare prāpte brahnasthaṃ pūrṇavāritaiḥ .
dhyānasruveṇa cāhṛtya sandhimārge'mṛtādhvanā .. 79 ..
 
hṛdayādavatīrṇasya jvālāgrāvasthitasya ca .
mantranāthasya śirasi vasudhārāmiva kṣipet .. 80 ..
 
cidagnimevaṃ santarpya jvālāgrāvasthitaṃ prabhum .
hṛdabjakarṇikāntasthaṃ bhūyo bhāvyāhutikriyāḥ .. 81 ..
 
samāpya vidhivat pūjāmaparāṅge hariṃ sthitam .
svamantreṇārcayitvā'tha homāntaṃ bhāvanāmṛtaiḥ .. 82 ..
 
tadante yantrarūpasya mukhadvayagatasya ca .
pantrasaṃghasya pūrṇāntaṃ kṛtvā santarpaṇaṃ tataḥ .. 83 ..
 
viṣṭarasthaṃ yajedbāhye tvarcārūpamukhadvaye .
mūrtairarghyāṃdibhirbhogairvidhivatsamupāhṛtaiḥ .. 84 ..
 
prāgvadarghyādipātrāṇāṃ pūjanaṃ sthāpanaṃ tathā .
daihavinyastamantrāṇāṃ garbhadvārasthapūjanam .. 85 ..
 
dhātāraṃ ca vidhātāraṃ pracaṇḍaṃ caṇḍapūrvakam .
pūrvapaścimayorbāhyamaṇṭapadvārayoḥ kramāt .. 86 ..
 
jayaṃ ca vijayaṃ cātha subhadraṃ cātha bhadrakam .
sūryācandramasau pūjyau dakṣetaragavākṣayoḥ .. 87 ..
 
kṛtvaivaṃ dvārayāgaṃ tu praviśyābhyantaraṃ tataḥ .
ādhāraśakterārabhya yantraviṣṭarapaścimam .. 88 ..
 
mantramāsanamabyarcya gaṇanāthādikaṃ tathā .
pratiṣṭhitasya devasya kuryādāvāhanaṃ tataḥ .. 89 ..
 
bimbahṛtkamalākāśāccaitanyamamalaṃ param .
prakāśānandarūpaṃ ca nityoditamanūpamam .. 90 ..
 
karṇikāmadhyamāśritya niviṣṭamanubhāvayet .
mūlamantraṃ samuccārya prabuddhaṃ bhāsvaraṃ tataḥ .. 91 ..
 
mantranyāsaṃ tataḥ kuryādyathā dehe svake tathā .
sthāneṣu hṛdayādīni cakrādyastravarāṇi ca .. 92 ..
 
bhūṣaṇādīni vinyasya mastakādeḥ samāni ca .
ratnarāśiprakāśāni layākhyenārcayettataḥ .. 93 ..
 
karṇikādiṣu yantrasthān bhāsvadrūpāṃstathaiva ca .
āsanādyaiśca sāṃspaśairhṛdayaṃgamapaścimaiḥ .. 94 ..
 
prīṇayitvā vidhānena mūrtisaṅghasamanvitam .
japtvā mantraṃ yathāśakti tannivedya yathā purā .. 95 ..
 
pāścātyayantramadhyasthamevaṃ narahariṃ tataḥ .
sāṅgaṃ saparivāraṃ ca sayantrārṇaṃ samarcayet .. 96 ..
 
iti saṅkṣepataḥ proktaṃ mahāyantrārcanaṃ param .
prīṇayedagnimadhyasthaṃ samidbhiḥ prāgudīritaiḥ .. 97 ..

Chapter - 26
śrīḥ .
ṣaḍviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ .
sanakaḥ .
pañcarātrārthatatvajña bhagavan bhavināṃ priya .
mayyanugrahabuddhayā tvamagnimadhyagatārcanam .. 1 ..
 
yathāvidhi samācakṣva sarvasiddhiprasādhanam .
śāṇḍilya .
munīndra sakalaprājña siddhimokṣapradaṃ śubham .. 2 ..
 
kuṇḍamadhyagataṃ yāgaṃ śrṛṇu vakṣye samāhitaḥ .
homārthaṃ maṇṭapaṃ kuryādvitataṃ vahnidiggatam .. 3 ..
 
dhūmarnigamanopetaṃ gavākṣagaṇamaṇḍitam .
tanmadhye vedikā kāryā caturaśrā catuṣkarā .. 4 ..
 
dvādaśāṅgulamānoccā prāsādāsanalakṣaṇā .
cakrābjalakṣaṇaṃ kuṇḍaṃ tadūrdhve kalpayecchubham .. 5 ..
 
madhye sūtratrayaṃ dadyāt prākpratyagdakṣiṇottaram .
hastadvayena tanmadhye caturaśraṃ prakalpya ca .. 6 ..
 
ekādaśāṅgulāyāmaṃ sūtraṃ saṃsthāpya madhyataḥ .
khātārthaṃ vṛttamāpādya bahirāvṛtiyogataḥ .. 7 ..
 
tyajedaṅgulamoṣṭhasya dvyaṅgulaṃ karṇikāvaneḥ .
aṅgulaṃ kesarāṇāṃ ca dvyaṅgulaṃ patrasantateḥ .. 8 ..
 
tadagrasyāṅgulaṃ jñeyaṃ nābherekāṅgulonnatam .
dvyaṅgulaṃ syādarakṣetraṃ nemerekāhgulaṃ bhavet .. 9 ..
 
dvyaṅgulaṃ mekhalāyāḥ syādevamāvṛtiyogataḥ .
mānamākhātaparyantaṃ mekhalāntaṃ hṛdi sthitam .. 10 ..
 
kṛtvā'tha nemiparyantaṃ kṣetrāṇāṃ vṛttatāṃ nayet .
mekhalā sarvabāhyasthā syātturyāśrā yathā bhavet .. 11 ..
 
samekhalaṃ dvihastaṃ tannirmāṇamadhunā śrṛṇu .
khātārthamantarāvṛttādantaraṃ nikhanet samam .. 12 ..
 
tripādamardhaṃ pādaṃ vā bāhyato daśanacchadāt .
sādhayet karṇikādīni nemyantāni yathākramam .. 13 ..
 
dbādaśāṃgulamānoccā kāryā syāt karṇikāntarā .
vistārasadṛśocchrāyā bāhyataḥ kesarānvitā .. 14 ..
 
yathābhimatasaṅkhyāni pajhapatrāṇi sādhayet .
pajhasaṅkhyāsamaṃ kṣetraṃ mahāpajhasamantataḥ .. 15 ..
 
kesarabhramakuṇḍena patrāgrabhramaṇāvadhi .
pakṣamadhyamasūtrāṇi prākpratyagdikṣu pātayet .. 16 ..
 
daḷamadhyagasūtreṇa daḷamadhyordhvagāminā .
daḷamadhyaprasādārthaṃ lāñchayedardhacandravat .. 17 ..
 
candraśrṛṅgaṃ ca madhyaṃ ca patrāgre saṅgatāni ca .
pakṣasūtreṇa patrāgraṃ janayet kuliśāgravat .. 18 ..
 
daḷasaṅkhyāsametāni svakṣetrāṇi ca sādhayet .
vibhajya daḷavat kṣetraṃ sūtrāṇyāsphālayettathā .. 19 ..
 
aṣṭadhā vā'tha ṣoḍhā vā kṛtvaikaikaṃ krabheṇa tu .
santyajya pārśvagau bhāgau bāhyasūtrasya madhyataḥ .. 20 ..
 
sthāpitābhyāṃ ca sūtrābhyāṃ gadābhyāmagramadhyamāt .
matsyavallāñchanaṃ kuryādyāvanmūlabhramāvadhi .. 21 ..
 
prathayo nemibhūmiṣṭhāḥ kāryāścordhve'thavā bahiḥ .
saṃsādhayedathāmadyādiṣṭakābhirmṛdā saha .. 22 ..
 
mekhalāvadhiparyantaṃ nīcānyaṅgāni mīlayet .
vistārocchrāyatulyāni samāni sudṛḍhāni ca .. 23 ..
 
karṇikākesarordhvasthā yoniḥ pippalapatravat .
jihvayā saṃspṛśantyoṣṭhaṃ kāryā yonyupamāśritā .. 24 ..
 
kesarāvanimākramya pṛṣṭhatordhvāṅgulena tu .
pārśvayormadhyasūtrasya bālacandradvayopamā .. 25 ..
 
pronnatā karṇikābūmaiḥ pṛṣṭhataścāṅgulena tu .
āmūlādagraparyantaṃ kramānnimnā gajoṣṭhavat .. 26 ..
 
koṇeṣu caivaṃ kuṇḍasya kāryaṃ śaṅkhacatuṣṭayam .
evametat samuddiṣṭaṃ bahudhā mānato bhavet .. 27 ..
 
ādbādaśāṅgulānmānādekaikāṅgulavardhanāt .
dvicaturhastaparyantamekāśītyadhikaṃ śatam .. 28 ..
 
eteṣvekataraṃ proktamanyeṣāmevameva hi .
tatsādhanaṃ vihā ya tat ahgavyūhaṃ prakalpya ca .. 29 ..
 
tato yathocitasthāne homadravyāṇi vinyaset .
saṃskṛtya vidhivat kuṇḍaṃ vahnimutpāditaṃ tathā .. 30 ..
 
saṃskṛtājyasya vipruḍbhiḥ saṃspṛśedindhanādikam .
santarpaṇaṃ tathāgneśca tasminmantrāsanādikam .. 31 ..
 
yantraviṣṭarasaṃsthānamantarāhavanaṃ tathā .
hṛdayādavatāraṃ ca mahāyantrasya viṣṭare .. 32 ..
 
samidbhiścātha nityābhiḥ kāmyaiśca havanaṃ tathā .
sviṣṭakṛddhavanaṃ cātha prāyaścittāhutiṃ tvapi .. 33 ..
 
pūrṇāhutiṃ pradhānaṃ ca yantrasthasya visarjanam .
hṛdayasthe praviśyātha maṇṭapaṃ yajanāspadam .. 34 ..
 
samarpaṇaṃ ca homasya pitṝṇāṃ tarpaṇaṃ tvapi .
balidānaṃ ca bhūtānāmiṣṭaśiṣṭodanasya ca .. 35 ..
 
pradānaṃ yajñaśīlānāṃ kāriṇāṃ bhāvitātmanām .
anuyāgaṃ ca vidhivannaivedyaprāśanādikam .. 36 ..
 
pūrvavat sakalaṃ kuryādbhogamokṣaprasiddhaye .
anena yantrarājena śāntikādiṣu karmasu .. 37 ..
 
dhyānena pūjitenaiva hutena japitena ca .
samīhitāni pūryante bhaktānāṃ bhāvitātmanām .. 38 ..
 
ekarūpamidaṃ dhyānaṃ varṇitaṃ śāntikādiṣu .
home svāhāntimo mantraḥ svabhāvādadhikaḥ sadā .. 39 ..
 
śāntike pauṣṭike vauṣaṭpūrṇāyāmapi tādṛśaḥ .
āpyāyane vaṣaṭprokto humanto vaśyakarmaṇi .. 40 ..
 
phaḍantaṃ kṣayavidveṣaprotsādanavidhau sadā .
humantaṃ cārividveṣe mohane huṃphaḍantimam .. 41 ..
 
stambhane vaṣaḍantaṃ sasyānnamonto mokṣakarmaṇi .
atho hitāya lokānāṃ rājñāmapi viśeṣataḥ .. 42 ..
 
pṛcchate nāradāyaitadahirbudhnyena vistarāt .
yathopadiṣṭaṃ vidhivattathā tatra nirīkṣya ca .. 43 ..
 
prayoktavyaṃ tu bahudhā śāntikāmī yathecchayā .
kuryādekamukhaṃ yantraṃ sthāpya saṃpūjayīta ca .. 44 ..
 
naimittikāni kāmyāni nityāni yajanāni vai .
viśeṣeṇaiva kāryāṇi vinā svāpaṃ mahotsavam .. 45 ..
 
na karmabimbāni tathā nityanaimittikādiṣu .
sthitaṃ yantraṃ samārādhyaṃ sthāpitaṃ mantravittamaiḥ .. 46 ..
 
divyādyāyatanāḍgatve sthāpite sati kutracit .
calasthiravibāgena havirantaṃ samarcayet .. 47 ..
 
dvādaśyādiṣu kāleṣu puṇyeṣu vividheṣvapi .
iti samyak samuddiṣṭaṃ mahāyantrārcanaṃ param .. 48 ..
 
adīkṣitānāṃ vidhivadaśiṣyāṇāṃ durātmanām .
gopanīyaṃ prayatnena tvabhaktānāṃ janārdane .. 49 ..
 
bhāvabhaktisametānāṃ vācyavācakayorgurau .
śāstre jñānakriyopete sātvike vedasaṃmite .. 50 ..
